<section>
<section.front>
<outline.name.block><label>&sect;</label><designator>31:22</designator><name>Application for exemption from the foundation rules</name></outline.name.block>
<research.reference.block>
<reference.entry><ref.text><cite type="topic.key" normalpub="key" sub="Internal Revenue" numref="4045 to 4079" numrange="y">West&apos;s Key Number Digest, Internal Revenue &key;4045 to 4079</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
</research.reference.block>
</section.front>
<section.body>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|22|31:22"><para.text>To be exempt from treatment as a private foundation, a charitable organization generally must notify the IRS within certain time limits that it is applying for recognition as a charitable organization.<footnote><footnote.reference>1</footnote.reference><footnote.body><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|22|31:22"><para.text><cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-code" titleref="26" secref="508" subref="(a)">26 U.S.C.A. &sect;508(a)</cite>; <cite type="lrre" normalpub="exec-us-cfr" titleref="26" secref="1.508-1" subref="(a)">26 C.F.R. &sect;1.508-1(a)</cite>.</para.text></para>
<research.reference.block>
<reference.entry><ref.text>Exempt organization status, <cite type="secondary" normalpub="ftc2" parmkref="D-4000">Federal Tax Coordinator 2d (RIA) &para;D-4000</cite>.</ref.text></reference.entry>
<reference.entry><ref.text>Application for exempt status, <cite type="secondary" normalpub="ftglf" secref="10:57">Federal Tax Guide to Legal Forms &sect;10:57</cite>.</ref.text></reference.entry>
</research.reference.block></footnote.body></footnote> Any charitable organization that does not notify the IRS that it intends to claim exemption from the foundation rules is presumed to be a private foundation.<footnote><footnote.reference>2</footnote.reference><footnote.body><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|22|31:22"><para.text><cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-code" titleref="26" secref="508" subref="(b)">26 U.S.C.A. &sect;508(b)</cite>.</para.text></para>
<research.reference.block>
<reference.entry><ref.text>Presumption that exempt organization is private foundation, <cite type="secondary" normalpub="ftc2" parmkref="D-7200">Federal Tax Coordinator 2d (RIA) &para;D-7200</cite>.</ref.text></reference.entry>
</research.reference.block></footnote.body></footnote></para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|22|31:22"><para.text>This notice is normally given by filing <cite type="lrre" normalpub="exec-us-irs-form" numref="1023">IRS Form 1023</cite> or <cite type="lrre" normalpub="exec-us-irs-form" numref="1024">1024</cite> (depending on the nature of the organization) within 15 months after the end of the month in which the organization was founded.<footnote><footnote.reference>3</footnote.reference><footnote.body><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|22|31:22"><para.text><cite type="lrre" normalpub="exec-us-cfr" titleref="26" secref="1.508-1" subref="(a)" pararef="(2)">26 C.F.R. &sect;1.508-1(a)(2)</cite>.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|22|31:22"><para.text>For a discussion of filing an application, see <cite type="secondaryxref" secref="31:11">&sect;31:11</cite>.</para.text></para></footnote.body></footnote></para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|22|31:22"><para.text>Churches and associated organizations, organizations that are not private foundations and have normal gross receipts of &dollar;5000 or less, certain subordinate organizations, and other classes of organizations that the IRS determines should be excluded from the notice requirement need not file this notice but may, nevertheless, file to obtain a favorable ruling.<footnote><footnote.reference>4</footnote.reference><footnote.body><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|22|31:22"><para.text><cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-code" titleref="26" secref="508" subref="(c)">26 U.S.C.A. &sect;508(c)</cite>; <cite type="lrre" normalpub="exec-us-cfr" titleref="26" secref="1.508-1" subref="(a)" pararef="(3)">26 C.F.R. &sect;1.508-1(a)(3)</cite>.</para.text></para></footnote.body></footnote></para.text></para>
</section.body>
</section>
<section>
<section.front>
<outline.name.block><label>&sect;</label><designator>31:23</designator><name>Exemption from income taxation; contents of foundation&apos;s governing instrument</name></outline.name.block>
<research.reference.block>
<reference.entry><ref.text><cite type="topic.key" normalpub="key" sub="Internal Revenue" numref="4045 to 4079" numrange="y">West&apos;s Key Number Digest, Internal Revenue &key;4045 to 4079</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
</research.reference.block>
</section.front>
<section.body>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|23|31:23"><para.text>To qualify for exemption from income taxation, private foundations must include limiting provisions in their governing instruments that the organization must distribute its income in each taxable year so as to avoid any tax under <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-irc" titleref="26" secref="4942">Internal Revenue Code Section 4942</cite> and that the foundation is prohibited from operating in such manner as to incur tax liability under <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-irc" titleref="26" secref="4941" subref="(d)">Internal Revenue Code Section 4941(d)</cite> (relating to self-dealing), <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-irc" titleref="26" secref="4943" subref="(c)">Internal Revenue Code Section 4943(c)</cite> (relating to excess business holdings), <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-irc" titleref="26" secref="4944">Internal Revenue Code Section 4944</cite> (relating to investments which jeopardize charitable purpose), or <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-irc" titleref="26" secref="4945">Internal Revenue Code Section 4945</cite> (relating to political expenditures).<footnote><footnote.reference>1</footnote.reference><footnote.body><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|23|31:23"><para.text><cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-code" titleref="26" secref="508" subref="(e)">26 U.S.C.A. &sect;508(e)</cite>.</para.text></para>
<research.reference.block>
<reference.entry><ref.text>Provisions required in governing instruments of private foundations, <cite type="secondary" normalpub="ftc2" parmkref="D-7219">Federal Tax Coordinator 2d (RIA) &para;D-7219</cite>.</ref.text></reference.entry>
<reference.entry><ref.text>Mandatory governing provisions for private foundations, <cite type="secondary" normalpub="ftglf" secref="10:103">Federal Tax Guide to Legal Forms &sect;10:103</cite>.</ref.text></reference.entry>
</research.reference.block></footnote.body></footnote></para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|23|31:23"><para.text>The regulations provide that a foundation&apos;s governing instrument will be deemed to contain these limitations if a valid state law requires the foundation to operate within these limitations.<footnote><footnote.reference>2</footnote.reference><footnote.body><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|23|31:23"><para.text><cite type="lrre" normalpub="exec-us-cfr" titleref="26" secref="1.508-3" subref="(d)" pararef="(1)">26 C.F.R. &sect;1.508-3(d)(1)</cite>.</para.text></para></footnote.body></footnote> Such a law has been passed in New York.<footnote><footnote.reference>3</footnote.reference><footnote.body><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|23|31:23"><para.text><cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="406">N-PCL &sect;406</cite>.</para.text></para>
<research.reference.block>
<reference.entry><ref.text>Specific requirements of the Not-for-Profit Corporation Law, see <cite type="secondary" normalpub="nyj2" topicname="Business Relationships" secref="71">N.Y. Jur. 2d, Business Relationships &sect;71</cite>.</ref.text></reference.entry>
</research.reference.block></footnote.body></footnote> To avoid any difficulties that might arise in the event of the repeal or invalidation of the statute, it is recommended that the governing instruments of all private foundations contain provisions conforming to Internal Revenue Code requirements, thus insuring the exempt status of the organization. However, any private foundation taking advantage of such a state statute must include in its annual return<footnote><footnote.reference>4</footnote.reference><footnote.body><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|23|31:23"><para.text><cite type="lrre" normalpub="exec-us-irs-form" numref="990-PF">IRS Form 990-PF</cite> or <cite type="lrre" normalpub="exec-us-irs-form" numref="4720">IRS Form 4720</cite>, filed pursuant to <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-code" titleref="26" secref="6033" subref="(a)">26 U.S.C.A. &sect;6033(a)</cite>, see <cite type="lrre" normalpub="exec-us-cfr" titleref="26" secref="1.6033-2">26 C.F.R. &sect;1.6033-2</cite>.</para.text></para></footnote.body></footnote> a statement that it has not taken any action that would exclude it from the coverage of the statute.<footnote><footnote.reference>5</footnote.reference><footnote.body><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|23|31:23"><para.text><cite type="lrre" normalpub="exec-us-cfr" titleref="26" secref="1.508-3" subref="(d)" pararef="(4)" spararef="(i)">26 C.F.R. &sect;1.508-3(d)(4)(i)</cite>.</para.text></para></footnote.body></footnote></para.text></para>
</section.body>
</section>
<section>
<section.front>
<outline.name.block><label>&sect;</label><designator>31:24</designator><name>Termination of private foundation status</name></outline.name.block>
<research.reference.block>
<reference.entry><ref.text><cite type="topic.key" normalpub="key" sub="Internal Revenue" numref="4063">West&apos;s Key Number Digest, Internal Revenue &key;4063</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
</research.reference.block>
</section.front>
<section.body>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|24|31:24"><para.text>The Internal Revenue Service may terminate an organization&apos;s status as a private foundation only if the organization has willfully and flagrantly committed or willfully repeated actions giving rise to penalty excise taxes.<footnote><footnote.reference>1</footnote.reference><footnote.body><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|24|31:24"><para.text><cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-code" titleref="26" secref="507" subref="(a)" pararef="(2)">26 U.S.C.A. &sect;507(a)(2)</cite>.</para.text></para>
<research.reference.block>
<reference.entry><ref.text>Involuntary termination of private foundation status, <cite type="secondary" normalpub="ftc2" parmkref="D-7222">Federal Tax Coordinator 2d (RIA) &para;D-7222</cite>.</ref.text></reference.entry>
<reference.entry><ref.text>Termination of foundation, <cite type="secondary" normalpub="ftglf" secref="10:118">Federal Tax Guide to Legal Forms &sect;10:118</cite>.</ref.text></reference.entry>
</research.reference.block></footnote.body></footnote> An organization may elect to terminate the private foundation status by giving notice to the Internal Revenue Service<footnote><footnote.reference>2</footnote.reference><footnote.body><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|24|31:24"><para.text><cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-code" titleref="26" secref="507" subref="(a)" pararef="(1)">26 U.S.C.A. &sect;507(a)(1)</cite>, <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-code" titleref="26" secref="507" subref="(b)" pararef="(1)" spararef="(B)" clref="(ii)">(b)(1)(B)(ii)</cite>.</para.text></para>
<research.reference.block>
<reference.entry><ref.text>Voluntary termination of private foundation status, <cite type="secondary" normalpub="ftc2" parmkref="D-7220, D-7221" parmkrange="y">Federal Tax Coordinator 2d (RIA) &dblpara;D-7220, D-7221</cite>.</ref.text></reference.entry>
<reference.entry><ref.text>Termination of foundation, <cite type="secondary" normalpub="ftglf" secref="10:118">Federal Tax Guide to Legal Forms &sect;10:118</cite>.</ref.text></reference.entry>
</research.reference.block></footnote.body></footnote> of its intent to do so.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|24|31:24"><para.text>On voluntary termination, the private foundation must file with the Internal Revenue Service a final return consisting of <cite type="lrre" normalpub="exec-us-irs-form" numref="990-PF">IRS Form 990-PF</cite>, if incorporated, a conformed copy of the resolution to dissolve and a certificate of dissolution issued by a court, and a list of organizations to which assets were distributed. All of the above must be signed by an officer of the foundation. In any event, the organization will be subject to a termination tax, unless the tax is abated.<footnote><footnote.reference>3</footnote.reference><footnote.body><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|24|31:24"><para.text><cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-code" titleref="26" secref="507" subref="(a), (g)">26 U.S.C.A. &sect;507(a), (g)</cite>.</para.text></para>
<research.reference.block>
<reference.entry><ref.text>Notification of voluntary termination of private foundation status, <cite type="secondary" normalpub="ftc2" parmkref="D-7221">Federal Tax Coordinator 2d (RIA) &para;D-7221</cite>.</ref.text></reference.entry>
<reference.entry><ref.text>Tax on termination of private foundation status, <cite type="secondary" normalpub="ftc2" parmkref="D-7228 to D-7234" parmkrange="y">Federal Tax Coordinator 2d (RIA) &dblpara;D-7228 to D-7234</cite>.</ref.text></reference.entry>
<reference.entry><ref.text>Termination of foundation, <cite type="secondary" normalpub="ftglf" secref="10:118">Federal Tax Guide to Legal Forms &sect;10:118</cite>.</ref.text></reference.entry>
</research.reference.block></footnote.body></footnote></para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|24|31:24"><para.text>The termination tax is equal to the lesser of the aggregate tax benefit, realized by the organization over the period during which it held exempt status, or the value of the foundation&apos;s net assets.<footnote><footnote.reference>4</footnote.reference><footnote.body><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|24|31:24"><para.text><cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-code" titleref="26" secref="507" subref="(c)">26 U.S.C.A. &sect;507(c)</cite>.</para.text></para>
<research.reference.block>
<reference.entry><ref.text>Tax on termination of private foundation status, <cite type="secondary" normalpub="ftc2" parmkref="D-7228 to D-7234" parmkrange="y">Federal Tax Coordinator 2d (RIA) &dblpara;D-7228 to D-7234</cite>.</ref.text></reference.entry>
<reference.entry><ref.text>Termination of foundation, <cite type="secondary" normalpub="ftglf" secref="10:118">Federal Tax Guide to Legal Forms &sect;10:118</cite>.</ref.text></reference.entry>
</research.reference.block></footnote.body></footnote></para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|24|31:24"><para.text>With respect to involuntary termination, the tax may be abated under certain circumstances.<footnote><footnote.reference>5</footnote.reference><footnote.body><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|24|31:24"><para.text>See <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-code" titleref="26" secref="507" subref="(a)" pararef="(2)">26 U.S.C.A. &sect;507(a)(2)</cite>, <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-code" titleref="26" secref="507" subref="(g)">(g)</cite>.</para.text></para>
<research.reference.block>
<reference.entry><ref.text>Abatement of tax on termination of private foundation status, <cite type="secondary" normalpub="ftc2" parmkref="D-7234">Federal Tax Coordinator 2d (RIA) &para;D-7234</cite>.</ref.text></reference.entry>
<reference.entry><ref.text>Termination of foundation, <cite type="secondary" normalpub="ftglf" secref="10:118">Federal Tax Guide to Legal Forms &sect;10:118</cite>.</ref.text></reference.entry>
</research.reference.block></footnote.body></footnote> With respect to voluntary termination, the tax will be abated if the organization either distributes all of its net assets to one or more publicly supported charitable organizations, which are not private foundations and which have been in continued existence for at least five years, or notifies the Internal Revenue Service that it intends to terminate its private foundation status by altering its organizational and operational structure so as to conform to the requirements for exemption for that status over a continuous five-year period.<footnote><footnote.reference>6</footnote.reference><footnote.body><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|24|31:24"><para.text><cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-code" titleref="26" secref="507" subref="(b)" pararef="(1)" spararef="(B)" clref="(i), (ii)">26 U.S.C.A. &sect;507(b)(1)(B)(i), (ii)</cite>.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|24|31:24"><para.text>For discussion of the organizational and operational requirements for exemption from private foundation status, see <cite type="secondaryxref" secref="31:9">&sect;31:9</cite>.</para.text></para>
<research.reference.block>
<reference.entry><ref.text>Abatement of tax on termination of private foundation status, <cite type="secondary" normalpub="ftc2" parmkref="D-7234">Federal Tax Coordinator 2d (RIA) &para;D-7234</cite>.</ref.text></reference.entry>
<reference.entry><ref.text>Termination of foundation, <cite type="secondary" normalpub="ftglf" secref="10:118">Federal Tax Guide to Legal Forms &sect;10:118</cite>.</ref.text></reference.entry>
</research.reference.block></footnote.body></footnote> This notice must include:<footnote><footnote.reference>7</footnote.reference><footnote.body><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|24|31:24"><para.text><cite type="lrre" normalpub="exec-us-cfr" titleref="26" secref="1.507-2" subref="(b)" pararef="(3)">26 C.F.R. &sect;1.507-2(b)(3)</cite>.</para.text></para>
<research.reference.block>
<reference.entry><ref.text>Abatement of tax on termination of private foundation status, <cite type="secondary" normalpub="ftc2" parmkref="D-7234">Federal Tax Coordinator 2d (RIA) &para;D-7234</cite>.</ref.text></reference.entry>
<reference.entry><ref.text>Termination of foundation, <cite type="secondary" normalpub="ftglf" secref="10:118">Federal Tax Guide to Legal Forms &sect;10:118</cite>.</ref.text></reference.entry>
</research.reference.block></footnote.body></footnote></para.text>

<list.item><name.block><designator>1</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|25|31:25"><para.text>Name of the corporation.</para.text></para></list.item>
<list.item><name.block><designator>2</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|25|31:25"><para.text>That the corporation is a corporation as defined in Section 102(a)(5) of the Law.</para.text></para></list.item>
<list.item><name.block><designator>3</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|25|31:25"><para.text>The specific purpose or purposes for which the corporation is organized, it being sufficient to state that the purpose of the corporation is any purpose for which corporations may be organized under the Law as a charitable or noncharitable corporation.</para.text></para></list.item>
<list.item><name.block><designator>4</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|25|31:25"><para.text>That it is a charitable corporation under section 201 of the Law.</para.text></para></list.item>
<list.item><name.block><designator>5</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|25|31:25"><para.text>If it is not formed to engage in any activity or for any purpose requiring consent or approval of any state official, department, board, agency or other body, a statement that no such consent or approval is required.</para.text></para></list.item>
<list.item><name.block><designator>6</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|25|31:25"><para.text>The county within New York State in which the office of the corporation is to be located. The certificate may also identify the post office address outside the state at which the books and records of the corporation will be kept pursuant to Section 621 of the Law.</para.text></para></list.item>
<list.item><name.block><designator>7</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|25|31:25"><para.text>The names and addresses of the initial directors.</para.text></para></list.item>
<list.item><name.block><designator>8</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|25|31:25"><para.text>The duration of the corporation if it is not to be perpetual.</para.text></para></list.item>
<list.item><name.block><designator>9</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|25|31:25"><para.text>A designation of the Secretary of State as agent of the corporation upon whom process against it may be served and the post office address to which the Secretary of State is to mail a copy of any process against the corporation served on him or her. The corporation may include an email address to which the secretary of state shall email a notice of the fact that process against it has been electronically served upon him or her.</para.text></para></list.item>
<list.item><name.block><designator>10</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|25|31:25"><para.text>If the corporation is to have a registered agent, his or her name and address within New York and a statement that the registered agent is to be the agent of the corporation upon whom process against it may be served.</para.text></para></list.item>
<list.item><name.block><designator>11</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|25|31:25"><para.text>The statements required of special not-for-profit corporations (corporations organized for certain statutory purposes under <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" artref="14">Article 14 of the Not-for-Profit Corporation Law</cite>).</para.text></para></list.item>
<list.item><name.block><designator>12</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|25|31:25"><para.text>In order to attain federal tax-exempt status and qualify as a charity for which contributions are deductible for federal income tax purposes, add:</para.text></para>
<list list.style="para">
<list.item><name.block><designator>(a)</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|25|31:25"><para.text>Charitable purposes, limitations, and powers in compliance with <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-irc" titleref="26" secref="501" subref="(c)" pararef="(3)">Internal Revenue Code Section 501(c)(3)</cite>.</para.text></para></list.item>
<list.item><name.block><designator>(b)</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|25|31:25"><para.text>Statement of manner of disposition of assets on dissolution complying with <cite type="lrre" normalpub="exec-us-cfr" titleref="26" secref="1.501(c)(3)-1" subref="(b)">26 C.F.R. &sect;1.501(c)(3)-1(b)</cite>.</para.text></para></list.item>
</list></list.item>
<list.item><name.block><designator>13</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|25|31:25"><para.text>The certificate may contain provisions not inconsistent with law:</para.text></para>
<list list.style="para">
<list.item><name.block><designator>(a)</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|25|31:25"><para.text>For the regulation of the internal affairs of the corporation, including types or classes of membership and distribution of its assets on dissolution.</para.text></para></list.item>
<list.item><name.block><designator>(b)</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|25|31:25"><para.text>Required by any governmental body or officer or other person or body as a condition for giving the consent or approval required for filing the certificate of incorporation.</para.text></para></list.item>
</list></list.item></list>
<note.block>
<note.group note.head="none">
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|25|31:25"><para.text>The certificate of incorporation must be entitled &ldquo;Certificate of Incorporation of (Name of Corporation), Under <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="402">Section 402 of the Not-for-Profit Corporation Law</cite>&rdquo; and must state the above matters.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|25|31:25"><para.text>The matters that must and may be included in the certificate of incorporation for state purposes are specified by statute. See <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="402">N-PCL &sect;402</cite>. Additional matters must be added to qualify the corporation for exemption from income taxes. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-code" titleref="26" secref="501" subref="(c)" pararef="(3)">26 U.S.C.A. &sect;501(c)(3)</cite>.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|25|31:25"><para.text>For additional matters that may be contained in the certificate, see <cite type="secondaryxref" secref="31:26">&sect;31:26</cite>.</para.text></para>
</note.group>
<research.reference.block>
<reference.entry><ref.text><cite type="topic.key" normalpub="key" sub="Corporations and Business Organizations" numref="3370 to 3375" numrange="y">West&apos;s Key Number Digest, Corporations and Business Organizations &key;3370 to 3375</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
</research.reference.block>
<item.reference.block>
<item.reference><name.block><label>Item</label><designator>1.</designator></name.block>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|25|31:25"><para.text><cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="301">N-PCL &sect;301</cite> sets out the general rules governing the requirements for corporate names for nonprofit corporations.</para.text></para>
<research.reference.block>
<reference.entry><ref.text><cite type="secondary" normalpub="nyj2" topicname="Business Relationships" secref="164 to 176" secrange="y">N.Y. Jur. 2d, Business Relationships &dblsect;164 to 176</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
</research.reference.block>
</item.reference>
<item.reference><name.block><label>Item</label><designator>3.</designator></name.block>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|25|31:25"><para.text>A corporation may be formed under the Not-for-Profit Corporation Law for any one or more of the purposes specified in the Law. See <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="201">N-PCL &sect;201</cite>.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|25|31:25"><para.text>It is not necessary to set forth in the certificate of incorporation any of the corporate powers enumerated in the Not-for-Profit Corporation Law. See <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="202">N-PCL &sect;202</cite>.</para.text></para>
<research.reference.block>
<reference.entry><ref.text><cite type="secondary" normalpub="nyj2" topicname="Business Relationships" secref="57, 58, 421" secrange="y">N.Y. Jur. 2d, Business Relationships &dblsect;57, 58, 421</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
</research.reference.block>
</item.reference>
<item.reference><name.block><label>Item</label><designator>4.</designator></name.block>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|25|31:25"><para.text>Prior to its amendment, four types of not-for-profit corporations, Types A, B, C and D, were provided for under the Not-for-Profit Corporation Law. These four types have been replaced with two types, charitable and noncharitable. A corporation formed under the Law on or after July 1, 2014 will either be a charitable corporation or a noncharitable corporation. Any corporation formed for both charitable purposes and noncharitable purposes will be deemed a charitable corporation for purposes of the Not-for-Profit Corporation Law. A type A not-for-profit corporation formed prior to July 1, 2014 will be deemed a noncharitable corporation. A type B or C not-for-profit corporation formed prior to July 1, 2014 will be deemed a charitable corporation. A type D not-for-profit corporation formed prior to July 1, 2014 for charitable purposes will be deemed a charitable corporation. Any other type D not-for-profit corporations formed prior to July 1, 2014 will be deemed a noncharitable corporation. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="201">N-PCL &sect;201</cite>. See <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="201" subref="(b)">N-PCL &sect;201(b)</cite>.</para.text></para>
</item.reference>
<item.reference><name.block><label>Item</label><designator>7.</designator></name.block>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|25|31:25"><para.text>The board of directors of a not-for-profit corporation must consist of three or more directors; the initial number of directors is implied by the listing of names and addresses of the initial directors in the certificate of incorporation. Thereafter, the number (never less than three) may be fixed by the bylaws or, in the case of a corporation having members, by action of the members or of the board under the specific provisions of a bylaw allowing such action. If not otherwise fixed, the number of directors will be three. See <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="702" subref="(a)">N-PCL &sect;702(a)</cite>.</para.text></para>
<research.reference.block>
<reference.entry><ref.text><cite type="secondary" normalpub="nyj2" topicname="Business Relationships" secref="71">N.Y. Jur. 2d, Business Relationships &sect;71</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
</research.reference.block>
</item.reference>
<item.reference><name.block><label>Item</label><designator>9.</designator></name.block>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|25|31:25"><para.text>The Secretary of State is the agent of every domestic corporation formed under the Not-for-Profit Corporation Law (see <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="304" subref="(a)">N-PCL &sect;304(a)</cite>). Additionally, the certificate of incorporation must contain a designation of the Secretary of State as agent of the corporation for service of process and provide therein a post office address to which the Secretary of State can mail a copy of any process against the corporation served on the Secretary of State. The corporation may include an email address to which the secretary of state shall email a notice of the fact that process against it has been electronically served upon him or her. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="402" subref="(a)" pararef="(6)">N-PCL &sect;402(a)(6)</cite>.</para.text></para>
<research.reference.block>
<reference.entry><ref.text><cite type="secondary" normalpub="nyj2" topicname="Business Relationships" secref="71">N.Y. Jur. 2d, Business Relationships &sect;71</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
<reference.entry><ref.text><cite type="secondary" normalpub="nyj2" topicname="Business Relationships" secref="1062, 1063" secrange="y">N.Y. Jur. 2d, Business Relationships &dblsect;1062, 1063</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
</research.reference.block>
</item.reference>
<item.reference><name.block><label>Item</label><designator>10.</designator></name.block>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|25|31:25"><para.text>A not-for-profit corporation is not required to have a registered agent, inasmuch as the statute is couched in permissive language (see <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="305" subref="(a)">N-PCL &sect;305(a)</cite>). In any event, however, the Secretary of State will be the agent for service of process against the corporation (see <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="304" subref="(a)">N-PCL &sect;304(a)</cite>) and must be designated as such in the certificate of incorporation. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="402" subref="(a)" pararef="(7)">N-PCL &sect;402(a)(7)</cite>.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|25|31:25"><para.text>The corporation&apos;s registered agent is the person upon whom process against the corporation may be served and who shall deliver to the corporation all process, notices, or demands received by the agent as agent for the corporation. The registered agent must be: (1) a natural person who is a resident of or has a business address in the State of New York; or (2) a domestic corporation or a foreign corporation of any type or kind formed or authorized to conduct business in the State of New York under the Not-for-Profit Corporation Law or other state statute. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="305" subref="(a)">N-PCL &sect;305(a)</cite>.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|25|31:25"><para.text>For the procedure for serving process on a registered agent, see <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="306">N.Y. Not-for-Profit Corp. Law &sect;306</cite>.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|25|31:25"><para.text>The designation of a registered agent may be made, revoked, or changed as provided in the Not-for-Profit Corporation Law. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="305" subref="(b)">N-PCL &sect;305(b)</cite>. This means that the designation may only be made in the certificate of incorporation and that any designation (if the corporation made no designation in its original certificate of incorporation), change, or revocation must be made by amending the certificate. See <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="801" subref="(b)" pararef="(8)">N-PCL &dblsect;801(b)(8)</cite>, <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="802" subref="(c)" pararef="(3)">802(c)(3)</cite>.</para.text></para>
<research.reference.block>
<reference.entry><ref.text><cite type="secondary" normalpub="nyj2" topicname="Business Relationships" secref="1062, 1063" secrange="y">N.Y. Jur. 2d, Business Relationships &dblsect;1062, 1063</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
</research.reference.block>
</item.reference>
<item.reference><name.block><label>Item</label><designator>11.</designator></name.block>
<research.reference.block>
<reference.entry><ref.text><cite type="secondary" normalpub="nyj2" topicname="Business Relationships" secref="58">N.Y. Jur. 2d, Business Relationships &sect;58</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
</research.reference.block>
</item.reference>
<item.reference><name.block><label>Item</label><designator>12.</designator></name.block>
<note.group note.head="taxnotes">
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|25|31:25"><para.text>A private foundation&apos;s governing instruments must: (1) contain or be reformed so that they will contain provisions limiting the organization&apos;s exempt purposes, prohibiting nonexempt activities, and dedicating its assets to exempt purposes; (2) require disposition of assets on dissolution complying with <cite type="lrre" normalpub="exec-us-cfr" titleref="26" secref="1.501(c)(3)-1" subref="(b)">26 C.F.R. &sect;1.501(c)(3)-1(b)</cite>; (3) require taxable income to be distributed; and (4) prohibit the foundation from engaging in acts which render it liable for any of the excise taxes on private foundations. See <cite type="lrre" normalpub="exec-us-cfr" titleref="26" secref="1.501(c)(3)-1" subref="(b)">26 C.F.R. &sect;1.501(c)(3)-1(b)</cite>; <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-irc" titleref="26" secref="508" subref="(e)" pararef="(1)">I.R.C. &sect;508(e)(1)</cite>.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|25|31:25"><para.text>The IRS has issued sample provisions that may be inserted in governing instruments. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="exec-us-irs-ruling" numref="70-270" volref="1970-1" reporter="C.B." volpg="135">Rev. Rul. 70-270, 1970-1 C.B. 135</cite>; <cite type="lrre" normalpub="exec-us-irs-ruling" numref="74-368" volref="1974-2" reporter="C.B." volpg="390">Rev. Rul. 74-368, 1974-2 C.B. 390</cite>.</para.text></para>
</note.group>
<research.reference.block>
<reference.entry><ref.text>Provisions required in governing instruments of private foundations, <cite type="secondary" normalpub="ftc2" parmkref="D-7219">RIA Federal Tax Coordinator 2d &para;D-7219</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
<reference.entry><ref.text>Mandatory governing provisions, <cite type="secondary" normalpub="ftglf" secref="10:103">Federal Tax Guide to Legal Forms &sect;10:103</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
</research.reference.block>
</item.reference>
<item.reference><name.block><label>Item</label><designator>13.</designator></name.block>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|25|31:25"><para.text>The certificate of incorporation may include any provision, not inconsistent with law, that the incorporator(s) may choose to insert: (1) for the regulation of the internal affairs of the corporation, including types or classes of membership and the distribution of assets on dissolution or final liquidation; or (2) as required by any governmental body or officer or other person or body as a condition for giving the consent or approval required for the filing of the certificate of incorporation. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="402" subref="(c)">N-PCL &sect;402(c)</cite>.</para.text></para>

<note.block>
<note.group note.head="none">
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|28|31:28"><para.text>See <cite type="lrre" normalpub="exec-us-irs-pub" numref="557">I.R.S. Pub. 557</cite>. The application must be on <cite type="lrre" normalpub="exec-us-irs-form" numref="1023">IRS Form 1023</cite> for applicants claiming to be exempt under <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-code" titleref="26" secref="501" subref="(c)" pararef="(3)">26 U.S.C.A. &sect;501(c)(3)</cite>. Additional information may be required depending on the applicant&apos;s proposed activities. Where the application requires a conformed copy, it must agree with the original document and all amendments thereto. If the copies are not signed, they must be accompanied by a written declaration signed by an officer authorized to sign for the organization, certifying that they are complete and accurate copies of the original documents. See <cite type="lrre" normalpub="exec-us-irs-proc" numref="68-14" volref="1968-1" reporter="C.B." volpg="768">Rev. Proc. 68-14, 1968-1 C.B. 768</cite> and the Instructions for <cite type="lrre" normalpub="exec-us-irs-form" numref="1023">IRS Form 1023</cite>.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|28|31:28"><para.text>If the application does not contain the required information, it may be returned with a letter of explanation without being considered on its merits. If the completed application is resubmitted within the time period indicated in the letter from the IRS, it will be considered received on the original submission date. In that case, if the original submission was timely, the application will be considered timely filed.</para.text></para>
</note.group>

</item.reference>

<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|28|31:28"><para.text>Any information submitted in the application or in support of it that relates to any trade secret, patent, process, style of work, or apparatus, upon request, may be withheld from public inspection if the Commissioner determines that the disclosure of such information would adversely affect the organization. The request must:</para.text>
<list list.style="para">
<list.item><name.block><designator>1</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|28|31:28"><para.text>Identify the material to be withheld (the document, page, paragraph, and line) by clearly marking it, &ldquo;NOT SUBJECT TO PUBLIC INSPECTION.&rdquo;</para.text></para></list.item>
<list.item><name.block><designator>2</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|28|31:28"><para.text>Include the reasons for your organization&apos;s position that the information is of the type that may be withheld from public inspection.</para.text></para></list.item>

<section.front>
<outline.name.block><label>&sect;</label><designator>31:29</designator><name>Checklist<sep/>Procedure to apply for determination letter of exempt status</name></outline.name.block>
<online.view>
<online.view.item>COL</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>NFP</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>CHK</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>FTR</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>FCV</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>EBL</online.view.item>
</online.view>
</section.front>
<section.body>
<check.list>
<list list.style="para">
<list.item><name.block><designator>1</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|29|31:29"><para.text>Obtain employer identification number (EIN).</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|29|31:29"><para.text>If not previously applied for, prepare Form SS-4.</para.text></para></list.item>
<list.item><name.block><designator>2</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|29|31:29"><para.text>Obtain and study <cite type="lrre" normalpub="exec-us-irs-pub" numref="557">I.R.S. Pub. 557</cite>, Tax Exempt Status for Your Organization.</para.text></para></list.item>
<list.item><name.block><designator>3</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|29|31:29"><para.text>Determine appropriate exemption classification for organization being formed.</para.text></para>
<list list.style="para">
<list.item><name.block><designator>(a)</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|29|31:29"><para.text>Includes determination whether submission is required and, if not, whether it should nevertheless be made.</para.text></para>
<list list.style="para">
<list.item><name.block><designator>(1)</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|29|31:29"><para.text>Usual advice as to obtaining determination letter.</para.text></para></list.item>
<list.item><name.block><designator>(2)</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|29|31:29"><para.text>Submission not required for churches, publicly supported organizations with revenues of less than &dollar;5000, and subordinate organizations covered by a parent&apos;s exemption.</para.text></para></list.item>
</list></list.item></list></list.item>
<list.item><name.block><designator>4</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|29|31:29"><para.text>Obtain appropriate form for application.</para.text></para>
<list list.style="para">
<list.item><name.block><designator>(a)</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|29|31:29"><para.text>Form 1023 is for most Section 501(c)(3) organizations.</para.text></para></list.item>
<list.item><name.block><designator>(b)</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|29|31:29"><para.text>Form 1024 is for Section 501(a) organizations.</para.text></para></list.item>
<list.item><name.block><designator>(c)</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|29|31:29"><para.text>Most, but not all, organizations come under the above forms. If not covered by one of these, application is by letter.</para.text></para>
<list list.style="para">
<list.item><name.block><designator>(1)</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|29|31:29"><para.text>Letter should follow general format of Forms 1023 and 1024 and include the same enclosures.</para.text></para></list.item>
</list></list.item>
<list.item><name.block><designator>(d)</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|29|31:29"><para.text>Study questions on application, including schedule applying to organization.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|29|31:29"><para.text>Determine what information is not currently available and means of obtaining it.</para.text></para></list.item>
<list.item><name.block><designator>(e)</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|29|31:29"><para.text>Gather all tax returns previously filed by organization, including information returns.</para.text></para></list.item>
</list></list.item>
<list.item><name.block><designator>5</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|29|31:29"><para.text>Prepare financial material.</para.text></para>
<list list.style="para">
<list.item><name.block><designator>(a)</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|29|31:29"><para.text>Gather financial statements for last three full years of organization&apos;s existence.</para.text></para></list.item>
<list.item><name.block><designator>(b)</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|29|31:29"><para.text>Prepare financial statement for current year to within 60 days of application filing date.</para.text></para></list.item>
<list.item><name.block><designator>(c)</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|29|31:29"><para.text>Determine whether financial information is sufficient to complete financial data section of form for last three years and current year.</para.text></para>
<list list.style="para">
<list.item><name.block><designator>(1)</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|29|31:29"><para.text>If not, determine how the information may be obtained.</para.text></para></list.item>
<list.item><name.block><designator>(2)</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|29|31:29"><para.text>In general, receipts and expenditures must be shown, including the sources of receipts and the nature of expenditures. A distinction must be drawn between expenditures for exempt purposes and expenditures for administration.</para.text></para></list.item>
<list.item><name.block><designator>(3)</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|29|31:29"><para.text>Break-down of revenue sources is required.</para.text></para>
<list list.style="para">
<list.item><name.block><designator>(A)</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|29|31:29"><para.text>Public or private sources.</para.text></para></list.item>
<list.item><name.block><designator>(B)</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|29|31:29"><para.text>Contributions, grants, or other sources.</para.text></para></list.item>
<list.item><name.block><designator>(C)</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|29|31:29"><para.text>Fundraising events, ticket sales, rentals, other business or investment sources.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|29|31:29"><para.text>Full explanation of the activities must be given.</para.text></para>
<list list.style="para">
<list.item><name.block><designator>(I)</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|29|31:29"><para.text>Need for this depends on individual forms.</para.text></para></list.item>
</list></list.item></list></list.item></list></list.item>
<list.item><name.block><designator>(d)</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|29|31:29"><para.text>If operations have not begun or have been conducted for less than a year prepare proposed budget for two full accounting periods and a current statement of assets and liabilities.</para.text></para></list.item>
</list></list.item>
<list.item><name.block><designator>6</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|29|31:29"><para.text>Prepare a description of the activities of the organization, past, present and planned.</para.text></para></list.item>
<list.item><name.block><designator>7</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|29|31:29"><para.text>Prepare a description of the fundraising program, actual and planned, and the method for effectuating it.</para.text></para></list.item>
<list.item><name.block><designator>8</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|29|31:29"><para.text>Prepare a description of the criteria used for selecting recipients of funds or benefits.</para.text></para></list.item>
<list.item><name.block><designator>9</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|29|31:29"><para.text>Obtain conformed copy of articles of incorporation, articles of association, or other foundation document for the organization.</para.text></para>
<list list.style="para">
<list.item><name.block><designator>(a)</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|29|31:29"><para.text>An enabling document is a requisite for determination of exemption.</para.text></para></list.item>
<list.item><name.block><designator>(b)</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|29|31:29"><para.text>If organization is incorporated, approval by the appropriate state official must be included.</para.text></para></list.item>
</list></list.item>
<list.item><name.block><designator>10</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|29|31:29"><para.text>Obtain conformed copy of bylaws.</para.text></para></list.item>
<list.item><name.block><designator>11</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|29|31:29"><para.text>Obtain <cite type="lrre" normalpub="exec-us-irs-form" numref="8718">IRS Form 8718</cite> (User Fee for Exempt Organization Determination Letter Request) and <cite type="lrre" normalpub="exec-us-irs-form" numref="2848">Form 2848</cite> (Power of Attorney and Declaration of Representative).</para.text></para>
<list list.style="para">
<list.item><name.block><designator>(a)</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|29|31:29"><para.text>Study instructions and complete forms.</para.text></para></list.item>
<list.item><name.block><designator>(b)</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|29|31:29"><para.text>Obtain check or money order for payment of fee.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|29|31:29"><para.text>Money order is recommended as action is delayed until a check clears.</para.text></para></list.item>
</list></list.item>
<list.item><name.block><designator>12</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|29|31:29"><para.text>Complete all forms and prepare package of material for submission. Include:</para.text></para>
<list list.style="para">
<list.item><name.block><designator>(a)</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|29|31:29"><para.text>Application form (usually Form 1023 or 1024).</para.text></para></list.item>
<list.item><name.block><designator>(b)</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|29|31:29"><para.text>Form 8718.</para.text></para></list.item>
<list.item><name.block><designator>(c)</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|29|31:29"><para.text>Form 2848, if applicable.</para.text></para></list.item>
<list.item><name.block><designator>(d)</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|29|31:29"><para.text>Fee.</para.text></para></list.item>
<list.item><name.block><designator>(e)</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|29|31:29"><para.text>Organizing documents, such as articles of incorporation.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|29|31:29"><para.text>Include approval by state official if incorporated.</para.text></para></list.item>
<list.item><name.block><designator>(f)</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|29|31:29"><para.text>Bylaws.</para.text></para></list.item>
<list.item><name.block><designator>(g)</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|29|31:29"><para.text>Every attachment must show name and EIN of organization, identification as an attachment to the application form and identification of the part and line item number to which it applies.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|29|31:29"><para.text>Organizing documents and bylaws must also be conformed with sworn statement of an officer or director as to the truth and correctness of documents.</para.text></para></list.item>
</list></list.item>
<list.item><name.block><designator>13</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|29|31:29"><para.text>Submit application to IRS office designated in Form 8718.</para.text></para></list.item>
</list>

<form uuid="Ic7036190181b11e68c12afa7f3a24041">
<form.name.block><name>MINUTES OF THE FIRST MEETING OF INCORPORATORS OF <inline.instr>&lsqb;NAME OF CORPORATION&rsqb;</inline.instr></name></form.name.block>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|31|31:30"><form.text>On <inline.instr>&lsqb;date of meeting&rsqb;</inline.instr>, at <inline.instr>&lsqb;time of meeting&rsqb;</inline.instr>, at <inline.instr>&lsqb;place of meeting&rsqb;</inline.instr>, <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of city&rsqb;</inline.instr>, <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of county&rsqb;</inline.instr>, <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of state&rsqb;</inline.instr>, a meeting of the following-named persons was held: <inline.instr>&lsqb;names of incorporators&rsqb;</inline.instr>.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|31|31:30"><form.text>The meeting was called to order by <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of presiding officer&rsqb;</inline.instr>, who presided over the elections of officers of the meeting. By motion duly made, seconded, and carried, <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of chairperson&rsqb;</inline.instr> was elected chair of the meeting and <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of secretary&rsqb;</inline.instr> was elected Secretary.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|31|31:30"><form.text><inline.instr>&lsqb;Name of chairperson&rsqb;</inline.instr> then announced that the object of the meeting was to take such steps as might be necessary to organize a not-for-profit charitable corporation under the Not-for-Profit Corporation Law of the State of New York, to be known as <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of corporation&rsqb;</inline.instr>, which would qualify for income tax exemption under <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-irc" titleref="26" secref="501" subref="(c)" pararef="(3)">Section 501(c)(3) of the Federal Internal Revenue Code</cite>.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|31|31:30"><form.text><inline.instr>&lsqb;Name of chairperson&rsqb;</inline.instr> presented a draft of the certificate of incorporation of <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of corporation&rsqb;</inline.instr>. The draft was then unanimously approved by the proposed incorporators, <inline.instr>&lsqb;names of incorporators&rsqb;</inline.instr>, all of whom signed the same in the manner required by law. A copy of the certificate of incorporation so presented and approved is attached.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|31|31:30"><form.text>By motion duly made, seconded, and unanimously carried, the Secretary was directed to follow the statutory procedure for obtaining the approval of the Supreme Court of the <inline.instr>&lsqb;identification of judicial district&rsqb;</inline.instr> of the above certificate and, upon obtaining such approval, to file the certificate of incorporation in the office of the Secretary of State of the State of New York.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|31|31:30"><form.text>There being no further business to come before the meeting, upon motion duly made, seconded, and unanimously carried, the meeting was adjourned.</form.text></form.para>

<form.name.block><name>CONSENT TO ACTION TAKEN IN LIEU OF THE ORGANIZATION MEETING OF <inline.instr>&lsqb;NAME OF CORPORATION&rsqb;</inline.instr></name></form.name.block>
<form.vertical.space amt="1"/>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|32|31:31"><form.text>The undersigned, being the President of the Corporation, hereby consents to the action taken, as hereafter stated, in lieu of the organization meeting:</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|32|31:31"><form.text>A copy of the certificate of incorporation together with the receipt issued by the Department of State showing the date and payment of the filing fee for the original certificate of incorporation was appended to this statement.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|32|31:31"><form.text>Bylaws regulating the conduct and the affairs of the corporation, as prepared by <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of law firm&rsqb;</inline.instr>, attorneys for the corporation, were adopted and ordered appended thereto.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|32|31:31"><form.text>The following persons were appointed directors of the corporation: <inline.instr>&lsqb;names of directors&rsqb;</inline.instr>.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|32|31:31"><form.text>The principal office of the corporation was fixed at <inline.instr>&lsqb;address of office&rsqb;</inline.instr>, <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of city&rsqb;</inline.instr>, New York <inline.instr>&lsqb;specification of ZIP code&rsqb;</inline.instr>.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|32|31:31"><form.text><inline.instr>&lsqb;Name of depository&rsqb;</inline.instr>, located at <inline.instr>&lsqb;address of depository&rsqb;</inline.instr>, <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of city&rsqb;</inline.instr>, New York <inline.instr>&lsqb;specification of ZIP code&rsqb;</inline.instr>, was designated as depository for bank accounts in the name of the corporation, with <inline.instr>&lsqb;titles of officers&rsqb;</inline.instr> as authorized signatories.</form.text></form.para>

<outline.name.block><label>&sect;</label><designator>31:31.40</designator><name>Statement of incorporator in lieu of organizational meeting</name></outline.name.block>
<online.view>
<online.view.item>FMS</online.view.item>

<form>
<form.name.block><name>STATEMENT OF INCORPORATOR IN LIEU OF ORGANIZATIONAL MEETING OF <inline.instr>&lsqb;NAME OF CORPORATION&rsqb;</inline.instr></name></form.name.block>
<form.vertical.space amt="1"/>
<form.para first.line="none"><form.text>The certificate of incorporation of the above-named corporation having been filed in the Office of the Secretary of State of the State of New York, the undersigned, being the incorporator named in said certificate, does hereby state that the following actions were taken on this day for the purpose of organizing this corporation:</form.text></form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>1</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Bylaws for the regulation of the affairs of the corporation were adopted by the undersigned incorporator and were ordered inserted in the minute book immediately following the copy of the certificate of incorporation and before this instrument.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>2</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>The undersigned hereby resigns as incorporator of the corporation as of the date set forth below and the following are hereby elected as the directors of the corporation to hold office until the first annual meeting of the corporation or until their successors are elected and qualified: <inline.instr>&lsqb;list of names of directors&rsqb;</inline.instr></form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit>
<form.line align="l">Dated: <inline.instr>&lsqb;date of signature&rsqb;</inline.instr></form.line>
<signature.block ref="manual">
<signature.group position="r">
<form.line align="l"><inline.instr>&lsqb;Name of incorporator&rsqb;</inline.instr></form.line>
</signature.group>

<image.block ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|33|31:32">

<note.block>
<note.group note.head="none">
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|33|31:32"><para.text>The above form, revised 12/22, is available from the New York State Department of State, <cite type="url" normalpub="webref">http://www.dos.ny.gov</cite>, and is reprinted here for illustrative purposes.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|33|31:32"><para.text>The required contents of a certificate of incorporation are set forth in <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="402" subref="(a)">N.Y. Not-for-Profit Corp. Law &sect;402(a)</cite>.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|33|31:32"><para.text>The certificate of incorporation may set forth any provision not inconsistent with the New York Not-for-Profit Corporation Law or any other statute of the state which provision is (1) for the regulation of the internal affairs of the corporation, including types or classes of membership and the distribution of assets on dissolution or final liquidation, or (2) required by any governmental body or officer or other person or body as a condition for giving the consent or approval required for filing the certificate of incorporation. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="402" subref="(c)">N-PCL &sect;402(c)</cite>.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|33|31:32"><para.text>The certificate must be signed by each incorporator, with each incorporator&apos;s name and address included in the certificate and delivered to the Department of State, together with any filing fees. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="402" subref="(a)">N-PCL &sect;402(a)</cite>. For a listing of such fees, see <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="104-a">N.Y. Not-for-Profit Corp. Law &sect;104-a</cite>.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|33|31:32"><para.text>For other forms and materials related to the drafting of a certificate of incorporation, see Corporations <cite type="secondaryxref" secref="17:1 et seq." secrange="y">&dblsect;17:1 et seq.</cite> and Social and Recreation Nonprofit Organizations <cite type="secondaryxref" secref="30:1 et seq." secrange="y">&dblsect;30:1 et seq.</cite></para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|33|31:32"><para.text>For a discussion of the incorporation of charitable organizations and the formal requirements, see <cite type="secondaryxref" secref="31:4 et seq." secrange="y">&dblsect;31:4 et seq.</cite></para.text></para>
</note.group>
<research.reference.block>
<reference.entry><ref.text><cite type="topic.key" normalpub="key" sub="Corporations and Business Organizations" numref="3370 to 3379" numrange="y">West&apos;s Key Number Digest, Corporations and Business Organizations &key;3370 to 3379</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
<reference.entry><ref.text><cite type="secondary" normalpub="alr3" titlename="Distribution of funds by nonprofit corporation absent dissolution" volref="51" pageref="1318">Distribution of funds by nonprofit corporation absent dissolution, 51 A.L.R.3d 1318</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
</research.reference.block>
<item.reference.block>
<item.reference><name.block><label>Paragraph</label><designator>First.</designator></name.block>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|33|31:32"><para.text>The corporate name must be distinct and must not violate other statutory requirements. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="301">N-PCL &sect;301</cite>. The corporate name may be reserved under a statutory procedure. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="303">N-PCL &sect;303</cite>. The corporate name may be in a language other than English if it is written in English letters or characters. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="104" subref="(a)">N-PCL &sect;104(a)</cite>. The corporation may not use a name other than the name that appears in the certificate of incorporation without following the procedures to use an assumed name. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="202" subref="(f)">N-PCL &sect;202(f)</cite>.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|33|31:32"><para.text>For a discussion of the procedures for using an assumed name, see <cite type="secondaryxref" secref="21:1 et seq." secrange="y">&dblsect;21:1 et seq.</cite></para.text></para>
<research.reference.block>
<reference.entry><ref.text><cite type="secondary" normalpub="alr3" titlename="Right of charitable or religious association or corporation to protection against use of same or similar name by another" volref="37" pageref="277">Right of charitable or religious association or corporation to protection against use of same or similar name by another, 37 A.L.R.3d 277</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
<reference.entry><ref.text><cite type="secondary" normalpub="nyj2" topicname="Business Relationships" secref="164 to 176" secrange="y">N.Y. Jur. 2d, Business Relationships &dblsect;164 to 176</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
</research.reference.block>
</item.reference>
<item.reference><name.block><label>Paragraph</label><designator>Second.</designator></name.block>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|33|31:32"><para.text>The language incorporating the statutory definition of a not-for-profit corporation is required by statute. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="402" subref="(a)" pararef="(2)">N-PCL &sect;402(a)(2)</cite>.</para.text></para>
</item.reference>
<item.reference><name.block><label>Paragraph</label><designator>Third.</designator></name.block>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|33|31:32"><para.text>The specific purpose(s) for which the corporation is organized must be stated in the certificate of incorporation, it being sufficient to state that the purpose of the corporation is any purpose for which corporations may be organized under the Not-for-Profit Corporation Law. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="402" subref="(a)" pararef="(2)">N-PCL &sect;402(a)(2)</cite>.</para.text></para>
<research.reference.block>
<reference.entry><ref.text><cite type="secondary" normalpub="nyj2" topicname="Business Relationships" secref="57, 58" secrange="y">N.Y. Jur. 2d, Business Relationships &dblsect;57, 58</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
</research.reference.block>
</item.reference>
<item.reference><name.block><label>Paragraph</label><designator>Sixth.</designator></name.block>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|33|31:32"><para.text>The certificate of incorporation must state the county within New York State in which the office of the corporation is to be located. If the office at which the books and records of the corporation will be kept is outside the state, the certificate may identify the post office address of the office. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="402" subref="(a)" pararef="(3)">N-PCL &sect;402(a)(3)</cite>.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|33|31:32"><para.text>The corporation must keep correct and complete books and records of account and minutes of the proceedings of its members, board, and executive committee, if any, at its office. This office may be outside the state if the certificate of incorporation so states. The corporation also must keep a list of its members and their interests in the corporation at its office or at the office of its transfer agent or registrar in New York State. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="621">N-PCL &sect;621</cite>.</para.text></para>
<research.reference.block>
<reference.entry><ref.text><cite type="secondary" normalpub="nyj2" topicname="Business Relationships" secref="369">N.Y. Jur. 2d, Business Relationships &sect;369</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
</research.reference.block>
</item.reference>
<item.reference><name.block><label>Paragraph</label><designator>Seventh.</designator></name.block>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|33|31:32"><para.text>Except as otherwise provided in the certificate of incorporation, the corporation is managed by its board of directors. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="701" subref="(a)">N-PCL &sect;701(a)</cite>. A director is any member of the governing board of a corporation, whether designated as director, trustee, manager, governor, or by any other title. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="102" subref="(6)">N-PCL &sect;102(6)</cite>. Any person who has the same role as a director in a corporation is subject to the same obligations and liabilities as is imposed on a director for managerial acts or omissions. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="701" subref="(b)">N-PCL &sect;701(b)</cite>.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|33|31:32"><para.text>The number of directors cannot be less than three and may be fixed by the bylaws or by a procedure stated in the bylaws. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="702" subref="(a)">N-PCL &sect;702(a)</cite>. The certificate of incorporation must state the names and addresses of the initial directors. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="402" subref="(a)" pararef="(4)">N-PCL &sect;402(a)(4)</cite>.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|33|31:32"><para.text>Each director must be at least 18 years of age except for directors in certain statutorily designated youth organizations. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="701" subref="(a)">N-PCL &sect;701(a)</cite>. The certificate of incorporation or bylaws may prescribe other qualifications for directors. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="701" subref="(a)">N-PCL &sect;701(a)</cite>.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|33|31:32"><para.text>The directors may be elected or appointed in the manner and for the term specified in the certificate of incorporation or the bylaws. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="703" subref="(b)">N-PCL &sect;703(b)</cite>. In the absence of a provision fixing the term of office of a director, the term is one year and, with certain exceptions specified by statute, cannot exceed five years. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="703" subref="(b)">N-PCL &sect;703(b)</cite>. Directors must hold office until the expiration of the term or until a successor is appointed. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="703" subref="(c)">N-PCL &sect;703(c)</cite>. Matters as to election or appointment of directors and their terms of office that may be specified in the certificate of incorporation or bylaws include:</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|33|31:32"><para.text>(1) Election or appointment of directors at large, or by special districts or membership sections, or by virtue of a director&apos;s office or former office in the corporation or other public or private entity, or by bondholders voting as a class, or any combination thereof. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="703" subref="(a)">N-PCL &sect;703(a)</cite>.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|33|31:32"><para.text>(2) Election or appointment of alternate directors if the certificate of incorporation or bylaws provide for appointment or election by special district or by membership section. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="703" subref="(d)">N-PCL &sect;703(d)</cite>.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|33|31:32"><para.text>(3) Staggering the terms of the board members. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="704">N-PCL &sect;704</cite>.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|33|31:32"><para.text>(4) Electing or appointing directors to newly created directorships or to fill vacancies on the board of directors. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="705">N-PCL &sect;705</cite>.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|33|31:32"><para.text>(5) Restricting the members&apos; right to remove a director without cause. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="706" subref="(b)">N-PCL &sect;706(b)</cite>.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|33|31:32"><para.text>(6) Making the number of directors that constitute a quorum more or less than a majority of the board of directors. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="707">N-PCL &dblsect;707</cite>, <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="709" subref="(a)" pararef="(1)">709(a)(1)</cite>.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|33|31:32"><para.text>(7) Prohibiting the board of directors from acting without a formal meeting. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="708" subref="(b)">N-PCL &sect;708(b)</cite>.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|33|31:32"><para.text>(8) Authorizing directors to participate in board or committee meetings by conference telephone or similar communications equipment or by electronic video screen communication. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="708" subref="(c)">N-PCL &sect;708(c)</cite>.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|33|31:32"><para.text>(9) Altering the proportion of directors&apos; votes necessary to transact all or specific types of business. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="709" subref="(a)" pararef="(2)">N-PCL &sect;709(a)(2)</cite>.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|33|31:32"><para.text>(10) Specifying the place of annual, regular, or special meetings of the board of directors. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="710" subref="(a)">N-PCL &sect;710(a)</cite>.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|33|31:32"><para.text>(11) Allowing committees of directors to act on behalf of the board of directors (except as to matters stated in the statute). <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="712">N-PCL &sect;712</cite>.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|33|31:32"><para.text>(12) Advancing or indemnifying directors for expenses. See <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="721">N-PCL &sect;721</cite>.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|33|31:32"><para.text>The certificate of incorporation may contain restrictions on contracts or transactions between the corporation and its directors. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="715" subref="(d)">N-PCL &sect;715(d)</cite>. Unless provided otherwise in the certificate of incorporation or bylaws, the board fixes the compensation of the directors for services in any capacity. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="715" subref="(e)">N-PCL &sect;715(e)</cite>.</para.text></para>
<research.reference.block>
<reference.entry><ref.text><cite type="secondary" normalpub="nyj2" topicname="Business Relationships" secref="71">N.Y. Jur. 2d, Business Relationships &sect;71</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
<reference.entry><ref.text><cite type="secondary" normalpub="nyj2" topicname="Business Relationships" secref="527 to 607" secrange="y">N.Y. Jur. 2d, Business Relationships &dblsect;527 to 607</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
<reference.entry><ref.text><cite type="secondary" normalpub="nyj2" topicname="Business Relationships" secref="683 et seq." secrange="y">N.Y. Jur. 2d, Business Relationships &dblsect;683 et seq.</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
</research.reference.block>
</item.reference>
<item.reference><name.block><label>Paragraph</label><designator>Eighth.</designator></name.block>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|33|31:32"><para.text>The certificate of incorporation must designate the Secretary of State as agent of the corporation upon whom process against it may be served and must designate the post office address to which the Secretary is to mail a copy of process against the corporation served on him or her. The corporation may include an email address to which the secretary of state shall email a notice of the fact that process against it has been electronically served upon him or her. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="402" subref="(a)" pararef="(6)">N-PCL &sect;402(a)(6)</cite>. The Secretary is deemed to be the agent for service of process on a corporation. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="304">N-PCL &sect;304</cite>.</para.text></para>
<research.reference.block>
<reference.entry><ref.text><cite type="secondary" normalpub="nyj2" topicname="Business Relationships" secref="71, 1062, 1063" secrange="y">N.Y. Jur. 2d, Business Relationships &dblsect;71, 1062, 1063</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
</research.reference.block>
</item.reference>
</item.reference.block>
