<section.front>
<outline.name.block><label>&sect;</label><designator>31:32.10</designator><name>Certificate of incorporation<sep/>Private foundation</name></outline.name.block>
<online.view>
<online.view.item>FMS</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>FCV</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>FTR</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>COL</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>NFP</online.view.item>
</online.view>
</section.front>
<section.body>
<form>
<form.name.block><name>CERTIFICATE OF INCORPORATION OF <inline.instr>&lsqb;NAME OF CORPORATION&rsqb;</inline.instr></name></form.name.block>
<form.line align="c">Under <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="402">Section 402 of the Not-For-Profit Corporation Law</cite></form.line>
<form.vertical.space amt="1"/>
<form.para><form.text>The undersigned, being a natural person of at least eighteen years of age and acting as the incorporator of the corporation being formed under the New York Not-for-Profit Corporation Law, certifies that:</form.text></form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>1</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Name. The name of the corporation (hereinafter, the &ldquo;Corporation&rdquo;) is: <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of corporation&rsqb;</inline.instr></form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>2</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>The Corporation is a corporation as defined in Subparagraph (5) of Paragraph (a) of Section 102 of the New York Not-for-Profit Corporation Law.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>3</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Purposes. The Corporation is formed for the following purposes:</form.text></form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(a)</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>To plan, develop, and operate a <inline.instr>&lsqb;specification of event&rsqb;</inline.instr> to raise and distribute funds to charitable organizations that perform medical research and combat diseases, disorders, and other medical disciplines.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(b)</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>To receive and maintain a fund or funds of real or personal property including, without limitation, cash contributions and, subject to the restrictions and limitations set forth in this certificate of incorporation, to use and apply the income and principal for the Corporation&apos;s purposes and activities;</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(c)</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>To do any other act or thing incidental to or connected with the Corporation&apos;s purposes and activities, but not for the pecuniary profit or financial gain of any of the Corporation&apos;s members, trustees, directors or officers, except as permitted under Article 5 of the New York Not-for-Profit Corporation Law, or as permitted in Section 7(a) of this certificate of incorporation; and</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(d)</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>To have in furtherance of its not-for-profit corporate purposes all of the powers conferred upon corporations organized under the New York Not-for-Profit Corporation Law subject to any limitations contained in this certificate of incorporation or in the laws of the State of New York.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>4</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Prohibition on Certain Political Activities. Notwithstanding the foregoing, no substantial part of the activities of the Corporation will be the carrying on of propaganda, or otherwise attempting to influence legislation through improper means, and no part of its activities will entail the participation or intervention in any political campaign by any means, including the publication or distribution of statements on behalf of (or in opposition to) any candidate for public office, nor will the Corporation engage in any activity which would, in the opinion of the directors, jeopardize an exemption from federal income taxation under <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-irc" titleref="26" secref="501" subref="(c)" pararef="(3)" date="1986">section 501(c)(3) of the Internal Revenue Code of 1986</cite> (the &ldquo;Code&rdquo;) and the regulations promulgated thereunder.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>5</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>State Approval. The Corporation is not formed to engage in any activity or of any purpose requiring consent or approval of any state official, department, board, agency or other body. No consent or approval is required.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>6</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Charitable Corporation. The Corporation is a charitable corporation under <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="201">Section 201 of the Not-for-Profit Corporation Law</cite>.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>7</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Restrictions on Use of Earnings and on Distributions.</form.text></form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(a)</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>No part of the net earnings of the Corporation shall inure to the benefit of any member, trustee, director or officer of the Corporation, or any private individual, except that reasonable compensation may be paid to any of the foregoing persons for services rendered to or for the Corporation; and no member, trustee, director or officer of the Corporation, or any private individual, shall be entitled to share in the distribution of any of the Corporation&apos;s assets upon dissolution of the Corporation.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(b)</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>The Corporation shall distribute its income for each taxable year at a time and in a manner that will not result in the Corporation becoming subject to the tax on undistributed income imposed by section 4942 of the Code.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(c)</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>In the event of the dissolution of the Corporation, all of the remaining assets and property of the Corporation, after payment of the necessary expenses, shall be distributed, as the board of directors of the Corporation determines, to another organization or organizations exempt under section 501(c)(3) of the Code, to the federal government, or to state or local government or government agencies operating for a public benefit or a public purpose, subject to any requisite approval and/or jurisdiction of the Supreme Court of the State of New York.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>8</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Prohibitions on Certain Other Activities.</form.text></form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(a)</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>The Corporation shall not: (i) engage in any act of self-dealing as defined in section 4941 of the Code; (ii) retain any excess business holdings as defined in section 4943 of the Code; (iii) make any investments in such manner as to subject it to tax under section 4944 of the Code; or (iv) make any taxable expenditures as defined in section 4945 of the Code.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(b)</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Without limiting the provisions of section 8(a) of this certificate of incorporation, the Corporation is organized exclusively for one or more of the exempt purposes as specified in section 501(c)(3) of the Code and shall not carry on any other activities not permitted to be carried on by (i) a corporation exempt from federal income tax under section 501(c)(3) of the Code and the regulations promulgated thereunder, or (ii) by a corporation to which contributions are deductible under section 170(c)(2) of the Code. Nothing herein contained shall authorize this corporation, directly or indirectly, to engage in or include among its purposes, any of the activities mentioned in <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="404" subref="(b) through (v)">Section 404(b) through (v) of the Not-For-Profit Corporation Law</cite>.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>9</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Office. The office of the Corporation is to be located in the County of <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of county&rsqb;</inline.instr>, State of New York.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>10</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Agent for Service of Process. The Secretary of State of the State of New York is hereby designated the agent of the Corporation upon whom process against it may be served. The post office address to which the Secretary of State shall mail a copy of any process against the Corporation served upon him or her as agent of the Corporation is: <inline.instr>&lsqb;name and address of agent&rsqb;</inline.instr></form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>11</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Indemnification of Directors and Officers. If a director or officer of the Corporation is made a party to any civil or criminal action, suit or proceeding in any matter arising from the performance of his or her duties for or on behalf of the Corporation, then to the fullest extent permitted by law, the Corporation shall indemnify the director or officer for all amounts paid by him or her in connection with the action, suit or proceeding, including any judgments, fines, amounts paid in settlement and reasonable expenses, including attorneys&apos; fees and expenses.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>12</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Initial Directors. The name and the address of each of the initial directors of the Corporation are as follows: <inline.instr>&lsqb;names and addresses of initial directors&rsqb;</inline.instr></form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>13</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Duration. The duration of the Corporation shall be perpetual.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>14</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Private Foundation. During such periods, if any, as the Corporation shall be a &ldquo;private foundation,&rdquo; as that term is defined in the Code, the Corporation shall operate subject to the following restrictions:</form.text></form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(a)</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>The Corporation shall distribute such amounts for each taxable year at such times and in such manner as not to subject the Corporation to tax on undistributed income under Section 4942 of the Code (or any successor provision thereof);</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(b)</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>The Corporation shall not engage in any act of self-dealing which is subject to tax under Section 4941 of the Code (or any successor provision thereof);</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(c)</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>The Corporation shall not retain any excess business holdings as to subject the Corporation to tax under Section 4943 of the Code (or any successor provision thereof);</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(d)</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>The Corporation shall not make any investments in such manner as to subject the corporation to tax under Section 4944 of the Code (or any successor provision thereof); and</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(e)</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>The Corporation shall not make any taxable expenditures, as defined in Section 4945(d) of the Code (or any successor provision thereof).</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>15</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>References to Internal Revenue Code, Etc. Every reference in this certificate of incorporation to the Code, or to any provision thereof or regulation thereunder, shall include every amendment thereto and every corresponding federal law, provision or regulation that may be subsequently enacted or promulgated.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit>

<section.body>
<form>
<form.para><form.text>The Corporation is formed for the following purpose or purposes:</form.text></form.para>
<form.para><form.text>The Corporation is organized exclusively for charitable, religious, educational, and/or scientific purposes, including, for such purposes, the making of distributions to organizations that qualify as exempt organizations under <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-irc" titleref="26" secref="501" subref="(c)" pararef="(3)">Section 501(c)(3) of the Internal Revenue Code</cite>, or the corresponding section of any future federal tax code.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para><form.text>The Corporation will be operated to promote and engage in general charitable activities and will received funds or real or personal property to be applied in whole or in any part of the income therefrom and the principal thereof exclusively for charitable, religious, literary or educational purposes either directly or by contributions to organizations that qualify as exempt organizations under <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-irc" titleref="26" secref="501" subref="(c)" pararef="(3)">Section 501(c)(3) of the Internal Revenue Code</cite>.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para><form.text>The Corporation will solicit funds and accept contributions for the aforementioned purposes.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para><form.text>To have in furtherance of its not-for-profit corporate purposes, the Corporation will have all of the powers conferred upon corporations organized under the Not-for-Profit Corporation Law subject to any limitations thereof contained in this Certificate of Incorporation or in the laws of the State of New York.</form.text></form.para>

<section.front>
<outline.name.block><label>&sect;</label><designator>31:34</designator><name>Certificate of incorporation<sep/>Provision<sep/>Article required to qualify for federal income tax exemption</name></outline.name.block>
<online.view>
<online.view.item>COL</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>NFP</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>CLS</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>FCV</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>FTR</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>EBL</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>TEM</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>MTD</online.view.item>
</online.view>
</section.front>
<section.body>
<form uuid="Ic7044bf0181b11e68c12afa7f3a24041">
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|35|31:34"><form.text>Anything in this certificate of incorporation to the contrary notwithstanding, the purpose or purposes for which this corporation is organized are limited to those that will qualify it as an exempt organization under <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-irc" titleref="26" secref="501" subref="(c)" pararef="(3)">Internal Revenue Code Section 501(c)(3)</cite>, including, for such purposes, the making of distributions to organizations that qualify as tax-exempt organizations under such Code.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|35|31:34"><form.text>This corporation shall not, as a substantial part of its activities, carry on propaganda or otherwise attempt to influence legislation. This corporation shall not participate in or intervene in (including the publishing or distributing of statements) any political campaign on behalf of any candidate for public office.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|35|31:34"><form.text>No part of the net earnings, properties, or assets of this corporation, on dissolution or otherwise, shall inure to the benefit of any private person or individual or any member or director of this corporation. On liquidation or dissolution, all properties and assets of this corporation remaining after paying or providing for all debts and obligations shall be distributed and paid over to such fund, foundation, or corporation organized and operated for charitable or religious purposes as the board of directors shall determine and as shall, at the time, qualify as a tax-exempt organization under <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-irc" titleref="26" secref="501" subref="(c)" pararef="(3)">Internal Revenue Code Section 501(c)(3)</cite> or as the same may be amended.</form.text></form.para>
<note.block>
<note.group note.head="taxnotes">
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|35|31:34"><para.text>Corporations and any community chest, fund, or foundation organized and operated exclusively for religious, charitable, scientific, testing for public safety, literary, or educational purposes, or to foster national or international amateur sports competition (but only if no part of its activities involve the provision of athletic facilities or equipment), or for the prevention of cruelty to children or animals, no part of the net earnings of which inures to the benefit of any private shareholder or individual, no substantial part of the activities of which is carrying on propaganda or otherwise attempting to influence legislation and which does not participate in or intervene in (including the publishing or distributing of statements) any political campaign on behalf of any candidate for public office, are exempt from taxation on their income. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-code" titleref="26" secref="501" subref="(c)" pararef="(3)">26 U.S.C.A. &sect;501(c)(3)</cite>; <cite type="lrre" normalpub="exec-us-cfr" titleref="26" secref="1.501(c)(3)-1">26 C.F.R. &sect;1.501(c)(3)-1</cite>. For such an organization to be exempt, it must be organized and operated exclusively for one or more of the purposes specified in the exemption statute, and, if it fails to meet either the organizational test or the operational test, it is not exempt. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="exec-us-cfr" titleref="26" secref="1.501(c)(3)-1" subref="(a)" pararef="(1)">26 C.F.R. &sect;1.501(c)(3)-1(a)(1)</cite>.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|35|31:34"><para.text>The provisions contained in the above form cover the general requirements imposed on organizations seeking tax-exempt status under <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-irc" titleref="26" secref="501" subref="(c)" pararef="(3)">Section 501(c)(3) of the Internal Revenue Code</cite>. Depending on the nature of the organization, other requirements may also be imposed. The exact section of the Code governing the particular type of organization formed will determine any further qualifications. If these exist, they, too, should be included in the certificate.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|35|31:34"><para.text>Although the form starts with the words &ldquo;Anything in this certificate of incorporation to the contrary notwithstanding &hellip;,&rdquo; the purposes stated should be only one or more of the exempt purposes allowed under the Code. Powers and purposes beyond those will lead to rejection of the exempt status even if an exempt purpose is pleaded under the &ldquo;to the contrary notwithstanding&rdquo; phrase.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|35|31:34"><para.text>The incorporation of this provision into the certificate of incorporation of a corporation organized for charitable purposes should enable the corporation to claim an exemption from taxation of income by making the corporation an exempt organization under <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-code" titleref="26" secref="501" subref="(c)" pararef="(3)">26 U.S.C.A. &sect;501(c)(3)</cite>, <cite type="lrre" normalpub="exec-us-cfr" titleref="26" secref="1.501(c)(3)-1">26 C.F.R. &sect;1.501(c)(3)-1</cite>.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|35|31:34"><para.text>For discussion concerning qualifying for exemption from federal income taxation, see <cite type="secondaryxref" secref="31:9 et seq." secrange="y">&dblsect;31:9 et seq.</cite></para.text></para>
</note.group>
<research.reference.block>
<reference.entry><ref.text><cite type="topic.key" normalpub="key" sub="Internal Revenue" numref="4045 to 4079" numrange="y">West&apos;s Key Number Digest, Internal Revenue &key;4045 to 4079</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
</research.reference.block>
</note.block>

<form uuid="Ic7047300181b11e68c12afa7f3a24041">
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(a)</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Distribution of Income.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|36|31:35"><form.text>The corporation shall distribute its income for each taxable year at such time and in such manner as not to become subject to the tax on undistributed income imposed by <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-irc" titleref="26" secref="4942">Section 4942 of the Internal Revenue Code</cite> or corresponding provisions of any subsequent federal tax laws.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(b)</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Self-dealing.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|36|31:35"><form.text>The corporation shall not engage in any act of self-dealing as defined in <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-irc" titleref="26" secref="4941" subref="(d)">Section 4941(d) of the Internal Revenue Code</cite> or corresponding provisions of any subsequent federal tax law.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(c)</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Excess Business Holdings.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|36|31:35"><form.text>The corporation shall not retain any excess business holdings as defined in <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-irc" titleref="26" secref="4943" subref="(c)">Section 4943(c) of the Internal Revenue Code</cite> or corresponding provisions of any subsequent federal tax laws.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(d)</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Investments Jeopardizing Charitable Purpose.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|36|31:35"><form.text>The corporation shall not make any investments in such manner as to subject it to tax under <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-irc" titleref="26" secref="4944">Section 4944 of the Internal Revenue Code</cite> or corresponding provisions of any subsequent federal tax laws.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(e)</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Taxable Expenditures.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|36|31:35"><form.text>The corporation shall not make any taxable expenditures as defined in <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-irc" titleref="26" secref="4945" subref="(d)">Section 4945(d) of the Internal Revenue Code</cite> or corresponding provisions of any subsequent federal tax law.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit>
<note.block>
<note.group note.head="taxnotes">
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|36|31:35"><para.text>This provision is intended to qualify a private foundation, otherwise exempt, for exemption from federal income taxation under <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-code" titleref="26" secref="508" subref="(e)">26 U.S.C.A. &sect;508(e)</cite> and has specifically been held adequate for that purpose by the Internal Revenue Service. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="exec-us-irs-ruling" numref="70-270" volref="1970-1" reporter="C.B." volpg="135">Rev. Rul. 70-270, 1970-1 C.B. 135</cite>.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|36|31:35"><para.text>If a disqualified person engages in self-dealing with a trust, that person is subject to a 10&percnt; tax that goes up to 200&percnt; if the self-dealing is not rectified. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-code" titleref="26" secref="4941">26 U.S.C.A. &sect;4941</cite>. A disqualified person is one or more of the following: (See <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-code" titleref="26" secref="4946" subref="(a)">26 U.S.C.A. &sect;4946(a)</cite>.)</para.text>
<list list.style="para">
<list.item><name.block><designator>1)</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|36|31:35"><para.text>a substantial contributor;</para.text></para></list.item>
<list.item><name.block><designator>2)</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|36|31:35"><para.text>a foundation manager;</para.text></para></list.item>
<list.item><name.block><designator>3)</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|36|31:35"><para.text>a person who owns more than 20&percnt; of a corporation, partnership, trust, or unincorporated enterprise which is itself a substantial contributor; and/or</para.text></para></list.item>
<list.item><name.block><designator>4)</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|36|31:35"><para.text>a member of the family of any individual of the first three categories.</para.text></para></list.item>
</list></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|36|31:35"><para.text>Self-dealing includes certain financial transactions, engaged in directly or indirectly by a &ldquo;disqualified person.&rdquo; See <cite type="lrre" normalpub="exec-us-cfr" titleref="26" secref="53.4941(d)-2">26 C.F.R. &sect;53.4941(d)-2</cite>.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|36|31:35"><para.text>For discussion of application for exemption from the foundation rules, see <cite type="secondaryxref" secref="31:22">&sect;31:22</cite>.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|36|31:35"><para.text>For discussion of the requirements concerning contents of organizational documents of a private foundation, generally, see <cite type="secondaryxref" secref="31:23">&sect;31:23</cite>.</para.text></para>
</note.group>
<research.reference.block>
<reference.entry><ref.text><cite type="topic.key" normalpub="key" sub="Internal Revenue" numref="4045 to 4079" numrange="y">West&apos;s Key Number Digest, Internal Revenue &key;4045 to 4079</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
</research.reference.block>
</note.block>

<section.body>
<form uuid="Ic704c120181b11e68c12afa7f3a24041">
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|37|31:36"><form.text>In the event of the dissolution of this corporation, or if it shall cease to carry out the purposes set forth in Article <inline.instr>&lsqb;designation of article&rsqb;</inline.instr>, all the business, property, and assets of the corporation shall be distributed to an organization or organizations organized and operated exclusively for <inline.instr>&lsqb;specification of tax-exempt purpose&rsqb;</inline.instr> and that is tax exempt under <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-irc" titleref="26" secref="501" subref="(c)" pararef="(3)">&sect;501(c)(3) of the Internal Revenue Code</cite>, as amended. That organization shall be <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of organization&rsqb;</inline.instr> if it qualifies as a distributee under this Article. No part of the assets or property of this corporation shall be distributed to members, either for the reimbursement of any sums subscribed, donated, or contributed by members or for any other purpose, it being the intent in the event of the dissolution of this corporation, or on its ceasing to carry out the purposes of the corporation, that the property and assets then owned by the corporation shall be devoted to the following nonprofit charitable purpose: <inline.instr>&lsqb;&lsqb;name of tax-exempt purpose&rsqb;/&lsqb;name of charitable purpose&rsqb;&rsqb;</inline.instr>.</form.text></form.para>
<note.block>
<note.group note.head="taxnotes">
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|37|31:36"><para.text>An organization is not organized exclusively for one or more exempt purposes unless its assets are dedicated to an exempt purpose. An organization&apos;s assets will be considered dedicated to an exempt purpose, for example, if, upon dissolution, such assets would, by reason of a provision in the organization&apos;s articles or by operation of law, be distributed for one or more exempt purposes or to the federal government or to a state or local government, for a public purpose, or would be distributed by a court to another organization to be used in such manner as in the judgment of the court will best accomplish the general purposes for which the dissolved organization was organized. However, an organization does not meet the organizational test if its articles or the law of the state in which it was created provides that its assets would, upon dissolution, be distributed to its members or shareholders. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="exec-us-cfr" titleref="26" secref="1.501(c)(3)-1" subref="(b)" pararef="(4)">26 C.F.R. &sect;1.501(c)(3)-1(b)(4)</cite>.</para.text></para>
</note.group>

<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|41|31:40"><form.text>Time of meeting: <inline.instr>&lsqb;time of meeting&rsqb;</inline.instr></form.text></form.para>

<form.vertical.space amt="1"/>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|42|31:41"><form.text>The Board of Directors of <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of corporation&rsqb;</inline.instr> held its first meeting at <inline.instr>&lsqb;location of meeting&rsqb;</inline.instr>, <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of city&rsqb;</inline.instr>, NY <inline.instr>&lsqb;specification of ZIP code&rsqb;</inline.instr> on <inline.instr>&lsqb;date of meeting&rsqb;</inline.instr>.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|42|31:41"><form.text>The following directors, constituting a quorum of the full board, were present at the meeting:</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|42|31:41"><form.text><inline.instr>&lsqb;names of directors present&rsqb;</inline.instr></form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|42|31:41"><form.text>The following directors were absent: <inline.instr>&lsqb;&lsqb;names of directors absent&rsqb;/none&rsqb;</inline.instr></form.text></form.para>
<form.vertical.space amt="1"/>
<form.line align="c">BYLAWS APPROVAL</form.line>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|42|31:41"><form.text>The Corporation distributed its Bylaws to the officers of the Corporation. Upon motion duly made and seconded, it was</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|42|31:41"><form.text>RESOLVED, the Corporation&apos;s proposed Bylaws are adopted in full.</form.text></form.para>
<form.vertical.space amt="1"/>
<form.line align="c">APPLICATION FOR RECOGNITION OF EXEMPTION UNDER <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-irc" titleref="26" secref="501" subref="(c)" pararef="(3)">SECTION 501(c)(3) OF THE INTERNAL REVENUE CODE</cite></form.line>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|42|31:41"><form.text><inline.instr>&lsqb;Name of officer&rsqb;</inline.instr>, <inline.instr>&lsqb;title of officer&rsqb;</inline.instr>, talked about the necessity for the corporation to apply to the Internal Revenue Service in order to have the corporation recognized as exempt under section 501(c)(3), and</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|42|31:41"><form.text>On motion duly made, seconded and unanimously carried, the following resolution was adopted:</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|42|31:41"><form.text>RESOLVED, that the board of directors request <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of company&rsqb;</inline.instr> to proceed with the filing of Form 1023 in order to obtain such recognition by the Internal Revenue Service and to be paid the respective fees that might be required to pay with the application.</form.text></form.para>
<form.vertical.space amt="1"/>
<form.line align="c">ELECTION OF DIRECTORS AND OFFICERS</form.line>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|42|31:41"><form.text>A permanent set of officers and directors needs be elected. Upon a motion duly made, seconded and unanimously carried, it was</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|42|31:41"><form.text>RESOLVED, that the following individuals are elected as directors of the corporation: <inline.instr>&lsqb;names of elected directors&rsqb;</inline.instr></form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|42|31:41"><form.text>FURTHER RESOLVED, that <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of president&rsqb;</inline.instr> is elected President of the corporation.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|42|31:41"><form.text>FURTHER RESOLVED, that <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of vice-president&rsqb;</inline.instr> is elected Vice-President of the corporation.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|42|31:41"><form.text>FURTHER RESOLVED, that <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of treasurer&rsqb;</inline.instr> is elected Treasurer of the corporation.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|42|31:41"><form.text>FURTHER RESOLVED, that <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of secretary&rsqb;</inline.instr> is elected Secretary.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|42|31:41"><form.text>FURTHER RESOLVED, that <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of director 1&rsqb;</inline.instr> is elected Director.</form.text></form.para>

<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|42|31:41"><form.text>Because there was no further business to come before the meeting, on motion duly made and seconded, the meeting was adjourned.</form.text></form.para>

<form uuid="Ic70620b0181b11e68c12afa7f3a24041">
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|43|31:42"><form.text>Minutes of the first meeting of the board of directors named in the certificate of incorporation of <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of corporation&rsqb;</inline.instr>, a New York not-for-profit corporation, which meeting was held at <inline.instr>&lsqb;address of corporation&rsqb;</inline.instr>, <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of city&rsqb;</inline.instr>, <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of county&rsqb;</inline.instr>, State of New York, on <inline.instr>&lsqb;date of first meeting&rsqb;</inline.instr>, at <inline.instr>&lsqb;time of first meeting&rsqb;</inline.instr>.</form.text></form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>1</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Attendance.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|43|31:42"><form.text>Present at the meeting and constituting a quorum of the full board were: <inline.instr>&lsqb;names of directors in attendance&rsqb;</inline.instr>.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|43|31:42"><form.text>Absent were: <inline.instr>&lsqb;names of absent directors&rsqb;</inline.instr>.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>2</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Temporary Chairperson and Secretary.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|43|31:42"><form.text>On motion duly approved, <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of temporary chairperson&rsqb;</inline.instr> was elected temporary chairperson and <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of temporary secretary&rsqb;</inline.instr> was elected temporary secretary of the meeting.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>3</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Call and Notice of Meeting.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|43|31:42"><form.text><inline.instr>&lsqb;Specification of manner of notice of meeting&rsqb;</inline.instr>. On motion duly approved, a copy of the call and notice was made a part of the minutes of this meeting.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>4</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Filing of Certificate of Incorporation.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|43|31:42"><form.text>The temporary chairperson reported that the original certificate of incorporation was filed with the Secretary of State of the State of New York on <inline.instr>&lsqb;date of filing original certificate of incorporation&rsqb;</inline.instr>. A certified copy of the certificate of incorporation, showing the above filing, was delivered to the temporary secretary with directions to insert it in the minute book of the corporation.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>5</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Adoption of Bylaws.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|43|31:42"><form.text>A draft of bylaws prepared by the attorney for the corporation was presented by the acting secretary, who read the full text to the meeting. After discussion, on motion duly approved, the following resolution was adopted:</form.text>
<quote.block>
<quote.para pstart="y"><para.text>Whereas, no bylaws have been adopted governing the conduct of the internal affairs of this corporation; and</para.text></quote.para>
<quote.para pstart="y"><para.text>Whereas, there has been presented to this meeting a set of bylaws suitable for the purpose, and their adoption is in the best interest of the corporation;</para.text></quote.para>
<quote.para pstart="y"><para.text>Resolved, that the bylaws presented to this meeting are adopted as the bylaws of this corporation effective immediately;</para.text></quote.para>
<quote.para pstart="y"><para.text>Further resolved, that the bylaws be authenticated as such by the certificate of the secretary of this corporation and placed in the minute book and that a current, full, and true copy of the bylaws, certified by the Secretary, be kept at the principal office of the corporation for inspection by members at all reasonable times during business hours.</para.text></quote.para>
</quote.block></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>6</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Election of Officers.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|43|31:42"><form.text>The chairperson announced that the bylaws provided for the election of a president, vice-president, secretary, and treasurer and that nominations were in order for the election of such officers. The following slate of officers was then nominated:</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|43|31:42"><form.text><inline.instr>&lsqb;Name of president&rsqb;</inline.instr>, President; <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of vice-president&rsqb;</inline.instr>, Vice-President; <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of secretary&rsqb;</inline.instr>, Secretary; <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of treasurer&rsqb;</inline.instr>, Treasurer. There being no further nominations, by motion duly approved, the slate of nominees was elected to hold office <inline.instr>&lsqb;OPTIONAL: for the terms provided in the bylaws&rsqb;</inline.instr>.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|43|31:42"><form.text>Each elected officer was present at the meeting and assumed the duties of office. The President replaced the temporary chairperson as presiding officer of the meeting. The Secretary replaced the temporary secretary of the meeting.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>7</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Bond for Treasurer.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|43|31:42"><form.text>On motion made, seconded, and unanimously carried, it was resolved that the Treasurer be required to post a corporate surety bond in the amount of &dollar;<inline.instr>&lsqb;dollar amount of corporate surety bond&rsqb;</inline.instr> before assuming the duties of that office and that the President be authorized to approve the bond as to its sufficiency and form.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>8</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Adoption of Seal.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|43|31:42"><form.text>On motion duly approved, it was resolved that the corporation adopt as its seal the words, figures, and design impressed on these minutes consisting of the words <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of corporation&rsqb;</inline.instr>, and the words and figures &ldquo;Incorporated on <inline.instr>&lsqb;date of incorporation&rsqb;</inline.instr>, State of New York.&rdquo; <inline.instr>&lsqb;Impression of seal&rsqb;</inline.instr>.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>9</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Depository for and Withdrawal of Funds.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|43|31:42"><form.text>To provide a depository for the funds of the corporation and to authorize those who may withdraw such funds on behalf of the corporation, on motion duly approved, the following resolution was adopted:</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|43|31:42"><form.text>Resolved, that <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of financial institution&rsqb;</inline.instr>, a corporation (the &ldquo;depository&rdquo;), is selected as a depository for the funds of this corporation and that accounts shall be governed by the rules, regulations, bylaws, and practices, present and future, of the depository, including interest and service charges;</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|43|31:42"><form.text>Further resolved, that the following officers of this corporation, who have been regularly elected or appointed:</form.text>
<tbl ident="NYLB:31-42_001">

<form.para first.line="none"><form.text>are authorized, on signature of any two of them, to withdraw those funds from the depository on the check of the corporation, signed as provided above, and that the officers authorized to withdraw funds are authorized to endorse and receive payment of bills and notes payable to the corporation;</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|43|31:42"><form.text>Further resolved, that the depository is authorized to pay any such instruments so endorsed and presented to it for payment, including those drawn to the individual order of any officer or any other person authorized to sign the instruments; and</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|43|31:42"><form.text>Further resolved, that the authority conferred by these minutes shall remain in full force and effect until written notice of its revocation by the board of directors of this corporation is received by the depository and that the Secretary is authorized and directed to deliver to the depository a certified copy of this resolution and to certify to it the true and correct signatures of the above-named officers.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>10</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Application for Tax Exemption.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|43|31:42"><form.text>The matter of corporate exemption from taxation was then discussed. After discussion, on motion duly approved, the following resolution was adopted:</form.text>
<quote.block>
<quote.para pstart="y"><para.text>Whereas, this corporation is organized for &lsqb;charitable/&lsqb;description of purpose of formation&rsqb;&rsqb; purposes within the meaning of <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-irc" titleref="26" secref="501" subref="(c)" pararef="(3)">Section 501(c)(3) of the Internal Revenue Code</cite>; and</para.text></quote.para>
<quote.para pstart="y"><para.text>Whereas, those and other statutes provide that corporations organized for such charitable purposes are exempt from federal income taxes, state franchise taxes, property taxes, and other forms of taxes and fees;</para.text></quote.para>
<quote.para pstart="y"><para.text>Resolved, that the secretary of this corporation is authorized to make application for such exemptions and to do any and all things which may be necessary to apply for and establish such exemptions, including the certification and transmission to the Internal Revenue Service of copies of the certificate of incorporation, bylaws, and financial statements of this corporation and furnishing to the New York State Department of Taxation and Finance and the County Assessor for &lsqb;name of county&rsqb;, New York, the copy of the Internal Revenue Service&apos;s letter of exemption or other evidence establishing that the corporation has applied in good faith for the federal tax exemption, together with such other documents as are necessary for the corporation to establish such exemptions.</para.text></quote.para>
</quote.block></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>11</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Payment of Organizational Expenses.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|43|31:42"><form.text>Payment for legal services in the formation and organization of this corporation was next considered. The Secretary read to the meeting a letter from <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of attorney&rsqb;</inline.instr> advising that the fee for <inline.instr>&lsqb;his/her&rsqb;</inline.instr> professional services in the organization and formation of this corporation is &dollar;<inline.instr>&lsqb;dollar amount of legal fees&rsqb;</inline.instr>. After discussion, on motion duly approved, the following resolution was adopted:</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|43|31:42"><form.text>Resolved, that the fair monetary value to this corporation of legal services performed in the formation and organization of the corporation is &dollar;<inline.instr>&lsqb;dollar amount of legal fees&rsqb;</inline.instr> and that the Treasurer is authorized and directed to pay to <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of attorney&rsqb;</inline.instr>, by check of this corporation, the above amount.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>12</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Adjournment.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|43|31:42"><form.text>There being no further business to come before the meeting, on motion duly made, seconded, and unanimously carried, the meeting was declared adjourned.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit>

<note.block>
<note.group note.head="none">
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|43|31:42"><para.text>After the certificate of incorporation is filed with the Department of State, a meeting to organize the corporation is held. The meeting is between the initial directors named in the certificate of incorporation or, if none were named, between the incorporators. The meeting need not be held in New York State. At the meeting, the directors or incorporators:</para.text>
<list list.style="para">
<list.item><name.block><designator>(1)</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|43|31:42"><para.text>Adopt bylaws.</para.text></para></list.item>
<list.item><name.block><designator>(2)</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|43|31:42"><para.text>Elect directors as provided in the certificate of incorporation or bylaws.</para.text></para></list.item>
<list.item><name.block><designator>(3)</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|43|31:42"><para.text>Transact such other business as comes before the meeting.</para.text></para></list.item>
</list></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|43|31:42"><para.text>The procedures as to notice of the meeting and as to other procedural aspects of the meeting are specified by statute. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="405" subref="(a)">N-PCL &sect;405(a)</cite>.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|43|31:42"><para.text>For other matters that may be considered at the first meeting of the board of directors of a corporation, see <cite type="secondaryxref" secref="17:1 et seq." secrange="y">&dblsect;17:1 et seq.</cite></para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|43|31:42"><para.text>For discussion of formal requirements for incorporating, see <cite type="secondaryxref" secref="31:5">&sect;31:5</cite>.</para.text></para>
</note.group>

<form.item><name.block><designator>9</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|44|31:43"><form.text>New Business</form.text></form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>A</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|44|31:43"><form.text>E-mail list.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|44|31:43"><form.text><inline.instr>&lsqb;Name of reporter&rsqb;</inline.instr> reported that our e-mail list continues to show a growth in its subscriber base and that <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of persons&rsqb;</inline.instr> persons were now subscribers. <inline.instr>&lsqb;He/She&rsqb;</inline.instr> briefly discussed the problem of abusive postings by a small number of subscribers.</form.text></form.para>

<section.body>
<form>
<form.name.block><name>Written Consent in Lieu of Meeting of the Members of the Board of Directors</name></form.name.block>
<form.line align="l"><inline.instr>&lsqb;Date of consent&rsqb;</inline.instr></form.line>
<form.vertical.space amt="1"/>
<form.para><form.text>The undersigned, being all of the members of the Board of Directors (the &ldquo;Board&rdquo;) of <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of corporation&rsqb;</inline.instr>, a New York not-for profit corporation (the &ldquo;Corporation&rdquo;), hereby consents to the taking of the following actions and the adoption of the following resolutions and agrees that such actions and resolutions shall have the same force and effect as if duly adopted at a meeting of the directors duly called and held for the purpose:</form.text></form.para>
<form.line align="l"><inline.instr>&lsqb;Recitation of resolutions&rsqb;</inline.instr></form.line>
<form.para><form.text>RESOLVED, that, on behalf of and in the name of the Corporation, the Officers be, and each of them acting alone hereby is, authorized and empowered to take any and all further action, to execute and deliver such documents, agreements or instruments and to take all further steps deemed by such Officers, or any one of them, to be necessary, appropriate or desirable to carry out the purposes and intent and to consummate the transactions contemplated by the foregoing resolutions; and it is hereby confirmed that all such action taken or to be taken by the Officers, or any one of them, was or will be taken as a representative of the Corporation.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para><form.text>RESOLVED, that whenever it is provided in the foregoing resolutions that any person or persons may execute any document, take any action, or do any thing which such person or persons deem necessary or appropriate, the execution of such document, the taking of such action, or the doing of such thing shall be deemed conclusive evidence that the execution, taking, or doing thereof, as the case may be, is deemed by such person or persons to be necessary or appropriate.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para><form.text>RESOLVED, that any actions taken by the Officers, or any representatives thereof, or any of them, prior to the adoption of these resolutions which are within the authority conferred hereby be, and they hereby are, ratified, confirmed, authorized, accepted and approved.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para><form.text>RESOLVED, that this consent be filed with the records of the Corporation.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para><form.text>IN WITNESS WHEREOF, the undersigned has executed this consent as of the date first set forth above.</form.text></form.para>
<form.line align="l">Dated: <inline.instr>&lsqb;date of consent&rsqb;</inline.instr></form.line>

<signature.group position="r">

<form uuid="Ic7070b10181b11e68c12afa7f3a24041">
<form.name.block><name>CONSENT IN LIEU OF ANNUAL MEETING OF THE MEMBERS OF <inline.instr>&lsqb;NAME OF CORPORATION&rsqb;</inline.instr></name></form.name.block>
<form.vertical.space amt="1"/>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|47|31:46"><form.text>The undersigned, constituting all of the Members of <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of corporation&rsqb;</inline.instr>, a New York nonprofit corporation (the &ldquo;Corporation&rdquo;), in lieu of holding an annual meeting, hereby consent to the adoption of the following resolutions, agreeing that such resolutions shall have the same force and effect as if unanimously adopted at a meeting of the Members at which all Members were present:</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|47|31:46"><form.text>RESOLVED, that the following individuals are hereby elected to serve as additional members of the Board of Directors of the Corporation: <inline.instr>&lsqb;names of individuals&rsqb;</inline.instr>;</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|47|31:46"><form.text>RESOLVED FURTHER, that the following individuals are hereby unanimously elected as additional Members of the Corporation: <inline.instr>&lsqb;names of additional members&rsqb;</inline.instr>;</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|47|31:46"><form.text>RESOLVED FURTHER, that the Certificate of Incorporation, Article <inline.instr>&lsqb;designation of article&rsqb;</inline.instr>, <inline.instr>&lsqb;title of article&rsqb;</inline.instr>, be amended to include the following clause: <inline.instr>&lsqb;recitation of clause&rsqb;</inline.instr>;</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|47|31:46"><form.text>RESOLVED FURTHER, that this instrument may be executed and delivered in any number of counterparts and by facsimile or other electronic means, each of which shall be deemed to be an original, but all of which together shall constitute one and the same instrument.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|47|31:46"><form.text>IN WITNESS WHEREOF, the undersigned have executed this instrument this <inline.instr>&lsqb;ordinal number of day&rsqb;</inline.instr> day of <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of month&rsqb;</inline.instr> <inline.instr>&lsqb;identification of year&rsqb;</inline.instr>.</form.text></form.para>

<section.front>
<outline.name.block><label>&sect;</label><designator>31:47</designator><name>Bylaws<sep/>Nonprofit corporation</name></outline.name.block>
<online.view>
<online.view.item>FMS</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>NFP</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>COL</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>FCV</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>FTR</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>EBL</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>TEM</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>MTD</online.view.item>
</online.view>
</section.front>
<section.body>
<form uuid="Ic7075930181b11e68c12afa7f3a24041">
<form.unit>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>1</designator><name>PURPOSE</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|48|31:47"><form.text><inline.instr>&lsqb;Name of corporation&rsqb;</inline.instr> (the &ldquo;Corporation&rdquo;) is created and shall be operated exclusively to <inline.instr>&lsqb;statement of purpose&rsqb;</inline.instr>, consistent with the requirements of <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-irc" titleref="26" secref="501" subref="(c)" pararef="(3)" date="1986">501(c)(3) of the Internal Revenue Code of 1986</cite> (the &ldquo;Code&rdquo;).</form.text></form.para>
<form.vertical.space amt="1"/></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>2</designator><name>BOARD OF DIRECTORS</name></name.block></head>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>2.1</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|48|31:47"><form.text>General Powers. The management, control and operation of the affairs and properties of the Corporation are vested in the board of directors of the Corporation (the &ldquo;Board&rdquo;).</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>2.2</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|48|31:47"><form.text>Number and Qualifications of Directors.</form.text></form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(a)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|48|31:47"><form.text>The Board shall consist of no fewer than three (3) and no more than <inline.instr>&lsqb;text number of maximum directors&rsqb;</inline.instr> (<inline.instr>&lsqb;number of maximum directors&rsqb;</inline.instr>) persons (the &ldquo;Directors&rdquo;). The exact number of Directors shall be set from time to time by resolution of the Board.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(b)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|48|31:47"><form.text>The Directors shall consist of persons who support the purpose of the Corporation. Other qualifications for Directors and criteria for the selection process may be established from time to time by the Board.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>2.3</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|48|31:47"><form.text>Election. The Directors shall be elected by the Board at its Annual Meeting. The Board shall elect the number of Directors necessary to maintain staggered terms pursuant to Section 2.4, and such additional persons as may be necessary to fill unexpired terms each year.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>2.4</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|48|31:47"><form.text>Term. Each Director shall serve a term of <inline.instr>&lsqb;text number of years&rsqb;</inline.instr> (<inline.instr>&lsqb;number of years&rsqb;</inline.instr>) years or until such Director&apos;s successor is appointed and qualified. If determined by the Board, the terms of the initial Board may be staggered so that the terms of future directors expire in different years. Directors may be reappointed for successive terms. When vacancies on the Board occur by reason of death, resignation, failure of qualification, or otherwise, the number shall be reduced by such vacancies until qualified replacements are appointed. Replacements shall be selected by the Board to fill the unexpired term.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>2.5</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|48|31:47"><form.text>Resignation and Removal. A resignation by a Director must be in writing and is effective when received by the Secretary. Any Director may be removed from the Board for any reason by a vote of two-thirds (2/3) of all of the other Directors.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>2.6</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|48|31:47"><form.text>Annual Meeting. The annual meeting of the Board shall be held in the <inline.instr>&lsqb;ordinal number of quarter&rsqb;</inline.instr> quarter of each year on such day and at such place and time as determined by the President (the &ldquo;Annual Meeting&rdquo;). The purpose of the Annual Meeting is to elect Directors and officers, and for the transaction of such other business as may come before the meeting.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>2.7</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|48|31:47"><form.text>Regular and Special Meetings. Regular meetings of the Board shall be held at such times as the President may designate, at such other place as the President may designate. Special meetings of the Board may be called by the President or by <inline.instr>&lsqb;text number of directors&rsqb;</inline.instr> (<inline.instr>&lsqb;number of directors&rsqb;</inline.instr>) or more Directors at such time and place as the President or Directors calling the meeting may specify and in accordance with the notice requirements of Section 2.13.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>2.8</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|48|31:47"><form.text>Quorum. To establish a quorum of the Board, a simple majority of all the Directors must be present.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>2.9</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|48|31:47"><form.text>Manner of Acting. The act of the majority of the Directors present at a meeting at which a quorum is present is the duly authorized act of the Board, except where otherwise provided by law or these Bylaws.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>2.10</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|48|31:47"><form.text>Action Without a Meeting. Any action required or permitted to be taken at a meeting of the Board may be taken without a meeting if a consent in writing or electronic setting forth the action to be taken is signed by all of the Directors, provided all Directors receive notice of the text of the written consent and of its effective date and time. Any such consent signed by all of the Directors has the same effect as a unanimous vote taken at a duly convened meeting of the Board at which a quorum is present and shall be filed with the minutes of the proceedings of the Board.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>2.11</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|48|31:47"><form.text>Compensation. Directors will not be paid compensation for their services as Directors, provided that nothing in these Bylaws will be construed to prohibit payment of compensation to an individual who serves as a Director for services rendered to the Corporation in another capacity or reimbursement of expenses related to undertaking the Corporation&apos;s business.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>2.12</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|48|31:47"><form.text>Meetings by Conference Telephone or Electronic Means of Communication. Members of the Board or any committee of the Board may conduct any regular or special meeting by use of a conference telephone or similar communications equipment or by electronic video screen communication provided: (1) all participating Directors may simultaneously hear each other&apos;s communications during the meeting and (2) each director can participate in all matters before the board, including, without limitation, the ability to propose, object to, and vote upon a specific action to be taken by the board or committee. Before the commencement of any business at a meeting at which any Directors do not participate in person, all participating Directors shall be informed that a meeting is taking place at which official business may be transacted. Participation in such manner shall constitute presence in person at such meeting for the purposes of these Bylaws.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>2.13</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|48|31:47"><form.text>Notice. Notice need not be given of regular meetings of the Board, except a regular meeting at which the amendment or repeal of the Bylaws or the adoption of new Bylaws or the removal of a Director is to be considered requires <inline.instr>&lsqb;text number of days&rsqb;</inline.instr> (<inline.instr>&lsqb;number of days&rsqb;</inline.instr>) days&apos; advance written notice. Special meetings must be preceded by at least <inline.instr>&lsqb;text number of hours&rsqb;</inline.instr> (<inline.instr>&lsqb;number of hours&rsqb;</inline.instr>) hours&apos; notice to each Director if notice is given by electronic mail (&ldquo;e-mail&rdquo;), or <inline.instr>&lsqb;text number of hours&rsqb;</inline.instr> (<inline.instr>&lsqb;number of hours&rsqb;</inline.instr>) hours&apos; notice if notice is given by mail or private carrier. Notice of meetings may be given by &ldquo;e-mail&rdquo;, provided, however, Directors who cannot receive notices electronically must receive notice via mail or personal delivery.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>2.14</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|48|31:47"><form.text>Waiver of Notice. Notice of a meeting need not be given to any director who submits a waiver of notice whether before or after the meeting, or who attends the meeting without protesting, prior thereto or at its commencement, the lack of notice to him or her. Such waiver of notice may be written or electronic. If written, the waiver must be executed by the director signing such waiver or causing his or her signature to be affixed to such waiver by any reasonable means including but not limited to facsimile signature. If electronic, the transmission of the waiver must be sent by electronic mail and set forth, or be submitted with, information from which it can reasonably be determined that the transmission was authorized by the director.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>2.15</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|48|31:47"><form.text>Director Conflict of Interest. The Board shall comply with the Conflict of Interest Policy attached as Exhibit <inline.instr>&lsqb;designation of exhibit&rsqb;</inline.instr>.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit>
<form.vertical.space amt="1"/></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>3</designator><name>OFFICERS</name></name.block></head>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>3.1</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|48|31:47"><form.text>Officers. The officers of the Corporation are a President, a Vice-President, a Secretary, and a Treasurer. The officers shall be chosen from among the Directors. The same individual may serve as both the Secretary and Treasurer.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>3.2</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|48|31:47"><form.text>Election and Term of Office. The Board shall elect the officers of the Corporation for <inline.instr>&lsqb;text number of years&rsqb;</inline.instr> (<inline.instr>&lsqb;number of years&rsqb;</inline.instr>) year terms, or until the Board again elects new officers, whichever occurs first.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>3.3</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|48|31:47"><form.text>Removal. Any officer of the Corporation may be removed from office at any time for any reason by a two-thirds (2/3) vote of all of the Directors.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>3.4</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|48|31:47"><form.text>President.</form.text></form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(a)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|48|31:47"><form.text>The President shall have general and active management of the affairs and property of the Corporation and shall see that all orders and resolutions of the Board are carried into effect. He or she shall preside at meetings of the Board. The President shall appoint a Director to preside over any meeting that he or she cannot attend.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(b)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|48|31:47"><form.text>The President may sign, with the other proper officer or agent of the Corporation authorized by the Board, any deeds, bonds, contracts or other instruments that the Board has authorized to be executed, and shall perform all duties incident to the office of President and such other duties as may be prescribed by the Board.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>3.5</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|48|31:47"><form.text>Vice-President. The Vice President shall have such duties as determined from time to time by the Board. The Vice-President shall discharge the duties of the President in the event of his or her absence or inability to act.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>3.6</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|48|31:47"><form.text>Secretary. The Secretary shall sign documents of the Corporation from time to time as required and shall see that minutes of the meetings of the Board are taken and maintained, see that notices are duly given in accordance with the provisions of these Bylaws or as required by law, and be custodian of the corporate records. The Secretary shall perform such other duties as may be assigned to the Secretary by the Board or President.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>3.7</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|48|31:47"><form.text>Treasurer. The Treasurer shall see that an adequate and accurate accounting system is maintained and ensure that financial reports are presented to the Board. The Treasurer shall also advise the Board on the handling of the Corporation&apos;s monies and investments and perform such additional duties as may be assigned to the Treasurer by the Board or the President.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit>
<form.vertical.space amt="1"/></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>4</designator><name>COMMITTEES OF THE BOARD OF DIRECTORS</name></name.block></head>
<form.vertical.space amt="1"/>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|48|31:47"><form.text>The Corporation may have an Executive Committee and such other committees as determined by the Board. If the Executive Committee is formed, it shall consist of at least three (3) Directors and be comprised of only Directors. The Executive Committee shall have and may exercise, when the Board is not in session and without specific delegation, all of the powers of the Board in the management of the affairs of the Corporation, except action with respect to election of officers or the filling of vacancies on the Board or on committees, the fixing of compensation of Directors for serving on the Board or on any committee, the amendment or repeal of the bylaws or the adoption of new bylaws, and the amendment or repeal of any resolution of the Board which by its terms shall not be so amendable or repealable.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|48|31:47"><form.text>Any other committee that does not consist entirely of Directors shall be chaired by a Director and include as many non-Director volunteers as the Board desires. Any other committee that does not consist entirely of Directors shall have only the authority delegated to it by the Board.</form.text></form.para>
<form.vertical.space amt="1"/></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>5</designator><name>CONTRACTS, CHECKS, DEPOSITS AND FUNDS</name></name.block></head>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>5.1</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|48|31:47"><form.text>Checks, Contracts. The Board is authorized to select such depositories as it shall deem proper for the funds of the Corporation and shall determine who shall be authorized on behalf of the Corporation to sign bills, notes, receipts, acceptances, endorsements, checks, releases, contracts and documents.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>5.2</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|48|31:47"><form.text>Books and Accounts. The Corporation shall keep or cause to be kept correct and complete books and records of account and also keep minutes of the proceedings of the Board and its committees. In addition, the Corporation shall cause to be filed the necessary reports, tax returns or other documents as may be required by law on its own behalf.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit>
<form.vertical.space amt="1"/></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>6</designator><name>INDEMNIFICATION</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|48|31:47"><form.text>The Corporation shall, to the fullest extent authorized by <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" artref="7">N.Y. Not-for-Profit Corporation Law Article 7</cite>, indemnify each Director and officer of the Corporation against reasonable expenses and against liability incurred by a Director or officer in a proceeding in which he or she was a party because he or she was a Director or officer of the Corporation. These indemnification rights shall not be deemed to exclude any other rights to which the Director or officer may otherwise be entitled. The Corporation shall indemnify any employee who is not a Director or officer of the Corporation, to the extent the employee has been successful on the merits or otherwise in defense of a proceeding, for all reasonable expenses incurred in the proceeding if the employee was a party because he or she was an employee of the Corporation. The Corporation may, to the fullest extent authorized by <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" artref="7">N.Y. Not-for-Profit Corporation Law Article 7</cite>, indemnify, reimburse, or advance expenses of Directors, officers, or employees.</form.text></form.para>
<form.vertical.space amt="1"/></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>7</designator><name>FISCAL YEAR AND TERM YEAR</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|48|31:47"><form.text>The fiscal year of the Corporation is <inline.instr>&lsqb;start date of fiscal year&rsqb;</inline.instr> through <inline.instr>&lsqb;end date of fiscal year&rsqb;</inline.instr>. The terms of the officers and Directors shall be the calendar year, unless otherwise determined by the Board.</form.text></form.para>
<form.vertical.space amt="1"/></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>8</designator><name>AMENDMENTS TO THE BYLAWS</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|48|31:47"><form.text>These Bylaws may be amended or repealed and new Bylaws may be adopted by the affirmative vote of two-thirds (2/3) of all of the Directors, provided that notice of the meeting is given stating the proposed amendment, repeal or new Bylaws to be considered.</form.text></form.para>
<form.vertical.space amt="1"/></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>9</designator><name>DISSOLUTION</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|48|31:47"><form.text>The Corporation shall be dissolved upon the affirmative vote of two-thirds (2/3) of all Directors of the Corporation. Upon dissolution, the assets shall be distributed in accordance with the Corporation&apos;s <inline.instr>&lsqb;Certificate of Incorporation/&lsqb;specification of other document&rsqb;&rsqb;</inline.instr>.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit>

</research.reference.block>
</note.block>

<section.body>
<form uuid="Ic7086aa0181b11e68c12afa7f3a24041">
<form.name.block><name>BYLAWS OF A NEW YORK NOT-FOR-PROFIT CORPORATION</name></form.name.block>
<form.unit>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>ONE</designator><name>OFFICES</name></name.block></head>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>1.1</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Principal Office.</form.text></form.para>
