<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>TWO</designator><name>MEMBERSHIP</name></name.block></head>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>2.1</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Classes of Membership.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>The corporation shall have one class of members, and no more than one membership may be held by any one person. The rights and privileges of all members shall be equal. Each member shall be entitled to one vote.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>2.2</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Qualifications.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>Any individual or organization that pays the dues as provided below and that agrees to be bound by the certificate of incorporation of this corporation, by these bylaws, and by such rules and regulations as the directors may, from time to time, adopt is eligible for membership in this corporation.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>2.3</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Admission to Membership.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>The directors shall, from time to time, prescribe the form and manner in which application may be made for membership.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>2.4</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Property Rights.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>No member shall have any right, title, or interest in any of the property or assets, including any earnings or investment income of this corporation, nor shall any of such property or assets be distributed to any member on its dissolution or winding up.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>2.5</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Liability of Members.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>No member of this corporation shall be personally liable for any of its debts, liabilities, or obligations, nor shall any member be subject to any assessment.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>2.6</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Transfer, Termination, and Reinstatement.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>Membership in this corporation is nontransferable. Membership shall terminate on the resignation or death of a member or on a member&apos;s failure to pay the dues required in these bylaws within <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of days&rsqb;</inline.instr> days of the due date. A member whose membership has been terminated may apply for reinstatement in the same manner as application is made for initial membership.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>THREE</designator><name>CERTIFICATES OF MEMBERSHIP</name></name.block></head>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>3.1</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Certificate of Membership.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>The Board of Directors may provide for the issuance of certificates evidencing membership in the corporation, which shall be of such form as may be determined by the Board. Such certificates shall be signed by the President or Vice President or by the Secretary or an Assistant Secretary and shall be sealed with the seal of the corporation. All certificates evidencing membership shall be consecutively numbered. The name and address of each member and the date of issuance of the certificate shall be entered on the records of the corporation. If any certificate shall become lost, mutilated, or destroyed, a new certificate may be issued to replace it on such terms and conditions as the Board of Directors may determine.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>3.2</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Issuance of Certificates.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>If the Board of Directors shall have provided for the issuance of certificates of membership under the provisions of Section 3.1 of this Article, then, when a person has been elected to membership and has paid any initiation fee and dues that may then be required, such a certificate shall be issued in the name of and delivered to the new member by the Secretary.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item>

<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>The Board of Directors may determine, from time to time, the amount of initiation fee, if any, and the amount of annual dues payable to the corporation by members.</form.text></form.para></form.item>

<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>Dues shall be payable in advance on the <inline.instr>&lsqb;ordinal number of day&rsqb;</inline.instr> day of <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of month&rsqb;</inline.instr> in each fiscal year. Dues of new members shall be prorated from the first day of the month in which such new member is elected to membership for the remainder of the fiscal year of the corporation and shall be payable, together with any initiation fee, at the time the new member is elected to membership.</form.text></form.para></form.item>

<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>FIVE</designator><name>MEETINGS OF MEMBERS</name></name.block></head>

<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>5.1</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Annual Meeting.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>An annual meeting of members shall be held at <inline.instr>&lsqb;time of annual meeting&rsqb;</inline.instr>, on the <inline.instr>&lsqb;ordinal number of day&rsqb;</inline.instr> day in <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of month&rsqb;</inline.instr> in each year, beginning with the year <inline.instr>&lsqb;identification of year&rsqb;</inline.instr>, at <inline.instr>&lsqb;place of annual meeting&rsqb;</inline.instr>, <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of city&rsqb;</inline.instr>, <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of county&rsqb;</inline.instr>, <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of state&rsqb;</inline.instr>, or at such other place or places as the Board of Directors may designate, from time to time, by resolution. Appropriate for consideration at such meetings shall be the election of directors and such other corporate business as may come before the meeting. If the day fixed for the annual meeting shall be a legal holiday in New York State, such meeting shall be held on the next succeeding business day. If the election of directors shall not be held on the day designated for an annual meeting or at any adjournment of such a meeting, the Board of Directors shall cause the election to be held at a special meeting of members conducted as soon as may be convenient.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>5.2</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Special Meetings.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>Special meetings of members may be called by the President, the Board of Directors, or not less than one-twentieth of such members as may be qualified to vote.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>5.3</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Place of Meeting.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>The Board of Directors may designate any place, either within or without New York State, as the place of meeting for any annual or special meeting of members. If no designation is made, the place of meeting shall be <inline.instr>&lsqb;place of meeting&rsqb;</inline.instr>, <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of city&rsqb;</inline.instr>, <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of county&rsqb;</inline.instr>, <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of state&rsqb;</inline.instr>. However, if all members shall meet at any time and place, either within or without New York State, and consent to the holding of a meeting, such meeting shall be valid without call or notice, and at such meeting any corporate action may be taken.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>5.4</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Notice of Meetings.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>Written or printed notice stating the place, day, and hour of any meeting of members shall be delivered, personally, by mail, or by facsimile telecommunications or by electronic mail, to each member entitled to vote at such meeting, not less than <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of days&rsqb;</inline.instr> nor more than <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of days&rsqb;</inline.instr> days before the date of such meeting, by or at the direction of the President, Secretary, or such officers or persons as are calling the meeting. In the case of special meetings or when required by these bylaws or bylaw, the purpose or purposes for which the meeting is called shall be stated in the notice. If sent by mail, a notice of meeting is given when deposited in the United States mail, postage prepaid, addressed to the member at the member&apos;s address as it appears on the records of the corporation at the time of mailing. If sent by facsimile telecommunication or mailed electronically, such notice is given when directed to the member&apos;s fax number or electronic mail address as it appears on the record of members, or, to such fax number or other electronic mail address as filed with the secretary of the corporation.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>5.5</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Informal Action by Members.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>Any action required or permitted to be taken at any meeting of members may be taken without such meeting if a consent in writing or electronic, setting forth the action to be taken, shall be signed or, if electronic, sent by electronic mail and set forth, or be submitted with, information from which it can reasonably be determined that the transmission was authorized, by all members entitled to vote with respect thereto.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>5.6</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Quorum.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>Members holding <inline.instr>&lsqb;percentage of total votes&rsqb;</inline.instr>&percnt; of the total votes which may be cast at any meeting shall constitute a quorum at such meeting. If a quorum is not present at any meeting of members, a majority of those present may adjourn the meeting, from time to time, without further notice.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>5.7</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Proxies.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>At any meeting of members, a member entitled to vote may vote by proxy executed in writing or authorized by electronic mail by the member or by the member&apos;s duly authorized attorney-in-fact. No proxy shall be valid after <inline.instr>&lsqb;specification of time period&rsqb;</inline.instr> from its date of execution unless otherwise provided in the proxy.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>5.8</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Voting by Mail.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>Where directors or officers are to be elected by members, such election may be conducted by mail in such manner as the Board of Directors shall determine.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>5.9</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Voting Rights.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>Each member shall be entitled to one vote. If an organization is a member, the organization shall designate one person who shall have the right to exercise the organization&apos;s voting rights.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>5.10</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Cumulative Voting.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>At any election for directors of this corporation, each and every member entitled to vote may cumulate that member&apos;s vote and give one candidate a number of votes equal to the number of directors to be elected, or each member may distribute that member&apos;s votes among as many candidates for director as the member thinks proper.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>The candidates for director receiving the highest number of votes up to the number of directors to be elected will be deemed to be elected.</form.text></form.para></form.item>

<form.item><name.block><designator>(b)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>Regular meetings shall be held <inline.instr>&lsqb;as soon as convenient after the first annual meeting of members/beginning with the month of &lsqb;name of month&rsqb; and &lsqb;identification of year&rsqb;, on the &lsqb;ordinal number of day&rsqb; of each month at &lsqb;time of meeting&rsqb;, unless such &lsqb;ordinal number of day&rsqb; falls on a legal holiday, in which case the meeting shall be held as may be prescribed by the board of directors&rsqb;</inline.instr>. <form.item><name.block><designator>(f)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>All meetings of the Board of Directors shall be governed by <ital>Robert&apos;s Rules of Order,</ital> including such revisions of those rules as may, from time to time, be published and, except as those rules are inconsistent with these bylaws, with the certificate of incorporation of this corporation or with applicable law.</form.text></form.para></form.item>

<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>6.8</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Action Without Meeting.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>No meeting need be held by the Board to take any action required or permitted to be taken by law, provided all members of the Board shall, individually or collectively, consent in writing or electronically to such action and such written consent or consents is filed with the minutes of the proceedings of the Board. Action by written consent shall have the same force and effect as action by unanimous vote of the directors. Any certificate or other document filed under any provision of law that relates to action so taken shall state that the action was taken by unanimous written consent of the Board of Directors without a meeting and that the <inline.instr>&lsqb;OPTIONAL: certificate of incorporation and&rsqb;</inline.instr> bylaws authorize the directors to so act. Such a statement shall be prima facie evidence of such authority.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>6.9</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Liability of Directors.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>The directors of this corporation shall not be personally liable for its debts, liabilities, or other obligations.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>SEVEN</designator><name>OFFICERS</name></name.block></head>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>7.1</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Designation of Officers.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>The officers of the corporation shall be a president, one or more vice presidents (as shall be determined by the Board of Directors), a secretary, a treasurer, and such other officers as may be elected in accordance with the provisions of this Article. The Board of Directors may elect or appoint such other officers, including one or more assistant secretaries and one or more assistant treasurers, as it shall deem desirable, such officers to have the authority and perform the duties prescribed, from time to time, by the Board of Directors. Any two or more offices may be held by the same person, except the offices of President and Secretary.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>7.2</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Election and Term of Office.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>The officers of this corporation shall be elected annually by the Board of Directors at the regular annual meeting of the Board of Directors. If the election of officers shall not be held at such meeting, such election shall be held as soon as may be convenient. New offices may be created and filled at any meeting of the Board. Each officer shall hold office until his or her successor shall have been duly elected and shall have been qualified.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>7.3</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Removal.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>Any officer elected or appointed by the Board of Directors may be removed by the Board of Directors whenever in its judgment the interests of the corporation would be best served. Any such removal shall be without prejudice to the contract rights, if any, of the officer so removed.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>7.4</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Vacancies.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>A vacancy in any office, whether due to death, resignation, removal, disqualification, or otherwise, may be filled by the Board of Directors for the unexpired portion of the term.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>7.5</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>President.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>The President shall be the chief executive officer of the corporation and shall exercise general supervision and control over all activities of the corporation. The President:</form.text></form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(a)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>Shall preside at all meetings of members and of directors;</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(b)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>May sign, with the Secretary or other officer duly authorized by the Board of Directors, any deeds, mortgages, bonds, contracts, or other instruments, the execution of which has been authorized by the Board of Directors, except in cases where the signing and execution or such instruments has been expressly delegated by the Board of Directors by these bylaws or to some other officer or agent of the corporation by law; and</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(c)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>Shall perform all other duties generally incident to the office of President and such other duties as may be prescribed by the Board of Directors.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>7.6</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Vice President.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>In the absence of the President or in the event of the President&apos;s inability or refusal to act, the <inline.instr>&lsqb;vice president/vice presidents in order of their election&rsqb;</inline.instr> shall perform the duties of the President and, when so acting, shall have all the powers of, and be subject to all the restrictions upon the President. Any vice president shall perform such additional duties as may, from time to time, be assigned to him by the President or by the Board of Directors.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>7.7</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Treasurer.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>If so required by the Board of Directors, the Treasurer shall:</form.text></form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(a)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>Give a bond for the faithful discharge of the Treasurer&apos;s duties in such sum and with such surety or sureties as the Board of Directors may deem appropriate;</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(b)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>Have charge and custody of, and be responsible for, all funds and securities of the corporation;</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(c)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>Receive and give receipts for moneys due and payable to the corporation from any source and deposit all such moneys in the name of the corporation in such banks, trust companies, or other depositaries as shall be selected by the Board of Directors; and</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(d)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>Perform all duties generally incidental to the office of Treasurer and such other duties as may, from time to time, be assigned to the Treasurer by the President or by the Board of Directors.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>7.8</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Secretary.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>The Secretary shall:</form.text></form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(a)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>Keep the minutes of meetings of members and of the Board of Directors in one or more books provided for that purpose;</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(b)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>See that all notices are duly given in accordance with these bylaws or as required by law;</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(c)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>Be custodian of the corporate records and of the seal of the corporation;</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(d)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>Keep a membership book containing the names and addresses of all members and directors of the corporation and, with respect to any membership that has been terminated, record that fact together with the date of termination; and</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(e)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>Exhibit to any director of the corporation, to a director&apos;s agent, or to any person or agency authorized by law to inspect them, at all reasonable times and on demand, these bylaws, the certificate of incorporation, the membership book, the minutes of any meeting, and the other records of the corporation.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>7.9</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Assistant Treasurers and Assistant Secretaries.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>The assistant treasurers and assistant secretaries, in general, shall perform such duties as may be assigned to them by the Board of Directors, the President, the Treasurer, or the Secretary of the corporation. If so required by the Board of Directors, the assistant treasurers shall give bonds for the faithful discharge of their duties in such sums and with such sureties as the Board of Directors may deem appropriate.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>EIGHT</designator><name>COMMITTEES</name></name.block></head>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>8.1</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Executive Committees.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>By majority vote of the directors in office, the Board of Directors may, by resolution duly adopted, establish one or more committees, each of which shall consist of three or more directors, which committees, to the extent provided by such resolution, shall have and exercise the authority of the Board of Directors in the management of the corporation, provided, however, that the designation of and delegation of authority to such committees shall not relieve the Board of Directors, or any director individually, of any responsibility imposed on the Board of Directors or any individual director by these bylaws or by law.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>8.2</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Finance Committee.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>The matter of controlling, managing, investing, and disposing of the property of this corporation for the purpose of earning an income, as distinguished from applying property and funds to charitable purposes, shall be exclusively vested in a finance committee, which shall consist of <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of directors&rsqb;</inline.instr> directors, <inline.instr>&lsqb;who shall be elected by majority vote of the board of directors/&lsqb;specification of other method of election&rsqb;&rsqb;</inline.instr>.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>8.3</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Other Committees.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>Other committees not having and exercising the managerial authority of the Board of Directors may be established by resolution duly adopted by majority vote of the Board of Directors. Except as may be provided by resolution, members of committees shall be members of the corporation and shall be appointed by the President. Any member may be removed by the President whenever, in the judgment of the President, the interests of the corporation would be best served by such removal.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>8.4</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Terms of Office.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>Each member of a committee shall continue as such until the next annual meeting of members of the corporation and until his or her successor is appointed, unless such committee shall be sooner abolished or unless such member be removed or cease to qualify as a member of the committee.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>8.5</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Chairperson.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>One member of each committee shall be appointed chairperson by the person or persons authorized to appoint the members of the committee.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>8.6</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Vacancies.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>Vacancies in the membership of any committee shall be filled by appointments made in the same manner as provided in the case of original appointments, and any member so elected shall be elected for the unexpired term of his predecessor.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>8.7</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Quorum.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>Unless otherwise provided in a committee&apos;s establishing resolution, a majority of the whole committee shall constitute a quorum, and the act of a majority of members present at a meeting at which a quorum is present shall be an act of the committee.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>8.8</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Rules.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>Each committee may adopt such rules and regulations for its meetings and the conduct of its activities as it may deem appropriate, provided, however, that such rules and regulations shall be consistent with these bylaws and provided further that regular minutes of all proceedings shall be kept.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>NINE</designator><name>CONTRACTS, CHECKS, DEPOSITS, AND FUNDS</name></name.block></head>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>9.1</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Contracts.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>The Board of Directors may, by resolution duly adopted, authorize any officer or officers, agent, or agents of the corporation, in addition to the officers so authorized by these bylaws, to enter into any contract or to execute and deliver any instrument in the name of and on behalf of the corporation. Such authority may be general or confined to specific instances.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>9.2</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Gifts and Contributions.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>The Board of Directors or an executive committee may:</form.text></form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(a)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>Accept on behalf of the corporation any contribution, gift, bequest, or devise of any type of property (&ldquo;donations&rdquo;) for the general and special charitable purposes of the corporation, on such terms as the Board or committee shall approve;</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(b)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>Hold such funds or property in the name of the corporation or of such nominee or nominees as the Board or committee may appoint;</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(c)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>Collect and receive the income from such funds or property;</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(d)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>Devote the principal or income from such donations to such benevolent and charitable purposes as the Board or committee may determine; and</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(e)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>Enter into an agreement with any donor to continue to devote the principal or income from the donation to such particular purpose as the donor may designate and after approval of such agreement by the Board or committee devote the principal or income from that donation according to the agreement.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>9.3</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Deposits.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>All funds of the corporation shall be deposited, from time to time, to the credit of the corporation in such banks, trust companies, or other depositaries as the Board of Directors may select.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>9.4</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Checks, Drafts, Orders for Payment.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>All checks, drafts, or orders for the payment of money, notes, or other evidences of indebtedness issued in the name of the corporation shall be signed by such officer or officers or agent or agents of the corporation and in such manner as the Board of Directors shall, from time to time, by resolution, determine. In the absence of such determination, the instruments shall be signed by the Treasurer or an assistant treasurer and countersigned by the President or a Vice President of the corporation.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>TEN</designator><name>MISCELLANEOUS</name></name.block></head>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>10.1</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Books and Records.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>The corporation shall prepare and maintain correct and complete books and records of account and shall also keep minutes of the meetings of its members, Board of Directors, and committees and shall keep at the registered or principal office a membership book giving the names and addresses of members entitled to vote. All books and records of the corporation may be inspected by any director, member, or the agent or attorney of either, or any proper person, at any reasonable time.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>10.2</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Fiscal Year.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>The fiscal year of the corporation shall begin on the first day of <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of month&rsqb;</inline.instr> and end on the last day of <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of month&rsqb;</inline.instr> in each year.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>10.3</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Corporate Seal.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>The Board of Directors shall provide a corporate seal described as follows: <inline.instr>&lsqb;description of corporate seal&rsqb;</inline.instr>.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>10.4</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Waiver of Notice.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>Whenever any notice is required to be given under the provisions of the N.Y. Not-for-Profit Corporation Law or under the provisions of the certificate of incorporation or the bylaws of this corporation, a waiver thereof in writing signed by the person or persons entitled to such notice, whether before or after the time stated therein, shall be deemed equivalent to the giving of such notice.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>ELEVEN</designator><name>AMENDMENTS</name></name.block></head>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>11.1</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Power of Members to Amend Bylaws.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>The bylaws of this corporation may be amended, repealed, or added to or new bylaws may be adopted <inline.instr>&lsqb;by the vote or written assent of &lsqb;a majority/&lsqb;percentage of members&rsqb;&percnt;&rsqb; of the members entitled to vote/by the vote of &lsqb;a majority/&lsqb;percentage of members constituting a quorum&rsqb;&percnt;&rsqb; at a meeting duly called for the purpose according to the certificate or bylaws&rsqb;</inline.instr>.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>11.2</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Power of Directors to Amend Bylaws.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><form.text>Subject to the limitations of the certificate of incorporation, these bylaws, and the N.Y. Not-for-Profit Corporation Law, concerning corporate action that must be authorized or approved by the members of the corporation, the bylaws of this corporation may be amended, repealed, or added to, or new bylaws may be adopted, by a resolution of the Board of Directors.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item></form.unit>
<note.block>
<note.group note.head="none">
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><para.text>Bylaws are the code or codes of rules adopted for the regulation or management of the affairs of the corporation irrespective of the name or names by which such rules are designated. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="102" subref="(a)" pararef="(2)">N-PCL &sect;102(a)(2)</cite>. The bylaws may be adopted by the incorporators at the organization meeting, or by the Board of Directors if the incorporators do not do so. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="602" subref="(a)">N-PCL &sect;602(a)</cite>. In drafting any bylaws for a charitable corporation, it should be remembered that the bylaws may contain any provision relating to the business of the corporation, the conduct of its affairs, its rights or powers, or the rights or powers of its members, directors, or officers, that are not inconsistent with statutory law or the certificate of incorporation. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="602" subref="(f)">N-PCL &sect;602(f)</cite>.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><para.text>This form is appropriate for use by any charitable corporation organized pursuant to the New York Not-for-Profit Corporation Law. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="101 et seq." secrange="y">N-PCL &dblsect;101 et seq.</cite> Included in these proposed bylaws are detailed provisions governing both membership in, and management of, the corporation. For example, provisions set forth the rights of membership and management, including detailed provisions governing the duties of corporate officers. Also, provision is made for formation of committees of directors to exercise authority delegated by the Board.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><para.text>It is customary to include in the articles of incorporation certain provisions to qualify an organization for tax-exempt status. Some of these provisions must be included in the articles. Inclusion of the mandatory provisions in the bylaws is not a substitute for inclusion in the basic foundation charter, whatever form it may take. On the other hand, it has become customary to include all these provisions in the bylaws, even though not required. This can be of particular importance for those matters not required to be included in the articles of organization, but which must nevertheless be covered. If they should be left out of the bylaws, problems could occur. In any event, the usual custom is to include all the mandatory tax provisions in the bylaws.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><para.text>For other matters that may be included in a corporation&apos;s bylaws, see Corporations <cite type="secondaryxref" secref="17:1 et seq." secrange="y">&dblsect;17:1 et seq.</cite> and Social and Recreation Nonprofit Organizations <cite type="secondaryxref" secref="30:1 et seq." secrange="y">&dblsect;30:1 et seq.</cite></para.text></para>
</note.group>

<reference.entry><ref.text><cite type="topic.key" normalpub="key" sub="Corporations and Business Organizations" numref="3384">West&apos;s Key Number Digest, Corporations and Business Organizations &key;3384</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
</research.reference.block>
<item.reference.block>
<item.reference><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>TWO.</designator></name.block>
<item.reference><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>2.1.</designator></name.block>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><para.text>Although these bylaws provide for only one class of members, a not-for-profit corporation is authorized to have more classes of members if so desired. Additionally, these bylaws provide that members are entitled to vote. As a consequence, the members must vote on any amendment to the certificate of incorporation. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="802" subref="(a)">N-PCL &sect;802(a)</cite>. They must also vote to authorize the sale, lease, exchange, mortgage, pledge, or other disposition of all or substantially all of the property and assets of the corporation. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="509">N-PCL &dblsect;509</cite>, <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="510">510</cite>.</para.text></para>
<research.reference.block>
<reference.entry><ref.text><cite type="secondary" normalpub="nyj2" topicname="Business Relationships" secref="823">N.Y. Jur. 2d, Business Relationships &sect;823</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
<reference.entry><ref.text><cite type="secondary" normalpub="nyj2" topicname="Business Relationships" secref="916">N.Y. Jur. 2d, Business Relationships &sect;916</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
</research.reference.block>
</item.reference></item.reference>
<item.reference><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>TWO.</designator></name.block>
<item.reference><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>2.2.</designator></name.block>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><para.text>Unless limited by the certificate of incorporation or bylaws, anyone may become a member of the corporation. See <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="601">N-PCL &sect;601</cite>.</para.text></para>
<research.reference.block>
<reference.entry><ref.text><cite type="secondary" normalpub="nyj2" topicname="Business Relationships" secref="823">N.Y. Jur. 2d, Business Relationships &sect;823</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
</research.reference.block>
</item.reference></item.reference>
<item.reference><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>TWO.</designator></name.block>
<item.reference><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>2.6.</designator></name.block>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><para.text>These bylaws provide that membership in the corporation is nontransferable. However, the certificate of incorporation or bylaws may provide for transfer of memberships. See <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="601" subref="(d)">N-PCL &sect;601(d)</cite>.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><para.text>Unless otherwise provided in the certificate of incorporation or bylaws, membership in a not-for-profit corporation shall by terminated by death, resignation, expulsion, expiration of a term of membership, or dissolution and liquidation under <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" artref="10">Articles 10</cite> and <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="11">11 of the Not-for-Profit Corporation Law</cite>. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="601" subref="(e)">N-PCL &sect;601(e)</cite>.</para.text></para>
<research.reference.block>
<reference.entry><ref.text><cite type="secondary" normalpub="nyj2" topicname="Business Relationships" secref="835">N.Y. Jur. 2d, Business Relationships &sect;835</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
</research.reference.block>
</item.reference></item.reference>
<item.reference><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>THREE.</designator></name.block>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><para.text>While these bylaws provide for the issuance of certificates of membership, it must be remembered that such certificates are not transferable and that a not-for-profit corporation is prohibited from having or issuing any shares of stock. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="501">N-PCL &dblsect;501</cite>, <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="601" subref="(c)">601(c)</cite>. Any certificate must state conspicuously that the corporation is a not-for-profit corporation. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="501">N-PCL &sect;501</cite>. No dividend may be paid and no part of its income may be distributed to its members, directors, or officers, except as authorized by statute. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="515">N-PCL &sect;515</cite>.</para.text></para>
</item.reference>
<item.reference><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>FIVE.</designator></name.block>
<item.reference><name.block><label>Sections</label><designator>5.1, 5.2, 5.3.</designator></name.block>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><para.text>These sections are declarative of New York law. First, in the absence of a specific provision for the place of meeting, all meetings must be held at the corporation&apos;s registered office. Next, failure to hold an annual meeting at the time and place designated in the bylaws will not work a forfeiture or dissolution of the corporation. Finally, the percentage of members necessary to call a special meeting may be specified in the bylaws or certificate of incorporation; in the event of a failure to specify such percentage, a special meeting may be called by members having 10&percnt; of the votes entitled to be cast. See <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="603">N-PCL &sect;603</cite>.</para.text></para>
<research.reference.block>

<item.reference><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>FIVE.</designator><name>Other Provisions.</name></name.block>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><para.text>The Not-for-Profit Corporation Law authorizes other provisions affecting members&apos; rights, including:</para.text></para>
</item.reference>
<item.reference><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>SIX.</designator></name.block>
<item.reference><name.block><label>Sections</label><designator>6.1, 6.2, 6.3.</designator></name.block>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><para.text>There must not be less than three members of the Board of Directors; however, the number of directors may be fixed by the bylaws and increased or decreased from time to time by amendment. See <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="702">N-PCL &sect;702</cite>. The term of office for a director, generally, cannot exceed five years. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="703" subref="(b)">N-PCL &sect;703(b)</cite>.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><para.text>New York law apparently places no restrictions on the qualifications necessary to serve on a Board of Directors; for example, directors need not be residents of the state or members of the corporation unless the certificate or bylaws so require. See <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="703">N-PCL &sect;703</cite>.</para.text></para>
<research.reference.block>

<item.reference><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>6.4(b)</designator></name.block>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><para.text>This provision is authorized by New York law. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="712">N-PCL &sect;712</cite>.</para.text></para>
</item.reference></item.reference>
<item.reference><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>SIX.</designator></name.block>
<item.reference><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>6.6.</designator></name.block>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><para.text>Although this provision denies compensation to the directors, reasonable compensation is authorized for services rendered. See <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="515">N-PCL &sect;515</cite>.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><para.text>This provision is suggested to avoid difficulties in establishing exemption from federal income taxation.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><para.text>For discussion of qualifying for tax exemption, see <cite type="secondaryxref" secref="31:9 et seq." secrange="y">&dblsect;31:9 et seq.</cite></para.text></para>
<research.reference.block>
<reference.entry><ref.text><cite type="secondary" normalpub="nyj2" topicname="Business Relationships" secref="789">N.Y. Jur. 2d, Business Relationships &sect;789</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
</research.reference.block>
</item.reference></item.reference>
<item.reference><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>SIX.</designator></name.block>
<item.reference><name.block><label>Section</label><designator>6.7.</designator></name.block>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><para.text>Unless otherwise provided in the certificate of incorporation or the bylaws, a majority of the entire board of directors constitutes a quorum, provided that the certificate of incorporation or the bylaws may fix the quorum at less than a majority of the entire board if, in the case of a board of 15 members or less, the quorum is at least one-third of the entire number of members, and, in the case of a board of more than 15 members, the quorum must be at least five members plus one additional member for every 10 members (or fraction thereof) in excess of 15. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="707">N-PCL &sect;707</cite>; <cite type="case">Desuzia v. Board of Directors of Concourse Village, Inc., 117 A.D.3d 426, 985 N.Y.S.2d 48 (1st Dep&apos;t 2014)</cite> stating that a supermajority quorum requirement may be imposed through corporate bylaws.</para.text></para>
<research.reference.block>
<reference.entry><ref.text><cite type="secondary" normalpub="nyj2" topicname="Business Relationships" secref="605">N.Y. Jur. 2d, Business Relationships &sect;605</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
</research.reference.block>
</item.reference></item.reference>

<item.reference><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>SEVEN.</designator></name.block>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><para.text>This article is declarative of New York law. See <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="713">N-PCL &sect;713</cite>. The removal of an officer without cause must be without prejudice to his or contract rights, if any. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="714">N-PCL &sect;714</cite>. Additionally, any two or more offices may be held by the same person, except the offices of President and Secretary. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="713" subref="(a)">N-PCL &sect;713(a)</cite>.</para.text></para>

</item.reference>
<item.reference><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>EIGHT.</designator></name.block>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><para.text>The creation of committees by the governing board of a not-for-profit corporation is authorized by <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="712">N.Y. Not-for-Profit Corp. Law &sect;712</cite>. Such committees may be composed of not less than three directors. Such statute places certain specified restrictions on the authority that may be delegated to such committees as does <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="509">N.Y. Not-for-Profit Corp. Law &dblsect;509</cite>, <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="510">510</cite>.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><para.text>Loans to corporate officers and directors are prohibited. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="716">N-PCL &sect;716</cite>. A loan made in violation of this section will be a violation of the duty to the corporation of the directors or officers authorizing it or participating in it, but the obligation of the borrower with respect to the loan will not be affected thereby.</para.text></para>
<research.reference.block>

<item.reference><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>ELEVEN.</designator></name.block>
<item.reference><name.block><label>Sections</label><designator>11.1, 11.2.</designator></name.block>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|49|31:48"><para.text>The rights of the members and board to amend the bylaws may be regulated by the certificate of incorporation or the bylaws. See <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="602">N-PCL &sect;602</cite>.</para.text></para>

<section>
<section.front>
<outline.name.block><label>&sect;</label><designator>31:49</designator><name>Bylaws<sep/>Nonprofit corporation<sep/>No members</name></outline.name.block>
<online.view>
<online.view.item>FMS</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>NFP</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>COL</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>FCV</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>FTR</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>EBL</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>TEM</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>MTD</online.view.item>
</online.view>
</section.front>
<section.body>
<form uuid="Ic708b8c0181b11e68c12afa7f3a24041">
<form.unit>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>I</designator><name>MEMBERS</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|50|31:49"><form.text>The Corporation shall have no members.</form.text></form.para>
<form.vertical.space amt="1"/></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>II</designator><name>DIRECTORS</name></name.block></head>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>1</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|50|31:49"><form.text>Number and Election of Directors. The Board of Directors (&ldquo;Board&rdquo;) shall consist of not less than three members, the exact number of which shall initially be three, but such number shall be subject to change from time to time by the Board. Each director shall be at least eighteen years of age. Except as provided in paragraph 2(c) of this Article, directors shall be elected by a majority of the votes cast at an Annual Meeting of the Board, and each director so elected shall hold office until the next Annual Meeting and until his or her successor is duly elected and qualified, or until his or her earlier resignation, removal or death.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>2</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|50|31:49"><form.text>Resignation; Removal; Vacancies.</form.text></form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(a)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|50|31:49"><form.text>A director may resign at any time by giving written notice to the Board or to an officer of the Corporation. Unless otherwise specified in the notice, the resignation shall take effect upon receipt thereof by the Board or such officer. Acceptance of such resignation shall not be necessary to make it effective.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(b)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|50|31:49"><form.text>Any or all of the directors may be removed by vote of the Board, with or without cause, provided there is a quorum of not less than a majority present at the meeting of the Board at which such action is taken.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(c)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|50|31:49"><form.text>Vacancies and newly created directorships resulting from any increase in the authorized number of directors may be filled by a majority of the directors then in office, though less than a quorum, and the directors so chosen shall hold office until the next annual election and until their successors are duly elected and qualified, or until their earlier resignation, removal or death.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>3</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|50|31:49"><form.text>Duties and Powers. The Board shall be the governing body of the Corporation. Accordingly, the business of the Corporation shall be managed by or under the direction of the Board and the Board shall have all such powers and authority to do all such lawful acts and things as are by statute or by the Certificate of Incorporation or by these Bylaws directed or required to be done in furtherance of the purposes of the Corporation.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>4</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|50|31:49"><form.text>Meetings. The Board may hold its Annual Meetings and its regular and special meetings either within or without the State of New York. The time and place for holding Annual Meetings and regular meetings of the Board shall be fixed from time to time by the Board. Such meetings of the Board may be held without notice. A special meeting of the Board may be called by the President, any other officer, or by any one director, upon written demand of not less than one-fifth of the entire Board. Notice thereof stating the place, date and hour of the meeting shall be given to each director either by mail not less than <inline.instr>&lsqb;text number of hours&rsqb;</inline.instr> (<inline.instr>&lsqb;number of hours&rsqb;</inline.instr>) hours before the date of the meeting, by telephone, facsimile transmission or e-mail on <inline.instr>&lsqb;text number of hours&rsqb;</inline.instr> (<inline.instr>&lsqb;number of hours&rsqb;</inline.instr>) hours&apos; notice, or on such shorter notice as the person or persons calling such meeting may deem necessary or appropriate in the circumstances. Notice of a meeting need not be given to any director who submits a signed or electronic waiver of notice whether before or after the meeting, or who attends the meeting without protesting, prior thereto or at its commencement, the lack of notice to such director.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>5</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|50|31:49"><form.text>Quorum. Except as may be otherwise specifically provided by law, the Certificate of Incorporation or these Bylaws, at all meetings of the Board a majority of the entire Board shall constitute a quorum for the transaction bf business and the act of a majority of the directors present at any meeting at which there is a quorum shall be the act of the Board. If a quorum shall not be present at any meeting of the Board, the directors present thereat may adjourn the meeting from time to time, without notice other than announcement at the meeting, until a quorum shall be present.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>6</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|50|31:49"><form.text>Action by the Board. Unless otherwise provided by the Certificate of Incorporation or these Bylaws, any action required or permitted to be taken at any meeting of the Board or of any committee thereof may be taken without a meeting if all the members of the Board or committee, as the case may be, consent to the adoption of a resolution authorizing the action. Such consent may be written or electronic. The resolution and written consents thereto by the members of the board or committee shall be filed with the minutes of the proceedings of the Board or committee.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>7</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|50|31:49"><form.text>Meetings by Means of Conference Telephone. Unless otherwise provided by the Certificate of Incorporation or these Bylaws, any one or more members of the Board or of any committee thereof who is not physically present at a meeting of the board or a committee may participate by means of a conference telephone or similar communications equipment or by electronic video screen communication. Participation by such means shall constitute presence in person at a meeting as long as all persons participating in the meeting can hear each other at the same time and each director can participate in all matters before the Board, including, without limitation, the ability to propose, object to, and vote upon a specific action to be taken by the board or committee.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>8</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|50|31:49"><form.text>Committees. The Board may, by resolution passed by a majority of the entire Board, designate from among its members an executive committee and other committees. Each committee so appointed shall consist of three or more directors and, to the extent provided in the resolution establishing it, shall have all the authority of the Board except as to the following matters:</form.text></form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(a)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|50|31:49"><form.text>the filling of vacancies in the Board or in any committee;</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(b)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|50|31:49"><form.text>the fixing of compensation of the directors for serving on the Board or any committee;</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(c)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|50|31:49"><form.text>the amendment or repeal of the Bylaws or the adoption of new Bylaws; and</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(d)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|50|31:49"><form.text>the amendment or repeal of any resolution of the Board which by its terms shall not be so amendable or repealable.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit>
<form.para><form.text>The President shall appoint the Chair of each committee. The Board may designate one or more directors as alternate members of any committee, who may replace any absent member or members at any meeting of such committee.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit>
<form.vertical.space amt="1"/></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>III</designator><name>OFFICERS</name></name.block></head>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>1</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|50|31:49"><form.text>General. The officers of the Corporation shall be chosen by the Board and shall be a President, a Secretary and a Treasurer. In addition, the Board may, from time to time, appoint such other officers, including without limitation, one or more Vice-Presidents, and confer upon such officers those powers and duties which the Board shall deem necessary or advisable for the conduct of the affairs of the Corporation. Any two or more offices may be held by the same person, except the offices of President and Secretary. The President shall be a member of the Board. The other officers may, but need not, be members of the Board.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>2</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|50|31:49"><form.text>Election. The Board at its Annual Meetings shall elect the officers of the Corporation who shall hold their offices for such terms and shall exercise such powers and perform such duties as are provided in these Bylaws or, to the extent not so provided, as shall be determined from time to time by the Board; and all officers of the Corporation shall hold office until their successors are elected or appointed and qualified, or until their earlier resignation, removal or death. Any officer elected by the Board may be removed at any time by the affirmative vote of a majority of the Board. Any vacancy occurring in any office of the Corporation shall be filled by the Board.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>3</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|50|31:49"><form.text>President. The President shall preside at all meetings of the Board. The President shall have general supervision over the affairs of the Corporation, and shall keep the Board fully informed about the activities of the Corporation. He or she shall have the power to sign and execute alone in the name of the Corporation all contracts authorized either generally or specifically by the Board, unless the Board shall specifically require an additional signature. The President shall perform all the duties incident to the office of the President, and shall perform such other duties as from time to time may be assigned by the Board.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>4</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|50|31:49"><form.text>Secretary. The secretary shall conduct the official correspondence, preserve all documents, books and communications, keep books of accounts, and maintain an accurate record of the proceedings of the corporation, the board of directors and all employees. At the expiration of his or her term of office he or she shall deliver to the board of directors the books, papers and other property of the corporation.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>5</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|50|31:49"><form.text>Treasurer. The Treasurer shall keep or cause to be kept full and accurate accounts of receipts and disbursements of the Corporation, and shall deposit or cause to be deposited all moneys, evidences of indebtedness and other valuable documents of the Corporation in the name of or to the credit of the Corporation in such banks or depositories as the Board may designate. At the annual meeting and whenever else required by the Board, he or she shall render a statement of the Corporation&apos;s accounts. He or she shall at all reasonable times exhibit the Corporation&apos;s books and accounts to any Officer or Director of the Corporation, and shall perform all duties incident to the position of Treasurer, subject to the control of the Board, and shall when required, give such security for the faithful performance of his or her duties as the Board may determine.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit>
<form.vertical.space amt="1"/></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>IV</designator><name>NOTICES</name></name.block></head>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>1</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|50|31:49"><form.text>Notices. Whenever written notice is required by law, the Certificate of Incorporation or these Bylaws, to be given to any director or member of a committee, such notice may be given by mail, addressed to such director or member of a committee, at his or her address as it appears on the records of the Corporation, with postage thereon prepaid, and such notice shall be deemed to be given at the time when the same shall be deposited in the United States mail. Written notice may also be given personally or by facsimile transmission or electronic mail, and such notice is given when directed to the director or member&apos;s fax number or electronic mail address as it appears on the records of the Corporation, or, to such fax number or other electronic mail address as filed with the Secretary of the Corporation.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>2</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|50|31:49"><form.text>Waivers of Notice. Whenever any notice is required by law, the Certificate of Incorporation or these Bylaws, to be given to any director or member of a committee, a waiver thereof in writing or electronic, signed or submitted by the person or persons entitled to said notice, whether before or after the time stated therein, shall be deemed equivalent thereto.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit>
<form.vertical.space amt="1"/></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>V</designator><name>GENERAL PROVISIONS</name></name.block></head>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>1</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|50|31:49"><form.text>Disbursements. All checks or demands for money and notes of the Corporation shall be signed by such officer or officers or such other person or persons as the Board may from time to time designate.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>2</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|50|31:49"><form.text>Fiscal Year. The fiscal year of the Corporation shall be fixed by resolution of the Board.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit>
<form.vertical.space amt="1"/></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>VI</designator><name>INDEMNIFICATION AND DIRECTORS&apos; LIABILITY</name></name.block></head>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>1</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|50|31:49"><form.text>Indemnification of Directors and Officers. To the fullest extent now or hereafter permitted by and in accordance with the standards and procedures provided for by <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="721 through 726" secrange="y">Sections 721 through 726 of the New York Not-for-Profit Corporation Law</cite> and any amendments thereto, the Corporation shall indemnify any person made or threatened to be made a party to any action, suit or proceeding, whether civil, criminal, administrative or investigative, by reason of the fact that he or she is or was a director or officer of the Corporation and may indemnify any person made or threatened to be made a party to any action, suit or proceeding, whether civil, criminal, administrative or investigative, by reason of the fact that he or she is or was an employee or agent of the Corporation, against judgments, fines, amounts paid in settlement and reasonable expenses, including attorney&apos;s fees. Without limiting the generality of the foregoing, the Corporation may provide for indemnification and advancement of reasonable expenses, including attorneys&apos; fees, actually and necessarily incurred by an indemnified person in connection with the defense of such action, or in connection with an appeal therein except in relation to matters as to which such director, officer, employee or agent is adjudged to have breached a duty to the Corporation under <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="717">Section 717 of the Not-for-Profit Corporation Law</cite>. Such indemnification may be authorized by resolution of the Board or by an agreement entered into with an individual director, officer employee or agent.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>2</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|50|31:49"><form.text>Limitation on Liability of Directors. The personal liability of each of the directors of the Corporation shall be limited to the fullest extent permitted by <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="720-a">Section 720-a of the Not-for-Profit Corporation Law</cite> as the same may be amended and supplemented.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit>
<form.vertical.space amt="1"/></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>VII</designator><name>AMENDMENTS</name></name.block></head>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>1</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|50|31:49"><form.text>These Bylaws may be altered, amended or repealed, in whole or in part, or new Bylaws may be adopted by the Board, provided, however, that notice of such alteration, amendment, repeal or adoption of new Bylaws be contained in the notice of such meeting of the Board. All such amendments must be approved by a majority of the entire Board then in office.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>2</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|50|31:49"><form.text>Entire Board. As used in this ARTICLE VII and in these Bylaws generally, the term &ldquo;entire Board&rdquo; means the total number of directors which the Corporation would have if there were no vacancies.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item></form.unit>
