<section.front>
<outline.name.block><label>&sect;</label><designator>31:50</designator><name>Bylaws<sep/>Charitable foundation for education scholarships</name></outline.name.block>
<online.view>
<online.view.item>FMS</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>COL</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>NFP</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>FCV</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>FTR</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>EBL</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>TEM</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>MTD</online.view.item>
</online.view>
</section.front>
<section.body>
<form uuid="Ic708dfd0181b11e68c12afa7f3a24041">
<form.unit>
<form.item><head><name.block><name>ARTICLE I.</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|51|31:50"><form.text>The corporation shall provide scholarships to accredited post-high school educational institutions for persons who are selected based on their leadership ability.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><name>ARTICLE II.</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|51|31:50"><form.text>No part of the net earnings of the corporation shall inure to the benefit of, or be distributable to, its members, directors, trustees, officers, or other private persons, except that the corporation shall be authorized and empowered to pay reasonable compensation for services rendered and to make payments and distributions in furtherance of the purpose set forth above. No substantial part of the activities of the corporation shall be the carrying on of propaganda or otherwise attempting to influence legislation, and the corporation shall not participate in or intervene in (including the publishing or distribution of statements) any political campaign on behalf of any candidate for public office. Notwithstanding any other provisions of these Articles, the corporation shall not carry on any other activities not permitted to be carried on: (a) by a corporation exempt from federal income tax under <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-irc" titleref="26" secref="501" subref="(c)" pararef="(3)" date="1986">Section 501(c)(3) of the Internal Revenue Code of 1986</cite>, as amended (or the corresponding provision of any future United States Internal Revenue law); or (b) by a corporation, contributions to which are deductible under <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-irc" titleref="26" secref="170" subref="(c)" pararef="(2)" date="1986">Section 170(c)(2) of the Internal Revenue Code of 1986</cite>, as amended (or the corresponding provision of any future United States Internal Revenue law).</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><name>ARTICLE III.</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|51|31:50"><form.text>Upon the dissolution of the corporation, the Board of Directors shall, after paying or making provision for the payment of all of the liabilities of the corporation, dispose of all of the assets of the corporation for the purpose of advancement of education or shall distribute such assets to the federal government or to a state or local government for such purpose. Any such assets not so disposed of shall be disposed of by the circuit court of the county in which the principal office of the corporation is then located, exclusively for the advancement of education.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><name>ARTICLE IV</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|51|31:50"><form.text>The corporation shall distribute its income for each taxable year at such time and in such manner as not to become subject to the tax on undistributed income imposed by <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-irc" titleref="26" secref="4942" date="1986">Section 4942 of the Internal Revenue Code of 1986</cite>, as amended (or the corresponding provision of any future United States Internal Revenue law).</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|51|31:50"><form.text>The corporation shall not engage in any act of self-dealing as defined in <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-irc" titleref="26" secref="4941" subref="(d)" date="1986">Section 4941(d) of the Internal Revenue Code of 1986</cite>, as amended (or the corresponding provision of any future United States Internal Revenue law).</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|51|31:50"><form.text>The corporation shall not retain any excess business holdings as defined in <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-irc" titleref="26" secref="4943" subref="(c)" date="1986">Section 4943(c) of the Internal Revenue Code of 1986</cite>, as amended (or the corresponding provision of any future United States Internal Revenue law).</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|51|31:50"><form.text>The corporation shall not make any investments in such manner as to subject it to tax under <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-irc" titleref="26" secref="4944" date="1986">Section 4944 of the Internal Revenue Code of 1986</cite>, as amended (or the corresponding provision of any future United States Internal Revenue law).</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|51|31:50"><form.text>The corporation shall not make any taxable expenditures as defined in <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-irc" titleref="26" secref="4945" subref="(d)" date="1986">Section 4945(d) of the Internal Revenue Code of 1986</cite>, as amended (or the corresponding provision of any future United States Internal Revenue law).</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit>
<note.block>
<note.group note.head="none">
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|51|31:50"><para.text>Bylaws are the code or codes of rules adopted for the regulation or management of the affairs of the corporation irrespective of the name or names by which such rules are designated. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="102" subref="(a)" pararef="(2)">N-PCL &sect;102(a)(2)</cite>.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|51|31:50"><para.text>The bylaws may be adopted by the incorporators at the organization meeting or by the board of directors if the incorporators do not do so. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="602" subref="(a)">N-PCL &sect;602(a)</cite>. In drafting any bylaws for a charitable corporation, it should be remembered that the bylaws may contain any provision relating to the business of the corporation, the conduct of its affairs, its rights or powers or the rights or powers of its members, directors, or officers, which are not inconsistent with statutory law or the certificate of incorporation. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="602" subref="(f)">N-PCL &sect;602(f)</cite>.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|51|31:50"><para.text>Note that <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="602">N-PCL &sect;602</cite> has been amended by L.2019, c. 558, &sect;2, eff. Jan. 24, 2020 that adds subsection (g) as follows:</para.text>
<quote.block>
<quote.para><para.text>(g) In the case of residential not-for-profit corporations, changes including the adoption, amendment or repeal of the by-laws by the board of directors shall be provided to the members, stockholders, and delegates of such corporation in writing, by physical or electronic means, within ten days of such adoption.</para.text></quote.para>
</quote.block></para>
</note.group>

<outline.name.block><label>&sect;</label><designator>31:51</designator><name>Bylaws<sep/>Provision<sep/>Automatic succession of vice president to presidency</name></outline.name.block>
<online.view>
<online.view.item>NFP</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>COL</online.view.item>

<online.view.item>TEM</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>MTD</online.view.item>
</online.view>
</section.front>
<section.body>
<form uuid="Ic70906e0181b11e68c12afa7f3a24041">
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>1</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|52|31:51"><form.text>In addition to his or her other rights and duties, the Vice President shall serve as President Elect and shall succeed to the office of President upon the expiration of the President&apos;s term of office.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>2</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|52|31:51"><form.text>The term of office of the Vice President is <inline.instr>&lsqb;identification of year&rsqb;</inline.instr> years, beginning on <inline.instr>&lsqb;begin date of term&rsqb;</inline.instr> and expiring on <inline.instr>&lsqb;end date of term&rsqb;</inline.instr>. At the expiration of this term, the Vice President shall succeed to the office of President and shall serve as President beginning on <inline.instr>&lsqb;begin date of term&rsqb;</inline.instr> and expiring on <inline.instr>&lsqb;end date of term&rsqb;</inline.instr>.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>3</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|52|31:51"><form.text>In the event of the resignation, removal, incapacity, lapse in membership, or death of the President while in office, the Vice President shall succeed to the office of President and serve as President both the remainder of the prior President&apos;s term and the full succeeding term of office as President.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>4</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|52|31:51"><form.text>In the event of the resignation, removal, incapacity, lapse in membership, or death of the Vice President, one or more successors shall be nominated by the Board of Directors and a special election for office of Vice President shall be conducted <inline.instr>&lsqb;within a stated number of days/within a reasonable time/as soon as practicable&rsqb;</inline.instr>. However, if the vacancy in the office of Vice President occurs less than <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of days&rsqb;</inline.instr> days before the scheduled expiration of the Vice President&apos;s term, a successor shall not be nominated or elected until the next scheduled election for officers.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>5</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|52|31:51"><form.text>A Vice President who resigns, is removed, becomes incapacitated, or fails to remain a member in good standing shall not succeed to the office of President.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit>

<section.front>
<outline.name.block><label>&sect;</label><designator>31:52</designator><name>Bylaws<sep/>Provision<sep/>Prohibition against sharing in charitable foundation earnings</name></outline.name.block>
<online.view>
<online.view.item>CLS</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>COL</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>NFP</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>FCV</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>FTR</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>TEM</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>MTD</online.view.item>
</online.view>
</section.front>
<section.body>
<form uuid="Ic7092df0181b11e68c12afa7f3a24041">
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|53|31:52"><form.text>No member, director, trustee, officer, or employee of, or member of a committee of, or person connected with, the charitable foundation or any other private individual shall receive at any time any of the net earnings or pecuniary profit from the operations of the charitable foundation, provided that this shall not prevent the payment to any such person of such reasonable compensation for services rendered to or for the charitable foundation in effecting any of its purposes as shall be fixed by the board of directors; in addition, no such person or persons shall be entitled to share in the distribution of any of the charitable foundation assets upon the dissolution of the charitable foundation.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|53|31:52"><form.text>All members of the corporation shall be deemed to have expressly consented and agreed that, upon such dissolution or winding up of the affairs of the charitable foundation, whether voluntary or involuntary, the assets of the charitable foundation, after all debts have been satisfied, then remaining in the hands of the board of directors shall be distributed, transferred, conveyed, delivered, and paid over for the purpose of advancement of education, or shall distribute such assets to the federal government or to a state or local government for such purpose. Any such assets not so disposed of shall be disposed of by the Supreme Court of the county in which the principal office of the charitable foundation is then located, exclusively for the advancement of education. The charitable foundation shall have the right to retain all or any part of any securities or property acquired by it in whatever manner and to invest and reinvest any funds held by it according to the judgment of the board of directors, without being restricted to the class of investments which a director is or may hereafter be permitted by law to make or any similar restriction, provided, however, that no action shall be taken by or on behalf of the charitable foundation if such action is a prohibited transaction or would result in the denial of the tax exemption under <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-irc" titleref="26" secref="503">Section 503</cite> or <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-irc" titleref="26" secref="507">Section 507 of the Internal Revenue Code</cite> and its regulations as they now exist or as they may hereafter be amended.</form.text></form.para>
<note.block>
<note.group note.head="none">
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|53|31:52"><para.text>Bylaws are the code or codes of rules adopted for the regulation or management of the affairs of the corporation irrespective of the name or names by which such rules are designated. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="102" subref="(a)" pararef="(2)">N-PCL &sect;102(a)(2)</cite>.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|53|31:52"><para.text>The bylaws may be adopted by the incorporators at the organization meeting or by the board of directors if the incorporators do not do so. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="602" subref="(a)">N-PCL &sect;602(a)</cite>. In drafting any bylaws for a charitable corporation, it should be remembered that the bylaws may contain any provision relating to the business of the corporation, the conduct of its affairs, its rights or powers or the rights or powers of its members, directors, or officers, which are not inconsistent with statutory law or the certificate of incorporation. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="602" subref="(f)">N-PCL &sect;602(f)</cite>.</para.text></para>
</note.group>

<section.front>
<outline.name.block><label>&sect;</label><designator>31:53</designator><name>Bylaws<sep/>Provision<sep/>Contracts, checks, deposits, and funds</name></outline.name.block>
<online.view>
<online.view.item>CLS</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>COL</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>NFP</online.view.item>

<online.view.item>FTR</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>TEM</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>MTD</online.view.item>
</online.view>
</section.front>
<section.body>
<form uuid="Ic7095500181b11e68c12afa7f3a24041">
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|54|31:53"><form.text><underscore>Contracts.</underscore> The board of directors may authorize any officer or officers, agent or agents of the charitable foundation, in addition to the officers so authorized by these bylaws to enter into any contract or execute and deliver any instrument in the name of and on behalf of the charitable foundation, and such authority may be general or confined to specific instances.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|54|31:53"><form.text><underscore>Checks, Drafts, Etc.</underscore> All checks, drafts, or other orders for the payment of money, notes, or other evidences of indebtedness issued in the name of the charitable foundation shall be signed by such officer or officers, agent, or agents of the charitable foundation and in such manner as shall, from time to time, be determined by resolution of the Board of Directors. In the absence of such determination by the board of directors, such instruments shall be signed by the Treasurer or an assistant Treasurer and countersigned by the President or a Vice President of the charitable foundation.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|54|31:53"><form.text><underscore>Deposits.</underscore> All funds of the charitable foundation shall be deposited, from time to time, to the credit of the corporation in such banks, trust companies, or other depositaries as the Board of Directors may select.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|54|31:53"><form.text><underscore>Gifts.</underscore> The Board of Directors may accept on behalf of the charitable foundation any contribution, gift, bequest, or devise for the general purposes or for any special purpose of the charitable foundation.</form.text></form.para>

<section.front>
<outline.name.block><label>&sect;</label><designator>31:54</designator><name>Bylaws<sep/>Provision<sep/>Board of directors</name></outline.name.block>
<online.view>
<online.view.item>CLS</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>COL</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>NFP</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>FCV</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>FTR</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>TEM</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>MTD</online.view.item>
</online.view>
</section.front>
<section.body>
<form uuid="Ic709a320181b11e68c12afa7f3a24041">
<form.name.block><name>BOARD OF DIRECTORS</name></form.name.block>
<form.unit>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>SECTION</label><designator>1</designator><name>General Powers</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|55|31:54"><form.text>The affairs of the corporation shall be managed by its board of directors.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>SECTION</label><designator>2</designator><name>Number, Tenure, and Qualifications</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|55|31:54"><form.text>The number of directors shall be three. Each director shall hold office until the next annual meeting of members and until his or her successors shall have been elected and qualified. Directors need not be residents of New York or members of the corporation. The number of directors may be decreased to not fewer than three or increased to any number from time to time by amendment of this section, unless the articles of incorporation provide that a change in the number of directors shall be made only by amendment of the articles of incorporation.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>SECTION</label><designator>3</designator><name>Regular Meetings</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|55|31:54"><form.text>A regular annual meeting of the board of directors shall be held without other notice than these bylaws, immediately after, and at the same place as, the annual meeting of members. The board of directors may provide by resolution the time and place for the holding of additional regular meetings of the board without other notice than such resolution.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>SECTION</label><designator>4</designator><name>Special Meetings</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|55|31:54"><form.text>Special meetings of the board of directors may be called by or at the request of the president or any two directors. The person or persons authorized to call special meetings of the board may fix any place as the place for holding any special meeting of the board called by them.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>SECTION</label><designator>5</designator><name>Notice</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|55|31:54"><form.text>Notice of any special meeting of the board of directors shall be given at least <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of days&rsqb;</inline.instr> days previously thereto by written notice to each director at his or her address as shown by the records of the corporation. If mailed, such notice is given when deposited in the United States mail in a sealed envelope so addressed, with postage thereon prepaid. If sent by facsimile telecommunication or mailed electronically, such notice is given when directed to the director&apos;s fax number or electronic mail address. Notice of any special meeting of the board of directors may be waived in writing signed by the person or persons entitled to the notice either before or after the time of the meeting. The attendance of a director at any meeting shall constitute a waiver of notice of such meeting, except where a director attends a meeting for the express purpose of objecting to the transaction of any business because the meeting is not lawfully called or convened. Neither the business to be transacted at, nor the purpose of, any regular or special meeting of the board need be specified in the notice or waiver of notice of such meeting, unless specifically required by law or by these bylaws.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>SECTION</label><designator>6</designator><name>Informal Action by Directors</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|55|31:54"><form.text>Any action required to be taken at a meeting of the directors of the corporation, or any other action which may be taken at a meeting of directors, may be taken without a meeting if a consent in writing or electronic, setting forth the action so taken, shall be signed by all of the directors entitled to vote with respect to the subject matter thereof.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>SECTION</label><designator>7</designator><name>Quorum</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|55|31:54"><form.text>A majority of the board of directors shall constitute a quorum for the transaction of business at any meeting of the board, provided that if less than a majority of the directors are present at said meeting, a majority of the directors present may adjourn the meeting to another time without further notice.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>SECTION</label><designator>8</designator><name>Manner of Acting</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|55|31:54"><form.text>The act of a majority of the directors present at a meeting at which a quorum is present shall be the act of the board of directors, unless the act of a greater number is required by statute, these bylaws, or the articles of incorporation.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>SECTION</label><designator>9</designator><name>Vacancies</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|55|31:54"><form.text>Any vacancy occurring in the board of directors or any directorship to be filled by reason of an increase in the number of directors shall be filled by the members unless the articles of incorporation, a statute, or these bylaws provide that a vacancy or a directorship so created shall be filled in some other manner, in which case such provision shall control. A director elected to fill a vacancy shall be elected for the unexpired term of his or her predecessor in office.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>SECTION</label><designator>10</designator><name>Compensation</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|55|31:54"><form.text>Directors shall not receive any stated salaries for their services, but by resolution of the board of directors a fixed sum and expenses of attendance, if any, may be allowed for each regular or special meeting of the board, provided that nothing herein contained shall be construed to preclude any director from serving the corporation in any other capacity and receiving reasonable compensation therefor.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit>
<note.block>
<research.reference.block>
<reference.entry><ref.text><cite type="topic.key" normalpub="key" sub="Corporations and Business Organizations" numref="3384">West&apos;s Key Number Digest, Corporations and Business Organizations &key;3384</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
</research.reference.block>
</note.block>

<outline.name.block><label>&sect;</label><designator>31:55</designator><name>Bylaws<sep/>Provision<sep/>Board of directors<sep/>Newly created directorships and vacancies</name></outline.name.block>
<online.view>
<online.view.item>CLS</online.view.item>

<section.body>
<form uuid="Ic709a321181b11e68c12afa7f3a24041">
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|56|31:55"><form.text>Newly created Directorships resulting from an increase in the number of Directors and vacancies occurring in the Board of Directors for any reason shall be filled by vote of a majority of Directors then in office, regardless of their number. Directors elected to fill newly created Directorships shall hold office in accordance with their classification (if Directors are classified) and until their successors have been elected and qualified. Directors elected to fill vacancies shall serve until the next annual meeting at which the election of Directors is in the regular order of business and until their successors are elected and have qualified.</form.text></form.para>

<section>
<section.front>
<outline.name.block><label>&sect;</label><designator>31:55.50</designator><name>Bylaws<sep/>Provision<sep/>Board of directors<sep/>Meetings</name></outline.name.block>
<online.view>
<online.view.item>FMS</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>FCV</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>FTR</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>COL</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>NFP</online.view.item>
</online.view>
</section.front>
<section.body>
<form>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>1</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Regular meetings of the board may be held on such dates and at such times and places as set by the secretary, subject to approval of the board. The annual meeting of the board must be held in <inline.instr>&lsqb;specification of time of year&rsqb;</inline.instr> of each year. A special meeting of the board may be called, and the date, time and place of the meeting will be set, by the board chair, the president, or any <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of directors&rsqb;</inline.instr> directors.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>2</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>The secretary must give to each director not less than <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of days&rsqb;</inline.instr> days&apos; written notice of the time and place of each annual and regular meeting of the board, and must give <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of days&rsqb;</inline.instr> days&apos; written notice of special meetings.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>3</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>At the annual meeting of the board, the president and the treasurer must present the annual financial report required by Section 519 of the New York Not-for-Profit Corporation Law or any successor statute. The report must be filed with the minutes of the annual meeting.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>4</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>A majority of the entire board will constitute a quorum for the transaction of business at meetings of the board. Except as required by law or these bylaws, all matters will be decided by a majority vote of the directors present at a meeting at which a quorum is present. In the absence of a quorum at the time and place set for a meeting of the board, the directors present may adjourn the meeting from time to time until a quorum is present.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>5</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Any one or more of the directors may participate in a meeting of the board by means of conference telephone, videoconference, or other communications equipment as long as all persons participating in the meeting can hear each other at the same time. Participation by such means will be deemed presence in person at the meeting.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>6</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Any action required or permitted to be taken by the board may be taken without a meeting, if all the directors consent to the adoption of a resolution authorizing the action. Consent may be written or electronic. If written, the consent must be executed by the director by signing such consent or causing his or her signature to be affixed to such consent by any reasonable means, including but not limited to facsimile signature. If electronic, the transmission of the consent must be sent by electronic mail and set forth or be submitted with information from which it can reasonably be determined that the transmission was authorized by the director. The resolution and the consents thereto shall be filed with the minutes of the board.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit>

<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|58|31:57"><form.text>Each director of the board of directors shall have one vote. Unless otherwise specified herein, the vote of the majority of the directors of the board of directors present at a meeting in which a quorum is present shall be the act of the board of directors. A majority of the number of directors of the board of directors then in office shall constitute a quorum for the transaction of business at any meeting of the board of directors, but if less than a quorum is present at a meeting, a majority of the directors of the board of directors present at such meeting may adjourn the meeting from time to time, without notice other than announcement at the meeting, until a quorum shall be present.</form.text></form.para>

To this end, the <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of foundation&rsqb;</inline.instr> Scholarship is designed to provide recognition for a deserving candidate and financial assistance for their initial year in college.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|63|31:61"><form.text>The educational grants provided by the foundation will be a one-time, nonrenewable, unrestricted stipend to be used by the recipient for costs associated with attending college (tuition, room, board, textbooks, etc).</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|63|31:61"><form.text>The purpose of the stipend is to provide positive recognition and assistance to a student entering college. The award will be a &dollar;<inline.instr>&lsqb;dollar amount of stipend&rsqb;</inline.instr> nonrenewable stipend for the student&apos;s first year only. <form.item><name.block><designator>4</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|64|31:62"><form.text>The merger shall become effective (the &ldquo;Effective Date&rdquo;) upon the filing of this Certificate of Merger by the Department of State of the State of New York, pursuant to <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="904" subref="(a)" pararef="(2)">Section 904(a)(2) of the Not-for-Profit Corporation Law</cite> of the State of New York.</form.text></form.para></form.item>

In that case, if the original submission was timely, the application will be considered timely filed.</para.text></para>

<note.block>
<note.group note.head="taxnotes">
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|70|31:68"><para.text>An organization seeking tax exemption under <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-code" titleref="26" secref="501" subref="(c)" pararef="(3)">26 U.S.C.A. &sect;501(c)(3)</cite>&mdash;charitable, religious, educational, etc. organizations&mdash;must notify the Internal Revenue Service that it considers itself exempt within 15 months of organization. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="exec-us-cfr" titleref="26" secref="1.508-1" subref="(a)" pararef="(2)">26 C.F.R. &sect;1.508-1(a)(2)</cite>. This requirement does not apply to churches, church organizations, or organizations (other than private foundations) with normal receipts of less than &dollar;5,000 a year. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-code" titleref="26" secref="508" subref="(c)">26 U.S.C.A. &sect;508(c)</cite>. The above form is a request that this 15-month period be extended and is allowed under the regulation cited. (See also <cite type="case">National Paralegal Inst. Coalition v. C.I.R., T.C. Memo. 2005-293, T.C.M. (RIA) P 2005-293 (2005)</cite>, where the Service reviews procedural aspects of filing Form 1023).</para.text></para>

<section.body>
<form uuid="Ic70c1420181b11e68c12afa7f3a24041">
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|71|31:69"><form.text>The annual return for <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of foundation&rsqb;</inline.instr> for the <inline.instr>&lsqb;fiscal/calendar&rsqb;</inline.instr> year ending <inline.instr>&lsqb;end date of year&rsqb;</inline.instr> is available for public inspection during regular business hours by any interested individual at the Foundation&apos;s principal office located at <inline.instr>&lsqb;office address of foundation&rsqb;</inline.instr>, <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of city&rsqb;</inline.instr>, <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of county&rsqb;</inline.instr>, <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of state&rsqb;</inline.instr>, <inline.instr>&lsqb;telephone number of foundation&rsqb;</inline.instr>, beginning on the date of this publication and continuing for 180 days thereafter.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|71|31:69"><form.text>Also available for inspection are the Foundation&apos;s application for determination of tax exemption and determination for the same by the Internal Revenue Service.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|71|31:69"><form.text>To request copies of the annual return and/or the exemption application, please direct your request to <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of officer 1&rsqb;</inline.instr>, <inline.instr>&lsqb;address of officer 1&rsqb;</inline.instr>, <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of city&rsqb;</inline.instr>, <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of county&rsqb;</inline.instr>, <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of state&rsqb;</inline.instr>. Inspection may also be made in person at the above address. To schedule an inspection, please call <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of officer 2&rsqb;</inline.instr> at <inline.instr>&lsqb;telephone number of officer 2&rsqb;</inline.instr>.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|71|31:69"><form.text>The principal manager of the Foundation is <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of principal manager&rsqb;</inline.instr>.</form.text></form.para>
<note.block>
<note.group note.head="taxnotes">
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|71|31:69"><para.text>In New York, <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-estpowerstrusts" secref="8-1.8">Section 8-1.8 of the N.Y. Estates, Powers &amp; Trusts Law</cite> and <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="406">Section 406 of the N.Y. Not-for-Profit Corporation Law</cite> require that private foundations publish notice of the availability of returns for inspection and that this notice be published no later than the last day for filing the return in question. The clerk of the county in which the private foundation&apos;s principal office is located designates in which newspaper in that county the publication must be made. The published notice is required to state that the foundation&apos;s annual return is available at its principal office for inspection during regular business hours by any citizen who requests it within 180 days after the date of publication. The notice must also state the address and telephone number of the foundation&apos;s principal office and the name of its principal manager.</para.text></para>
</note.group>

<image.block ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|76|31:74">

<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|76|31:74"><para.text>The above form, revised 9/08, is available from the New York State Department of Taxation and Finance, <cite type="url" normalpub="webref">http://www.tax.ny.gov</cite>, and is reprinted here for illustrative purposes.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|76|31:74"><para.text>Real property that is owned by a not-for-profit corporation organized for religious or educational purposes and used exclusively for carrying out such purposes is entitled to be exempt from real estate taxes. <cite type="case">Sisters of the Presentation of the Blessed Virgin Mary v. Van Wagenen, 223 A.D.3d 987, 202 N.Y.S.3d 814, 425 Ed. Law Rep. 950 (3d Dep&apos;t 2024), appeal dismissed, 41 N.Y.3d 990, 211 N.Y.S.3d 262, 234 N.E.3d 1054 (2024)</cite>.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|76|31:74"><para.text>A building was not property-tax exempt under the statutory provision allowing for a property-tax exemption for property that was owned by certain not-for-profit entities and that was used for certain not-for-profit purposes; the building owner was a not-for-profit healthcare fund that did not reside on the premises or otherwise itself use the building in whole or in part for its exempt fundraising purpose, and the owner&apos;s tenant was a for-profit corporation that had sole occupancy and used the building during the lease term exclusively to perform its for-charge dialysis services. <cite type="case">Brookdale Physicians&apos; Dialysis Associates, Inc. v. Department of Finance of City of New York, 41 N.Y.3d 608, 215 N.Y.S.3d 51, 239 N.E.3d 157 (2024)</cite>.</para.text></para>
</note.group>

<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|77|31:75"><para.text>A not-for-profit corporation that owned property that had previously qualified as exempt from real property taxes as being used for religious and educational purposes was entitled to continued exemption only for the portion of the property that was still being used for those purposes as a playground for students and areas that were incidental to such use; the remaining portion of the property containing a vacant and unused school and mansion that were not safe to use and had no running water, and thus no longer served to further the exempted purpose. <cite type="case">Sisters of the Presentation of the Blessed Virgin Mary v. Van Wagenen, 223 A.D.3d 987, 202 N.Y.S.3d 814, 425 Ed. Law Rep. 950 (3d Dep&apos;t 2024), appeal dismissed, 41 N.Y.3d 990, 211 N.Y.S.3d 262, 234 N.E.3d 1054 (2024)</cite>.</para.text></para>

<section>
<section.front>
<outline.name.block><label>&sect;</label><designator>31:77</designator><name>Conflict of interest policy for charitable organization</name></outline.name.block>
<online.view>
<online.view.item>FMS</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>COL</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>NFP</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>FCV</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>FTR</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>EBL</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>TEM</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>MTD</online.view.item>
</online.view>
</section.front>
<section.body>
<form uuid="Ic70d73b0181b11e68c12afa7f3a24041">
<form.name.block><name>CONFLICT OF INTEREST POLICY</name></form.name.block>
<form.unit>
<form.item><head><name.block><designator>I</designator><name>PURPOSE</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|79|31:77"><form.text>The purpose of this conflict of interest policy is to protect the interest of <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of charitable organization&rsqb;</inline.instr> (&ldquo;Organization&rdquo;) when it is contemplating entering into a transaction or arrangement that might benefit the private interest of an officer or director of the Organization or might result in a possible excess benefit transaction. This policy is intended to supplement, but not replace, any applicable state and federal laws governing conflict of interest applicable to nonprofit and charitable organizations such as the Organization.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><designator>II</designator><name>DEFINITIONS</name></name.block></head>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>1</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Interested Person</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|79|31:77"><form.text>Any director, principal officer, or member of a committee with governing board delegated powers, who has a direct or indirect financial interest, as defined below, is an interested person.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>2</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Financial Interest</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|79|31:77"><form.text>A person has a financial interest if the person has, directly or indirectly, through business, investment, or family:</form.text></form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>a</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|79|31:77"><form.text>An ownership or investment interest in any entity with which the Organization has a transaction or arrangement;</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>b</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|79|31:77"><form.text>A compensation arrangement with the Organization or with any entity or individual with which the Organization has a transaction or arrangement; or</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>c</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|79|31:77"><form.text>A potential ownership or investment interest in, or compensation arrangement with, any entity or individual with which the Organization is negotiating a transaction or arrangement.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|79|31:77"><form.text>Compensation includes direct and indirect remuneration as well as gifts or favors that are not insubstantial.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|79|31:77"><form.text>A financial interest is not necessarily a conflict of interest. Under Part III, Section 2 below, a person who has a financial interest may have a conflict of interest only if the appropriate governing board or committee decides that a conflict of interest exists.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><designator>III</designator><name>PROCEDURES</name></name.block></head>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>1</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Duty to Disclose</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|79|31:77"><form.text>In connection with any actual or possible conflict of interest, an interested person must disclose the existence of the financial interest and be given the opportunity to disclose all material facts to the directors and members of committees with governing board delegated powers considering the proposed transaction or arrangement.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>2</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Determining Whether a Conflict of Interest Exists</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|79|31:77"><form.text>After disclosure of the financial interest and all material facts and after any discussion with the interested person, he or she shall leave the governing board or committee meeting while the determination of a conflict of interest is discussed and voted upon. The remaining board or committee members shall decide if a conflict of interest exists.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>3</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Procedures for Addressing the Conflict of Interest</form.text></form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>a</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|79|31:77"><form.text>An interested person may make a presentation at the governing board or committee meeting, but after the presentation he or she shall leave the meeting during the discussion of and the vote on the transaction or arrangement involving the possible conflict of interest.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>b</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|79|31:77"><form.text>The chairperson of the governing board or committee shall, if appropriate, appoint a disinterested person or committee to investigate alternatives to the proposed transaction or arrangement.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>c</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|79|31:77"><form.text>After exercising due diligence, the governing board or committee shall determine whether the Organization can obtain, with reasonable efforts, a more advantageous transaction or arrangement from a person or entity that would not give rise to a conflict of interest.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>d</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|79|31:77"><form.text>If a more advantageous transaction or arrangement is not reasonably possible under circumstances not producing a conflict of interest, the governing board or committee shall determine by a majority vote of the disinterested directors whether the transaction or arrangement is in the Organization&apos;s best interest and for its own benefit and whether it is fair and reasonable. In conformity with the above determination, it shall make its decision as to whether to enter into the transaction or arrangement.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>4</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Violations of the Conflicts of Interest Policy</form.text></form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>a</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|79|31:77"><form.text>If the governing board or committee has reasonable cause to believe a member has failed to disclose actual or possible conflicts of interest, it shall inform the member of the basis for such belief and afford the member an opportunity to explain the alleged failure to disclose.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>b</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|79|31:77"><form.text>If, after hearing the member&apos;s response and after making further investigation as warranted by the circumstances, the governing board or committee determines the member has failed to disclose an actual or possible conflict of interest, it shall take appropriate disciplinary and corrective action.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item></form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><designator>IV</designator><name>RECORDS OF PROCEEDINGS</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|79|31:77"><form.text>The minutes of the governing board and all committees with board delegated powers shall contain:</form.text></form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>a</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|79|31:77"><form.text>The names of the persons who disclosed or otherwise were found to have a financial interest in connection with an actual or possible conflict of interest, the nature of the financial interest, any action taken to determine whether a conflict of interest was present, and the governing board&apos;s or committee&apos;s decision as to whether a conflict of interest in fact existed.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>b</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|79|31:77"><form.text>The names of the persons who were present for discussions and votes relating to the transaction or arrangement, the content of the discussion, including any alternatives to the proposed transaction or arrangement, and a record of any votes taken in connection with the proceedings.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><designator>V</designator><name>COMPENSATION</name></name.block></head>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>a</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|79|31:77"><form.text>A voting member of the governing board who receives compensation, directly or indirectly, from the Organization for services is precluded from voting on matters pertaining to that member&apos;s compensation.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>b</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|79|31:77"><form.text>A voting member of any committee whose jurisdiction includes compensation matters and who receives compensation, directly or indirectly, from the Organization for services is precluded from voting on matters pertaining to that member&apos;s compensation.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>c</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|79|31:77"><form.text>No voting member of the governing board or any committee whose jurisdiction includes compensation matters and who receives compensation, directly or indirectly, from the Organization, either individually or collectively, is prohibited from providing information to any committee regarding compensation.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><designator>VI</designator><name>ANNUAL STATEMENTS</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|79|31:77"><form.text>Each director, principal officer, and member of a committee with governing board delegated powers shall annually sign a statement which affirms such person:</form.text></form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>a</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|79|31:77"><form.text>Has received a copy of the conflict of interest policy;</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>b</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|79|31:77"><form.text>Has read and understands the policy;</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>c</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|79|31:77"><form.text>Has agreed to comply with the policy; and</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>d</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|79|31:77"><form.text>Understands the Organization is charitable and in order to maintain its federal tax exemption it must engage primarily in activities that accomplish one or more of its tax-exempt purposes.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><designator>VII</designator><name>PERIODIC REVIEWS</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|79|31:77"><form.text>To ensure the Organization operates in a manner consistent with charitable purposes and does not engage in activities that could jeopardize its tax-exempt status, periodic reviews shall be conducted. The periodic reviews shall, at a minimum, include the following subjects:</form.text></form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>a</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|79|31:77"><form.text>Whether compensation arrangements and benefits are reasonable, based on competent survey information, and the result of arm&apos;s length bargaining.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>b</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|79|31:77"><form.text>Whether partnerships, joint ventures, and arrangements with management organizations conform to the Organization&apos;s written policies; are properly recorded; reflect reasonable investment or payments for goods and services; further charitable purposes; and do not result in inurement, impermissible private benefit, or in an excess benefit transaction.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><designator>VIII</designator><name>USE OF OUTSIDE EXPERTS</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|79|31:77"><form.text>When conducting the periodic reviews as provided for in Part VII, the Organization may, but need not, use outside advisors. If outside experts are used, their use shall not relieve the governing board of its responsibility for ensuring periodic reviews are conducted.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|79|31:77"><form.text>Adopted by the Board of Directors: <inline.instr>&lsqb;date of adoption&rsqb;</inline.instr>.</form.text></form.para>
<note.block>
<note.group note.head="none">
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|79|31:77"><para.text>An &ldquo;excess benefit transaction&rdquo; is a transaction in which an economic benefit is provided by an exempt organization to a disqualified person in excess of the consideration received. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-code" titleref="26" secref="4958" subref="(c)" pararef="(1)">26 U.S.C.A. &sect;4958(c)(1)</cite>.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|79|31:77"><para.text>A &ldquo;disqualified person&rdquo; is someone who, during the five years preceding the transaction, was in a position to exercise substantial influence over the affairs of the organization. Disqualified persons also include family members and certain entities in which at least 35&percnt; of the control or beneficial interest are held by persons described in the preceding sentence. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-code" titleref="26" secref="4958" subref="(f)" pararef="(1)">26 U.S.C.A. &sect;4958(f)(1)</cite>.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|79|31:77"><para.text>Initially, the person receiving the benefit must pay a tax of 25&percnt; of the amount of the excess benefit. If not corrected within the prescribed period, the person must then pay a tax of 200&percnt; of the excess benefit. In addition, an organization manager who knowingly participates in the excess benefit transaction must pay a tax of 10&percnt; of the excess benefit. The maximum amount of this final tax is limited to &dollar;20,000. Persons liable for these taxes must file a Form 4720. See <cite type="lrre" normalpub="exec-us-cfr" titleref="26" secref="53.6011-1" subref="(b)">26 C.F.R. &sect;53.6011-1(b)</cite>.</para.text></para>
</note.group>
<research.reference.block>
<reference.entry><ref.text><cite type="topic.key" normalpub="key" sub="Internal Revenue" numref="4045 to 4079" numrange="y">West&apos;s Key Number Digest, Internal Revenue &key;4045 to 4079</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
<reference.entry><ref.text>Excise taxes on excess benefit transactions, <cite type="secondary" normalpub="ftc2" parmkref="D-6650 et seq." parmkrange="y">Federal Tax Coordinator 2d (RIA) &dblpara;D-6650 et seq.</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>
</research.reference.block>
</note.block>
</form>
</section.body>

<form uuid="Ic70d9ac0181b11e68c12afa7f3a24041">
<form.name.block><name>CONFLICT OF INTEREST ACKNOWLEDGMENT AND DISCLOSURE FORM</name></form.name.block>
<form.vertical.space amt="1"/>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|80|31:78"><form.text>I have read and received the conflict of interest policy set forth above and agree to comply fully with its terms and conditions at all times during my service as a <inline.instr>&lsqb;specification of role&rsqb;</inline.instr> of <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of organization&rsqb;</inline.instr>. If at any time following the submission of this form I become aware of any actual or potential conflicts of interest, or if the information provided below becomes inaccurate or incomplete, I will promptly notify the <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of organization&rsqb;</inline.instr> Board of Directors in writing.</form.text></form.para>
<form.vertical.space amt="1"/>
<form.line align="c">Statement of Actual or Potential Conflicts of Interest:</form.line>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|80|31:78"><form.text><inline.instr>&lsqb;Specification of conflict of interest&rsqb;</inline.instr>.</form.text></form.para>
<form.vertical.space amt="1"/>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|80|31:78"><form.text>I hereby certify that the information set forth above is true and complete to the best of my knowledge.</form.text></form.para>
