<section>
<section.front>
<outline.name.block><label>&sect;</label><designator>31:79</designator><name>Charitable foundation trust agreement</name></outline.name.block>
<online.view>
<online.view.item>FMS</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>NFP</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>COL</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>FCV</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>FTR</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>EPP</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>TAO</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>EBL</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>TEM</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>MTD</online.view.item>
</online.view>
</section.front>
<section.body>
<form uuid="Ic70e0ff0181b11e68c12afa7f3a24041">
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|81|31:79"><form.text>Agreement dated as of the day of <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of month&rsqb;</inline.instr> <inline.instr>&lsqb;identification of year&rsqb;</inline.instr>, between <inline.instr>&lsqb;names of donors&rsqb;</inline.instr> as Donors (hereinafter called the Donors), and <inline.instr>&lsqb;names of trustees&rsqb;</inline.instr>, as Trustees (hereinafter called the Trustees).</form.text></form.para>
<form.line align="c">WITNESSETH:</form.line>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|81|31:79"><form.text>That the Donors hereby assign, transfer, and set over unto the Trustees and their successors and assigns all the Donor&apos;s right, title, and interest in and to the property described in Schedule <inline.instr>&lsqb;designation of schedule&rsqb;</inline.instr> hereto annexed and made a part of this Agreement, receipt of which the Trustees hereby acknowledge, this Trust to be known as the <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of trust&rsqb;</inline.instr>.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|81|31:79"><form.text>Said property, together with any additions, is termed the &ldquo;trust estate&rdquo; and shall be held in trust upon the following terms.</form.text></form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>First:</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|81|31:79"><form.text>The Trustees may receive and accept property, whether real, personal, or mixed, by way of gift, bequest, or devise, from any person, firm, trust, or corporation, to be held, administered, and disposed of in accordance with and pursuant to the provisions of this Trust, but no gift, bequest, or devise of any such property shall be received and accepted if it is conditioned or limited in such manner as to require the disposition of the income or its principal to any person or organization other than a charitable organization or for other than charitable purposes within the meaning of such terms, as defined in ARTICLE SECOND of this Trust, or as shall, in the opinion of the Trustees, jeopardize the federal income tax exemption of this trust pursuant to <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-irc" titleref="26" secref="501" subref="(c)" pararef="(3)">Section 501(c)(3) of the Internal Revenue Code</cite> or the corresponding section of any future federal tax code.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>Second:</designator></name.block>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(A)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|81|31:79"><form.text>The principal and income of all property received and accepted by the Trustees to be administered under this Trust shall be held in trust by them, and the Trustees may make payments or distributions from income or principal, or both, to or for the use of such charitable organizations, within the meaning of that term as defined in Paragraph D hereof, in such amounts and for such charitable purposes of the Trust as the Trustees shall, from time to time, select and determine; in addition, the Trustees may make payments or distributions from income or principal, or both, directly for such charitable purposes, within the meaning of that term as defined in Paragraph E hereof, in such amounts as the Trustees shall, from time to time, select and determine without making use of any other charitable organization. The Trustees may also make payments or distributions of all or any part of the income or principal to states, territories, or possessions of the United States, any political subdivision of any of the foregoing, or to the United States or the District of Columbia but only for charitable purposes within the meaning of that term as defined in Paragraph E hereof. Income or principal derived from contributions by corporations shall be distributed by the Trustees for use solely within the United States or its possessions. No part of the net earnings of this Trust shall inure or be payable to or for the benefit of any private shareholder or individual, except that the Trustees may make distributions to individuals in furtherance of the charitable purposes set forth in this Paragraph, and no substantial part of the activities of this Trust shall be the carrying on of propaganda or otherwise attempting to influence legislation. No part of the activities of this Trust shall be the participation in or intervention in (including the publishing or distributing of statements) any political campaign on behalf of any candidate for public office.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(B)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|81|31:79"><form.text>The Trust shall continue forever unless the Trustees terminate it and distribute all of the principal and income, which action may be taken by the Trustees in their discretion at any time. On such termination, assets shall be distributed for one or more exempt purposes within the meaning of <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-irc" titleref="26" secref="501" subref="(c)" pararef="(3)">Section 501(c)(3) of the Internal Revenue Code</cite> or the corresponding section of any future federal tax code or shall be distributed to the federal government, or to a state or local government, for a public purpose.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(C)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|81|31:79"><form.text>The Donors authorize and empower the Trustees to form and organize a nonprofit corporation limited to the uses and purposes provided for in this Trust, such corporation to be organized under the laws of any state or under the laws of the United States as may be determined by the Trustees and such corporation, when organized, to have power to administer and control the affairs and property and to carry out the uses, objects, and purposes of this Trust. Upon the creation and organization of such corporation, the Trustees are authorized and empowered to convey, transfer, and deliver to such corporation all the property and assets to which this Trust may be or become entitled. The charter, bylaws, and other provisions for the organization and management of such corporation and its affairs and property shall be such as the Trustees shall determine, consistent with the provisions of this Paragraph C.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(D)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|81|31:79"><form.text>In this Trust and in any amendments to it, references to &ldquo;charitable organizations&rdquo; or &ldquo;charitable organization&rdquo; mean corporations, trusts, funds, foundations, or community chests organized and operated exclusively for charitable purposes, no part of the net earnings of which inures or is payable to or for the benefit of any private shareholder or individual and no substantial part of the activities of which is carrying on propaganda or otherwise attempting to influence legislation, and which do not participate in, or intervene in, (including the publishing or distributing of statements) any political campaign on behalf of or in opposition to any candidate for public office. It is intended that the organizations described in this Paragraph D shall be entitled to exemption from federal income tax under <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-irc" titleref="26" secref="501" subref="(c)" pararef="(3)">Section 501(c)(3) of the Internal Revenue Code</cite> or the corresponding section of any future federal tax code.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(E)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|81|31:79"><form.text>In this Trust and in any amendments to it, the term &ldquo;charitable purposes&rdquo; shall be limited to and shall include only religious, charitable, scientific, literary, or educational purposes, within the meaning of those terms as used in <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-irc" titleref="26" secref="501" subref="(c)" pararef="(3)">Section 501(c)(3) of the Internal Revenue Code</cite> or the corresponding section of any future federal tax code, but only such purposes as also constitute public charitable purposes under the law of trusts of the State of New York.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>Third</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|81|31:79"><form.text>This Trust may be amended at any time or times by written instrument or instruments signed and sealed by the Trustees and acknowledged by a majority of the Trustees, provided that no amendment shall authorize the Trustees to conduct the affairs of this Trust in any manner or for any purpose contrary to the provisions of <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-irc" titleref="26" secref="501" subref="(c)" pararef="(3)">Section 501(c)(3) of the Internal Revenue Code</cite> or the corresponding section of any future federal tax code. An amendment of the provisions of this ARTICLE THIRD (or any amendment to it) shall be valid only if and to the extent that such amendment further restricts the Trustees&apos; amending power. All instruments amending this Trust shall be noted upon or kept attached to the executed original of this Trust held by the Trustees.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>Fourth:</designator></name.block>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(A)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|81|31:79"><form.text>If <inline.instr>&lsqb;names of trustees&rsqb;</inline.instr> shall fail or cease to act as Trustees hereunder, then <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of trustee 1&rsqb;</inline.instr> shall become a Trustee hereunder. If <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of trustee 1&rsqb;</inline.instr> shall fail or cease to act as a Trustee hereunder, then <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of trustee 2&rsqb;</inline.instr> shall become a Trustee hereunder. Subject to the foregoing order of designation, any Trustee in office hereunder shall have the power to appoint an individual successor Trustee or a succession of individuals to succeed him or her and to serve as a Trustee hereunder if he or she shall fail or cease to act as a Trustee hereunder.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(B)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|81|31:79"><form.text>Any Trustee under this Trust may, by written instrument, signed and acknowledged, resign his or her office, provided, however, that a sole Trustee shall not be permitted to resign unless and until a successor is appointed.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(C)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|81|31:79"><form.text>A Trustee may appoint one or more additional Trustees. Appointments shall be made by the Trustee or Trustees for the time in office by written instruments signed and acknowledged. Any succeeding or additional Trustee shall, upon his or her acceptance of the office by written instrument signed and acknowledged, have the same powers, rights, and duties and the same title to the Trust estate jointly with the surviving or remaining Trustee or Trustees as if originally appointed.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(D)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|81|31:79"><form.text>Except as otherwise provided herein, if there shall be three or more Trustees, the decisions and acts of a majority of the Trustees shall be required to exercise the powers and discretions conferred upon the Trustees. Except as otherwise provided herein, if there shall be one or two Trustees at any time, a unanimous vote of the Trustees shall be and constitute an exercise of the Trust powers and discretions conferred upon the Trustees.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(E)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|81|31:79"><form.text>No Trustee shall be required to furnish any bond or surety. No Trustee shall be responsible or liable for the acts or omissions of any other Trustee or of any predecessor or of a custodian, agent, depositary, or counsel selected with reasonable care.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(F)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|81|31:79"><form.text>A Trustee may, by appropriate written instrument, delegate all or any part of his or her powers to another or others of the Trustees for such periods and subject to such conditions as such delegating Trustee may determine.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(G)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|81|31:79"><form.text>The Trustees serving under this Trust are authorized to pay to themselves amounts for reasonable expenses incurred and reasonable compensation for services rendered in the administration of this Trust, but in no event shall any Trustee who has made a contribution to this Trust receive any compensation thereafter.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>Fifth</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|81|31:79"><form.text>In extension and not in limitation of the common-law and statutory powers of Trustees and other powers granted in this Trust, the Trustees shall have the following discretionary powers:</form.text></form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(A)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|81|31:79"><form.text>To invest and reinvest the principal and income of the Trust in such property, real, personal, or mixed, and in such manner as they shall deem proper and, from time to time, to change investments as they shall deem advisable; to invest in or retain any stocks, shares, bonds, notes, obligations, or personal or real property (including without limitation any interests in or obligations of any corporation, association, business trust, investment trust, common Trust Fund, or investment company), although some or all of the property so acquired or retained is a kind or size which, but for this express authority, would not be considered proper and although all of the trust funds are invested in the securities of one company. No principal or income, however, shall be loaned, directly or indirectly, to any Trustee or to anyone else, corporate or otherwise, who has at any time made a contribution to this Trust nor to anyone except on the basis of an adequate interest charge and with adequate security.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(B)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|81|31:79"><form.text>To sell, lease, or exchange any personal, mixed, or real property at public auction or by private contract for such consideration and on such terms as to credit or otherwise and to make such contracts and enter into such undertakings relating to the Trust property, as they consider advisable, whether or not such leases or contracts may extend beyond the duration of the Trust.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(C)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|81|31:79"><form.text>To borrow money for such periods, at such rates of interest, and upon such terms as the Trustees consider advisable and, as security for such loans, to mortgage or pledge any real or personal property with or without power of sale; to acquire or hold any real or personal property, subject to any mortgage or pledge; and to assume any mortgage or pledge on or of property acquired or held by this Trust.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(D)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|81|31:79"><form.text>To execute and deliver deeds, assignments, transfers, mortgages, pledges, leases, covenants, contracts, promissory notes, releases, and other instruments, sealed or unsealed, incident to any transaction in which they engage.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(E)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|81|31:79"><form.text>To vote, to give proxies, to participate in the reorganization, merger, or consolidation of any concern or in the <inline.instr>&lsqb;description of article&rsqb;</inline.instr> sale, lease, disposition, or distribution of its assets; to join with other security holders in acting through a committee, depositary, voting trustees, or otherwise and, in this connection, to delegate authority to such committee, depositary, or trustees and to deposit securities with them or transfer securities to them; and to pay assessments levied on securities or to exercise subscription rights in respect of securities.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(F)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|81|31:79"><form.text>To employ a bank or trust company as custodian of any funds or securities and to delegate to it such powers as they deem appropriate; to hold Trust property without indication of fiduciary capacity but only in the name of a registered nominee, provided the Trust property is at all times identified as such on the books of the Trust; to keep any or all of the Trust property or funds in any place or places in the United States of America; to employ clerks, accountants, investment counsel, investment agents, and any special services and to pay the reasonable compensation and expense of all such services in addition to the compensation of the Trustees.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>Sixth:</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|81|31:79"><form.text>The Trustees&apos; powers are exercisable solely in a fiduciary capacity consistent with and in furtherance of the charitable purposes of this Trust as specified in ARTICLE SECOND and not otherwise.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>Seventh:</designator></name.block>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(A)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|81|31:79"><form.text>Any other provisions of this instrument notwithstanding, the Trustees shall distribute its income for each tax year at such time and in such manner so that it will not become subject to the tax on undistributed income imposed by <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-irc" titleref="26" secref="4942">Section 4942 of the Internal Revenue Code</cite> or corresponding provisions of any future federal tax laws.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(B)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|81|31:79"><form.text>Any other provisions of this instrument notwithstanding, the Trustees will not engage in any act of self-dealing as defined in <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-irc" titleref="26" secref="4941" subref="(d)">Section 4941(d) of the Internal Revenue Code</cite> or corresponding provisions of any future federal tax laws; nor retain any excess business holdings as defined in <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-irc" titleref="26" secref="4943" subref="(c)">Section 4943(c) of the Internal Revenue Code</cite> or corresponding provisions of any future federal tax laws; nor make any investments in a manner that would incur tax liability under <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-irc" titleref="26" secref="4944">Section 4944 of the Internal Revenue Code</cite> or corresponding provisions of any future federal tax laws; nor make any taxable expenditures as defined in <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-irc" titleref="26" secref="4945" subref="(d)">Section 4945(d) of the Internal Revenue Code</cite>, or corresponding provisions of any future federal tax laws.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>Eighth:</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|81|31:79"><form.text>In this Trust and in any amendment to it, references to &ldquo;Trustees&rdquo; mean the one or more Trustees, whether original or successor, for the time being in office.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>Ninth:</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|81|31:79"><form.text>Any person may rely on a copy, certified by a notary public, of the executed original of this Trust held by the Trustees and of any of the notations on it and writings attached to it, as fully as he or she might rely on the original documents themselves. Any such person may rely fully on any statements of fact certified by anyone who appears from such original documents or from such certified copy to be a Trustee under this Trust. No one dealing with the Trustees need inquire concerning the validity of anything the Trustees purport to do.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>Tenth:</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|81|31:79"><form.text>Except as the context shall otherwise plainly require, words in the masculine or feminine gender shall be deemed to include masculine, feminine, and neuter genders and words in the singular or plural number shall be deemed to include both singular and plural numbers.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>Eleventh:</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|81|31:79"><form.text>This Trust is to be governed in all respects by the laws of the State of New York.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|81|31:79"><form.text>In Witnesseth Whereof, the parties hereto have set their respective hands and seals as of the day and year first written.</form.text></form.para>

<note.block>
<note.group note.head="none">
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|81|31:79"><para.text>This agreement will create a private foundation under <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-irc" titleref="26" secref="509">Section 509 of the Internal Revenue Code</cite> with attendant excise taxes and reporting requirements resulting in additional administration expenses and restrictions. It is based in part on the suggested form found in <cite type="lrre" normalpub="exec-us-irs-pub" numref="557">IRS Pub. 557</cite>.</para.text></para>

<item.reference.block>
<item.reference><name.block><designator>Seventh.</designator></name.block>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|81|31:79"><para.text>If a disqualified person engages in self-dealing with a trust, that person is subject to a 10&percnt; tax that goes up to 200&percnt; if the self-dealing is not rectified. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-code" titleref="26" secref="4941">26 U.S.C.A. &sect;4941</cite>. A disqualified person is one or more of the following: (See <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-code" titleref="26" secref="4946" subref="(a)">26 U.S.C.A. &sect;4946(a)</cite>.)</para.text>
<list list.style="para">
<list.item><name.block><designator>1)</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|81|31:79"><para.text>a substantial contributor;</para.text></para></list.item>
<list.item><name.block><designator>2)</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|81|31:79"><para.text>a foundation manager;</para.text></para></list.item>
<list.item><name.block><designator>3)</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|81|31:79"><para.text>a person who owns more than 20&percnt; of a corporation, partnership, trust, or unincorporated enterprise which is itself a substantial contributor; and/or</para.text></para></list.item>
<list.item><name.block><designator>4)</designator></name.block><para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|81|31:79"><para.text>a member of the family of any individual of the first three categories.</para.text></para></list.item>
</list></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|81|31:79"><para.text>Self-dealing includes certain financial transactions, engaged in directly or indirectly by a &ldquo;disqualified person.&rdquo; See <cite type="lrre" normalpub="exec-us-cfr" titleref="26" secref="53.4941(d)-2">26 C.F.R. &sect;53.4941(d)-2</cite>.</para.text></para>

<section.body>
<form uuid="Ic70e5e10181b11e68c12afa7f3a24041">
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|82|31:80"><form.text>This Agreement, made this <inline.instr>&lsqb;date of agreement&rsqb;</inline.instr>, between <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of settlor&rsqb;</inline.instr>, a corporation organized under the laws of the State of New York (hereinafter called &ldquo;Settlor&rdquo;) party of the first part, and <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of corporate trustee&rsqb;</inline.instr>, a corporation organized under the laws of the State of New York (hereinafter called &ldquo;Corporate Trustee&rdquo;), and <inline.instr>&lsqb;names of trustees&rsqb;</inline.instr> (hereinafter called &ldquo;Individual Trustees&rdquo;) parties of the second part (hereinafter collectively called &ldquo;Trustees&rdquo;).</form.text></form.para>
<form.line align="c">WITNESSETH:</form.line>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|82|31:80"><form.text>Whereas the Settlor has supported and is desirous of continuing to discharge its duty to support worthy philanthropic causes in the communities in which it operates and which it serves and of contributing generally to the public welfare through the alleviation of human suffering; the advancement of science, education, and the cultural arts; and the promotion of our traditional way of life and is further desirous of establishing a systematic plan for the accomplishment of such purposes;</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|82|31:80"><form.text>Now, Therefore, the Settlor gives to the Trustees the sum of &dollar;<inline.instr>&lsqb;dollar amount of payment&rsqb;</inline.instr>, the receipt whereof is hereby acknowledged by the Trustees;</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|82|31:80"><form.text>To Have and to Hold the same and such monies and properties as may be added thereto by the Settlor or by any other corporations or persons (provided such additions are accepted by the Trustees) in trust for the uses and subject to the terms and conditions hereinafter set forth, as follows:</form.text></form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.item><head><name.block><designator>I</designator><name>NAME</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|82|31:80"><form.text>The Trust hereby created shall be known as the <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of foundation&rsqb;</inline.instr>.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><designator>II</designator><name>PURPOSES</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|82|31:80"><form.text>The earnings of the Trust Fund and so much of the principal as the Trustees, from time to time, shall deem appropriate shall be used (except to the extent necessary to defray administration expenses) exclusively for contributions to organizations, including governmental bodies, operated exclusively for religious, charitable, educational, veteran rehabilitation service, literary, or scientific purposes or for prevention of cruelty to children or animals, no substantial part of the activities of which is carrying on propaganda or otherwise attempting to influence legislation or the election of public officials, provided, however, that such contributions may be made only for use within the United States or its possessions and provided, also, that the organizations to which the contributions are made: (a) are exempt from taxation under the Internal Revenue Code of 1986; and (b) shall not be classified as a private foundation or private foundation charitable trust under the Internal Revenue Code of 1986, except that the restriction contained in this clause (b) shall not apply to operating private foundations as defined in <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-irc" titleref="26" secref="4942" subref="(j)" pararef="(3)" date="1986">Section 4942(j)(3) of the Internal Revenue Code of 1986</cite>. The Trust shall not engage in any activities that are unlawful under the laws of the United States of America, the State of New York, or any other state, district, territory, or possession of the United States where its activities or the activities of the Settlor are carried on, nor shall the Trust engage in any transaction described as &ldquo;prohibited&rdquo; by requirements of the Internal Revenue Code relating to the exemption of organizations from income and profits taxes or that would attract an excise tax or otherwise result in loss of tax exempt status under the Internal Revenue Code of 1986. In furtherance and not limitation of the restrictions and limitations herein set forth, the Trust shall never be operated for the purpose of carrying on a trade or business for profit, and no payment of principal or income shall ever be made to the Settlor (as such term is defined in ARTICLE IV(1) of this Agreement) or to any private shareholder of the Settlor, unless the shareholder be an organization entitled to receive contributions hereunder, or to any officer, director, or employee of the Settlor or to any Trustee of this Trust, except as a reasonable allowance for actual expenditures or services actually rendered as such Trustee, it being the intent that no part of the Trust Fund or the earnings thereof shall ever inure to the benefit of any private individuals within the meaning of the tax-exemption requirements of the laws of the United States, the State of New York, or any other state, district, territory, or possession of the United States that might have or claim jurisdiction over the Settlor or the Trust.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|82|31:80"><form.text>All references in this Agreement to provisions or requirements in the Internal Revenue Code of 1986 shall also include corresponding provisions in such Code as amended from time to time and in subsequent tax laws of the United States. The term &ldquo;excise tax&rdquo; as used in this Agreement shall not include the tax imposed by <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-irc" titleref="26" secref="4940" date="1986">Section 4940 of the Internal Revenue Code of 1986</cite>.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><designator>III</designator><name>PAYMENTS</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|82|31:80"><form.text>It shall be the function of the Individual Trustees to determine to whom and in what amounts and at what times and under what conditions contributions shall be made in furtherance of the purposes of the Trust. Accordingly, the Corporate Trustee shall make such disbursements of principal and income as may be directed from time to time by a majority of the Individual Trustees in writing, signed by them, and delivered to the Corporate Trustee, certifying that the disbursement is proper under ARTICLE II of this Agreement, and, upon making such disbursement, the Corporate Trustee shall be discharged from any liability concerning such disbursement.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><designator>IV</designator><name>POWERS OF TRUSTEE</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|82|31:80"><form.text>It shall be the function of the Corporate Trustee to receive and to hold in safekeeping all assets of the Trust or appropriate evidences of ownership thereof, to make all authorized disbursements from the Trust, to keep records of all receipts and disbursements by and from the Trust, and generally to administer the Trust fund. Accordingly, the Corporate Trustee is vested hereby with all appropriate powers (to be exercised upon the determination of a majority of the then acting Trustees, including among them the Corporate Trustee) granted by law to Trustees, including (but not by way of limitation) the following:</form.text></form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>1</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Investments.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|82|31:80"><form.text>To invest and reinvest the fund and keep the fund invested in such stocks, bonds, or other investments as the Corporate Trustee may deem suitable for the fund, whether or not the same are authorized, under the laws of the State of New York, for the investment of trust funds (but no part of the Trust Fund shall be invested in the shares or obligations of or loans to the Settlor). The Corporate Trustee in its discretion may keep such portion of the fund in cash balances as it may, from time to time, deem needful or appropriate, and it shall be without obligation to pay interest on any such cash balances. No investments shall be made hereunder that would attract an excise tax on account of such investments under the Internal Revenue Code of 1986. For the purposes of this paragraph 1 the term &ldquo;Settlor&rdquo; shall include any business organization, foreign or domestic: (a) with which the Settlor could file a consolidated return under the Internal Revenue Code of the United States if such entity were a domestic corporation; or (b) the stockholdings of which are attributed to Settlor under any provision of the Internal Revenue Code of 1986.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>2</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Sale.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|82|31:80"><form.text>To sell, exchange, convey, transfer, or otherwise dispose of any property held by it.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>3</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Owner.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|82|31:80"><form.text>To vote upon any stocks, bonds, or other securities; to give general or special proxies or powers of attorney with or without power of substitution; to exercise any conversion privileges, subscription rights, or other options and to make any payments incidental thereto; to consent to or otherwise participate in corporate reorganization or other changes affecting corporate securities; to delegate discretionary powers; to pay any assessments or charges in connection therewith; and generally to exercise any of the powers of an owner with respect to stocks, bonds, securities, or other property held in the Fund.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>4</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Execution of Instruments.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|82|31:80"><form.text>To make, execute, acknowledge, and deliver any and all documents of transfer and conveyance and any and all other instruments that may be necessary or appropriate to carry out the powers herein granted.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>5</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Registration.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|82|31:80"><form.text>To register any investment held in the fund in its own name or in the name of a nominee and to hold any investment in bearer form, but the records of the Trustee shall at all times show that all such investments are part of the fund.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>6</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Legal Counsel.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|82|31:80"><form.text>To employ suitable agents and counsel and pay their reasonable expenses and compensation; to prosecute, defend, settle, or compromise or submit to arbitration any claims, debts, or damages due to or from the Trust.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>7</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Borrow Money.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|82|31:80"><form.text>To borrow money (from itself or others, except the Settlor) in such amounts and upon such terms as it shall deem advisable to carry out the purposes of the Trust and to pledge any property for the repayment of any such loan.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><designator>V</designator><name>ACCOUNTS</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|82|31:80"><form.text>The Trustees shall annually render to the Settlor an account of their transactions and the Settlor may approve each such account by instrument in writing signed by the President, a Vice President, the Treasurer, or Secretary of the Settlor and delivered to the Corporate Trustee. If no objection to any such account shall be filed in writing with the Corporate Trustee within <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of days&rsqb;</inline.instr> days after delivery of the account to the Settlor, the Settlor shall be deemed to have approved the account. Upon approval by the Settlor, whether explicitly or by implication, as above, the Trustees shall be released and discharged with respect to all matters reported in the account as though the account had been settled in a court of competent jurisdiction. The Trustees nevertheless may at any time seek a judicial settlement of their accounts in the courts of the State of New York or may in the courts of the same state seek determination of a question of construction or otherwise ask for instruction, and, except as otherwise required by the laws of the State of New York, the only necessary parties to any such proceeding shall be the Settlor and the Trustees; the Trustees or the Corporate Trustee, however, at their or its election may name as parties in any such proceeding any other person, persons, or governmental authority.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><designator>VI</designator><name>GENERAL PROVISIONS</name></name.block></head>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>1</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Resignation of Trustee; Removal; Successor Trustee; Additional Trustees.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|82|31:80"><form.text>Any Trustee acting hereunder may resign at any time by giving written notice to the Settlor. The Settlor may remove any Trustee at any time. Upon the death, removal, or resignation of any Trustee, the Settlor shall appoint a successor Trustee by instrument in writing delivered to the then Corporate Trustee or successor Corporate Trustee, as the case may be, but, if at any time a vacancy shall exist among the Individual Trustees, the remaining Individual Trustees during such time shall have all of the powers herein granted to Individual Trustees. There shall always be a Corporate Trustee that shall be an organization authorized to act as such under the laws of the State of New York. Upon appointment of a successor Corporate Trustee, the predecessor Corporate Trustee shall deliver the Trust Fund to its successor after reserving such funds as it may deem necessary to pay all then existing proper charges against the Trust. Successor Trustees shall have the same powers as those conferred upon their class (that is, Corporate or Individual) by the terms of this Agreement. The Settlor may appoint an additional Trustee or additional Trustees at any time by instrument in writing delivered to the then Corporate Trustee or Successor Corporate Trustee, provided that notwithstanding anything contained in this ARTICLE VI(1), vacancy in the office of individual Trustee need not be filled.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>2</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Liability.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|82|31:80"><form.text>No Trustee shall be liable hereunder for the acts or omissions of any other Trustee or for any cause, save for its, his, or her own negligence or breach of trust. All persons dealing with the Trustees are released from inquiry into the authority of the Trustees and from seeing to the application of any money or other property paid or delivered to the Corporate Trustee.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>3</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Compensation.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|82|31:80"><form.text>The Corporate Trustee shall be paid such reasonable compensation as shall, from time to time, be agreed upon between the Settlor and the Corporate Trustee. The Individual Trustees shall serve without compensation. Both the Corporate and the Individual Trustees shall be entitled to reimbursement for their reasonable expenses incurred in the performance of their duties as Trustees. The compensation of the Corporate Trustee and all expenses of administration shall be a charge against the Trust Fund, unless paid by the Settlor.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>4</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Exculpatory Clause.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|82|31:80"><form.text>Any action by the Settlor pursuant to any of the provisions of this Agreement shall be evidenced by a resolution of its Board of Directors certified to the Trustees over the signature of its Secretary or Assistant Secretary under the Corporate seal. The Trustees severally shall be fully protected in acting upon any instrument in writing believed by them to be genuine and to be signed by the proper person or persons; they shall be under no duty to make any inquiry as to any statement contained in any such writing but may accept the same as conclusive evidence of the truth, completeness, and accuracy of the statements therein contained.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>5</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Additional Trustees.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|82|31:80"><form.text>Any additional or successor Trustee (including a Successor Corporate Trustee) may exercise all the power and authority vested in the original Trustees or the Original Corporate Trustee, as the case may be.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>6</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Bond.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|82|31:80"><form.text>No Trustee (individual or corporate, original or successor) shall be required to furnish any bond or undertaking or security for such Trustee&apos;s good behavior as such.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><designator>VII</designator><name>AMENDMENT AND REVOCATION</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|82|31:80"><form.text>It is intended that this shall be a permanent Trust. It may, nevertheless, be terminated or amended at any time by the Settlor, by instrument in writing, delivered to the Corporate Trustee, provided, however, that upon termination the principal of the Trust Fund and any income then undistributed shall be paid over to such organizations qualified under ARTICLE II hereof as the Individual Trustees, in their absolute discretion, shall deem appropriate to carry out the expressed purposes of this Agreement. If there shall, at any time, be no Corporate Trustee serving by reason of the Settlor&apos;s failure to appoint a successor within <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of days&rsqb;</inline.instr> days after the resignation or removal of a Corporate Trustee, then the acting Individual Trustees (or, if there are none, the Supreme Court of the State of New York) shall appoint a successor Corporate Trustee. If there shall be, at any time, no Individual Trustee serving by reason of the Settlor&apos;s failure to appoint successors, then the Corporate Trustee may, in its absolute discretion, consider the Trust terminated and make a similar distribution of principal and income of the Trust or, in its discretion, appoint two or more individual trustees. In no event shall any principal or income from this Trust revert to the Settlor, (as such term is defined in ARTICLE IV(1) of this Agreement), but any principal or income that would otherwise revert to the Settlor shall be distributed to the <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of fund&rsqb;</inline.instr>; nor shall any distribution or amendment be made that will affect, impair, or remove the restrictions on income or principal distributions or reverters contained in ARTICLE II or this ARTICLE VII or impair or destroy the tax-exempt status of this Trust or result in denying tax-exempt status to donations made to the Trust, to the extent allowed by the provisions of the Internal Revenue Code of 1986 and other applicable legislation and regulations; nor shall any amendments be made that will increase the obligations of the Trustees or deny compensation to the Corporate Trustee without their and its consent.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|82|31:80"><form.text>Notwithstanding anything to the contrary contained in this Agreement, all assets (whether principal or income) shall be distributed in such way upon occurrence of any event described in <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-irc" titleref="26" secref="507" date="1986">Section 507 of the Internal Revenue Code of 1986</cite> that neither such occurrence nor such distribution shall attract any tax under <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-irc" titleref="26" secref="507" date="1986">Section 507 of the Internal Revenue Code of 1986</cite>.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><designator>VIII</designator><name>SITUS</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|82|31:80"><form.text>This Agreement and the Trust hereby created shall be administered, construed, and enforced according to the laws of the State of New York. All donations to the Trust shall be deemed to take place in the State of New York.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><designator>IX</designator><name>COUNTERPARTS</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|82|31:80"><form.text>The Agreement has been executed in <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of original counterparts&rsqb;</inline.instr> counterparts, each of which shall be deemed to be the original, although the others shall not be produced.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|82|31:80"><form.text>In Witnesseth Whereof, this instrument has been executed at <inline.instr>&lsqb;place of execution&rsqb;</inline.instr>, as of the <inline.instr>&lsqb;date of agreement&rsqb;</inline.instr>, by <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of settlor&rsqb;</inline.instr>, <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of corporate trustee&rsqb;</inline.instr> and the Individual Trustees hereinabove named.</form.text></form.para>
<signature.block ref="manual">
<signature.group position="r">
<form.vertical.space amt="1"/>

</signature.group>
</signature.block>
<form.vertical.space amt="1"/>
<signature.block ref="manual">
<signature.group position="r">
<form.line align="l"><inline.instr>&lsqb;Name of corporate trustee&rsqb;</inline.instr></form.line>
<form.line align="l">By:</form.line>
<form.vertical.space amt="1"/>
<form.line align="l" lineover="y"><inline.instr>&lsqb;Name of president&rsqb;</inline.instr></form.line>
<form.line align="l">President</form.line>
<form.vertical.space amt="1"/>
<form.line align="l">Attested:</form.line>
<form.vertical.space amt="1"/>
<form.line align="l" lineover="y"><inline.instr>&lsqb;Name of secretary&rsqb;</inline.instr></form.line>
<form.line align="l">Secretary</form.line>
<form.vertical.space amt="1"/>
<form.vertical.space amt="1"/>
<form.line align="l" lineover="y"><inline.instr>&lsqb;Names of trustees&rsqb;</inline.instr></form.line>

</signature.group>
</signature.block>
<note.block>
<note.group note.head="none">
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|82|31:80"><para.text>This agreement will create a private foundation under <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-irc" titleref="26" secref="509">Section 509 of the Internal Revenue Code</cite> with attendant 2&percnt; excise tax and reporting requirements resulting in additional administration expenses and restrictions.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|82|31:80"><para.text>The transfer to a private foundation contemplated by this form may also affect the amount of the charitable deduction available to the Settlor: (1) if appreciated property is transferred by any Settlor, whether individual or corporate; or (2) if by an individual, when the maximum amount of the charitable deduction will be lower than in the case of a contribution not made to a private foundation.</para.text></para>

<section.body>
<form uuid="Ic70ed340181b11e68c12afa7f3a24041">
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>This Agreement made as of <inline.instr>&lsqb;date of agreement&rsqb;</inline.instr> by and between <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of settlor&rsqb;</inline.instr>, party of the first part (hereafter referred to as the &ldquo;Settlor&rdquo;), and <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of trustee&rsqb;</inline.instr>, party of the second part (hereinafter referred to as the &ldquo;Trustee&rdquo;).</form.text></form.para>
<form.line align="c">WITNESSETH:</form.line>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>WHEREAS, the Settlor intends to hereby create and establish a charitable trust for the exclusive purposes hereinafter set forth; and</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>WHEREAS, the Settlor intends to hereby provide that such charitable trust shall always exist and be operated for the exclusive purposes hereinafter set forth; and</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>WHEREAS, the Settlor intends to provide hereby that all donations to and all income of such charitable trust shall always be received, held, administered, and (to the extent applicable) distributed for the exclusive purposes hereinafter set forth;</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>NOW, THEREFORE, for the purpose of carrying out and giving effect to the above-stated intentions of the Settlor and also for the purpose of prescribing the terms and conditions upon which all donations to and all income of the charitable trust are to be held and administered and distributed for the exclusive purposes for which the charitable trust is created and for which the charitable trust is to be operated, and also for the purpose of defining the powers and duties of the Trustee, and also for such other purposes as may be required by law, the Settlor and the Trustee do hereby covenant and agree as follows:</form.text></form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>I</designator><name>CREATION OF THE TRUST</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>The Settlor hereby creates and establishes a charitable trust (hereinafter referred to as the &ldquo;Trust&rdquo;) for the exclusive purposes hereinafter set forth, and the Trustee hereby accepts the Trust and agrees to act as Trustee of and under the Trust in accordance with the terms and conditions hereinafter set forth.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>II</designator><name>NAME OF THE TRUST</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>The Trust hereby created and established shall be known and designated as <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of foundation&rsqb;</inline.instr>.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>III</designator><name>THE COMMITTEE</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>It is the intent of the Settlor to provide herein for a self-perpetuating Committee, which shall consist at all times of not less than <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of individuals&rsqb;</inline.instr> individuals.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>The original members of the Committee shall be <inline.instr>&lsqb;names of original members&rsqb;</inline.instr>.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>At any time and times during his or her lifetime, the Settlor shall have the right, without the consent of the other then members of the Committee: (1) to appoint a new member in addition to the other then members of the Committee; (2) to appoint a new member to fill any vacancy in the Committee; and (3) to discharge any member of the Committee.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>At any time and times, a majority of the then members of the Committee shall have the right: (1) to appoint a new member in addition to the other then members of the Committee; (2) to appoint a new member to fill any vacancy in the Committee; and (3) to discharge any member of the Committee. However, the Settlor must consent to any such appointment or discharge made during the lifetime of the Settlor.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>Regardless of the existence of any vacancy, the Committee may act as long as there shall be in office at least <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of members&rsqb;</inline.instr> members. If, at any time and for any reason or no reason, the Committee consists of less than <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of members&rsqb;</inline.instr> members for a period of <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of days&rsqb;</inline.instr> days, the Trustee shall appoint a new member or members to fill the vacancy or vacancies so that the Committee shall consist of <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of members&rsqb;</inline.instr> members, and such appointment or appointments by the Trustee may be made without the consent of either the Settlor or any other then member of the Committee, provided that the Trustee shall give the Settlor at least 45-days prior written notice of the intention to fill any vacancy among the Committee hereunder so as to enable the Settlor to make an appointment or appointments to raise the number of members of the Committee to <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of members&rsqb;</inline.instr> members. Upon the Settlor&apos;s appointment of new members pursuant to the preceding sentence, the Trustee&apos;s power to fill any vacancy prior to its notice to Settlor shall cease with respect to the vacancies existing prior to such written notice by the Trustee. The Trustee shall not make any appointments of new members during the Settlor&apos;s lifetime prior to the expiration of the 45-day period contemplated by the preceding sentence.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>If a member of the Committee is discharged under the prior provisions of this ARTICLE III, he or she shall not be entitled to ask for or receive any reason for his or her discharge or any prior notice of his or her discharge.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>The Committee shall have the specific powers hereinafter granted and shall also have all other powers necessary or advisable to carry out the functions contemplated for the Committee hereunder in discharging the purposes of the Trust.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>On all matters and questions, a decision of the majority of the then members of the Committee shall govern and control, except as otherwise expressly provided herein to the contrary.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>If any written instrument is required to be signed or if any action is required to be taken by or on behalf of the Committee, such written instrument may be signed and such action may be taken on behalf of the Committee by any person or persons authorized by all members of the Committee to sign such written instrument or to take such action on its behalf. Any such authorized person need not be a member of the Committee.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>No bond or other security shall be required of any member of the Committee. No fee or other compensation shall be paid to any member of the Committee for his or her services as such member.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>The Committee may use the name of <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of foundation committee&rsqb;</inline.instr> or any other name which the Committee may elect to use at any time or times.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>IV</designator><name>DONATIONS TO THE TRUST</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>Donations to the Trust may be made by the Settlor. Without undertaking any legal obligation thereby, it is the expressed intention of the Settlor to make such donations from time to time.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>Donations to the Trust may also be made by any person or party other than the Settlor, but expressly subject to the condition that the Trustee may refuse to accept as a donation from the Settlor or from any such other person or party any item of property of a type which the Trustee, in its sole and uncontrolled discretion, deems inadvisable or improper to accept.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>Each donation to the Trust shall be made by paying or transferring or otherwise delivering to the Trustee the item or items of property representing such donation.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>Any donation to the Trust may be in the form of cash, in the form of any type of check or any type of other instrument for the payment of money, or in the form of any type of security or other property.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>V</designator><name>THE TRUST FUND</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>Subject to the right of refusal conferred by ARTICLE IV, the Trustee shall receive each donation paid or transferred or otherwise delivered to the Trustee by the Settlor and by any person or party other than the Settlor.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>All such donations so received by the Trustee, together with all income therefrom and thereon, is hereinafter referred to as the &ldquo;Trust Fund.&rdquo;</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>The Trustee shall receive, hold, manage, and administer the Trust Fund for the exclusive purposes hereinafter set forth and in accordance with the terms and conditions hereinafter prescribed.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>VI</designator><name>EXCLUSIVE PURPOSES OF TRUST AND TRUST FUND</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>The Trust is created and shall exist and shall be operated exclusively for religious, charitable, scientific, literary, or educational purposes or for the prevention of cruelty to children or animals within the United States of America, and no part of the net earnings or principal of the Trust shall inure to the benefit of any contributor (including the Settlor) to the Trust Fund, member of the Committee or Trustee except that the Trustee shall be entitled to reasonable compensation as such; in addition, no part of the activities of the Trust shall consist of carrying on propaganda or otherwise attempting to influence legislation.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>The Trust Fund (other than such part as may be required to pay taxes and administration expenses) shall exist and shall be held, administered, and distributed exclusively for religious, charitable, scientific, literary, or educational purposes or for the prevention of cruelty to children or animals within the United States of America, and no part of the net earnings of the Trust Fund shall inure to the benefit of any contributor (including the Settlor) to the Trust Fund, member of the Committee or Trustee except that the Trustee shall be entitled to reasonable compensation as such, and no part of the activities of the Trust Fund shall consist of carrying on propaganda or otherwise attempting to influence legislation.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>It is the expressed intention of the Settlor that at all times the Trust and the Trust Fund shall be tax exempt and that at all times all donations to the Trust and Trust Fund shall be deductible from the taxable income of the donating party to the extent allowed by law.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>Neither the Trustee nor the Committee shall have any power or authority to take or omit any action or proceeding that would: (a) deprive the Trust or Trust Fund of tax exemption or otherwise constitute a prohibited transaction under the provisions of the Internal Revenue Code of 1986; (b) attract any excise tax under the Internal Revenue Code of 1986 (other than under Section 4940); or (c) result in any tax under <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-irc" titleref="26" secref="507" date="1986">Section 507 of the Internal Revenue Code of 1986</cite>. All reference to the Internal Revenue Code of 1986 or any section thereof shall be to such Code or section, as amended from time to time, or to corresponding internal revenue laws of the United States or corresponding provisions thereof.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>VII</designator><name>PAYMENTS FROM THE TRUST FUND</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>Except only as hereinafter expressly provided to the contrary, the Trustee shall make payments of and from the Trust Fund only upon and in accordance with the written directions of the Committee and only in such manner and at such times and in such amounts and to such persons or parties as may be specified in such written directions of the Committee, which directions shall comply with all the requirements of ARTICLE VII of this Agreement.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>VIII</designator><name>ADMINISTRATIVE POWERS</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>The Trustee shall have the following powers and authorities in the administration of the Trust Fund, to wit:</form.text></form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(1)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>To invest and reinvest the Trust Fund by way of purchase or subscription or exchange or otherwise in any securities or other property and to retain in the Trust Fund any securities or other property, without regard to the proportion that any one item or any one type of such securities or other property may bear to the total principal of the Trust Fund at any time, subject, however, always to the directions of ARTICLE VI of this Agreement.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(2)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>To sell for cash or on credit, convert, redeem, exchange, or otherwise dispose of any securities or other property at any time held by the Trustee.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(3)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>To exercise any conversion privilege and/or subscription right available in connection with any securities or other property held by it at any time.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(4)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>To consent to the reorganization, consolidation, merger, or readjustment of the finances of any corporation, company, or association any of the securities of which may be held by it; to consent to the sale, mortgage, pledge, or lease of the property of any corporation, company, or association any of the securities of which may be held by it; to do any act with reference to or in connection with any of the foregoing that it may deem to be necessary or advisable, including the exercise of options, the making of agreements or subscriptions, and the holding and retaining of any securities or other property that it may acquire as a result of any of the foregoing.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(5)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>To settle, compromise, or submit to arbitration any claims, debts, or damages due and owing to or from the Trust Fund and to commence or defend suits or legal proceedings and to represent the Trust in all suits and legal proceedings.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(6)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>To vote personally or by general or limited proxy any securities or other property held by it at any time and to exercise, personally or by general or limited power of attorney, any right appurtenant to any securities or other property held by it at any time.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(7)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>To keep in cash at any time and times any part or all of the Trust Fund without payment of any interest thereon.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(8)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>To employ suitable agents and counsel and to pay their reasonable expenses and compensation from the Trust Fund.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(9)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>To register any securities or other property held by it at any time in its own name or in the name of a nominee with or without the addition of words, indicating that such securities or other property are held in a fiduciary capacity except as may otherwise be required by law, and to hold in bearer form any securities or other property held by it at any time so that the same will pass by delivery.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>(10)</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>To make and execute and deliver, as Trustee, any and all instruments in writing necessary or proper for the accomplishment of any of the foregoing powers.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>IX</designator><name>DEFINITION OF SECURITIES OR OTHER PROPERTY</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>Wherever used in this Agreement, the words &ldquo;securities or other property&rdquo; are hereby defined to mean and refer to all types or classes of any real property, personal property, common stocks, preferred stocks, capital stocks, notes, bonds, debentures, mortgages, evidences of indebtedness, evidences of ownership, life insurance policies, endowment policies, and annuity policies, regardless of whether or not any of the same are of the character authorized as legal investments for a Trustee under any laws applicable to the Trust or Trust Fund or the Trustee.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>X</designator><name>ACCOUNTINGS OF TRUSTEE</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>From time to time, the Trustee shall render accounts of its transactions to the Committee, but the Trustee shall not be required to account more than once a year. The Committee may approve such accounts by an instrument in writing delivered to the Trustee. In the absence of the filing in writing with the Trustee by the Committee of exceptions or objections to any such account within <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of days&rsqb;</inline.instr> days after the date the same was rendered, the Committee shall be deemed to have approved such account. Upon the approval of any such account by the Committee, whether such approval be in writing or as set forth in the next preceding sentence, the Trustee shall be released and relieved and discharged with respect to all matters and things set forth in such account with the same force and effect as though such account had been settled by the decree of a court of competent jurisdiction. Except as otherwise provided by law, no person or party other than the Committee may require any such accounting by the Trustee.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>The Trustee may initiate at any time any action or proceedings for the settlement of its accounts or for the determination of any question of construction that may arise. In such event, except as otherwise provided by law, the only necessary parties to any such action or proceedings shall be the Committee, except that the Trustee, if it so elects, may name as parties any other person, party, or governmental authority.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>XI</designator><name>TRUST AND TRUST FUND IRREVOCABLE</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>This agreement and the Trust and the Trust Fund shall be and shall remain irrevocable, and the Settlor shall not have the right at any time to revoke this Agreement or the Trust Fund.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>XII</designator><name>AMENDMENTS TO TRUST</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>This Agreement may be amended at any time and times only: (a) by the Settlor during his or her lifetime; and (b) by the Committee after the death of the Settlor. However, no such amendment shall permit any part of the Trust Fund to be held or administered or distributed for any purposes other than the exclusive purposes set forth in ARTICLE VI hereof, and no such amendment shall effect or result in a revocation or termination of this Agreement or of the Trust, the Trust Fund, or any part thereof.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>An amendment shall be by a written instrument delivered to the Trustee and signed by the Settlor during his or her lifetime or by the survivor of him or her during his or her lifetime or by the Committee after the death of the Settlor. The signature of the Trustee shall not be required unless the amendment increases its duties or obligations or changes its compensation.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>XIII</designator><name>GOVERNING LAW</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>This Agreement and the Trust and Trust Fund shall be construed, regulated, and administered under the laws of the State of New York. All donations to the Trust shall be deemed to take place in the State of New York. The Trustee shall be liable to account only in the courts of the State of New York.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>XIV</designator><name>ADDITIONAL AND SUCCESSOR TRUSTEES</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>At any time and times, the Committee may appoint one or more individuals or corporation to act as Trustee or Trustees hereunder with and in addition to the then acting Trustee or Trustees, provided, however, that only one bank or trust company shall be acting as corporate Trustee hereunder at any one time.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>At any time and times, any Trustee then acting hereunder may resign or may be removed by the Committee, and any individual acting as Trustee hereunder shall automatically cease to be a Trustee upon the event of his or her death. If the resigning or removed or deceased Trustee is the sole Trustee then acting hereunder, the Committee is directed to appoint one or more individuals and/or corporations to act as successor Trustee or Trustees hereunder.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>Any Trustee who has resigned or who has been removed by the Committee shall transfer and deliver the Trust Fund or any part thereof in its possession to the then remaining Trustee or Trustees or, if none, to its successor Trustee or Trustees.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>There shall at all times be one corporate Trustee acting hereunder.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>The appointment of any additional Trustee or any successor Trustee and the resignation or removal of any Trustee shall be by an instrument in writing satisfactory to both such Trustee and the Committee.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>When more than one Trustee is acting hereunder, all such Trustees shall jointly have the same powers and duties as those conferred upon the original Trustee named in this Agreement, and, on all matters and questions, the decision of a majority of the then Trustees shall govern and control.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>When more than one Trustee is acting hereunder, the words &ldquo;Trustee&rdquo; and &ldquo;Trustees&rdquo; shall be read and interpreted in the plural so as to refer to all such Trustees.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>XV</designator><name>TRUSTEE BOND AND COMPENSATION</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>No bond or other security shall be required of any Trustee hereunder, whether original, additional, or successor, for the faithful performance of its or <inline.instr>&lsqb;his/her/their&rsqb;</inline.instr> duties in any jurisdiction.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>Any Corporate Trustee shall be paid such reasonable compensation as shall be agreed upon from time to time by the Committee and the Trustee. Such compensation and all expenses of administration, including counsel fees, shall be paid to and withdrawn by the Trustee from and out of the Trust Fund. No individual Trustee shall be entitled to any compensation as such.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>Subject to the provisions of ARTICLE VI, the Trustee shall charge against and withdraw and pay from the Trust Fund all real and personal property taxes, income taxes, and other taxes of any and all kinds levied or assessed under existing or future laws of the United States of America or any state or jurisdiction thereof upon or in respect to the Trust Fund or any securities or other property forming a part of the Trust Fund.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><label>ARTICLE</label><designator>XVI</designator><name>TRUSTEE LIABILITY</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>The Trustee shall not be liable hereunder for any matter or thing, except only for its own negligence or willful misconduct.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>This Agreement shall be executed in <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of original counterparts&rsqb;</inline.instr> counterparts, each one of which shall be deemed to be the original regardless of whether or not the others are produced.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><form.text>In Witnesseth Whereof the Settlor has affixed his or her hand and seal on or as of the day and year first above written, and the Trustee has caused these presents to be executed by its duly authorized officer or officers and its corporate seal to be hereunto affixed on or as of the day and year first above written.</form.text></form.para>
