<note.block>
<note.group note.head="none">
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><para.text>This agreement will create a private foundation under <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-irc" titleref="26" secref="509">Section 509 of the Internal Revenue Code</cite> with attendant 2&percnt; excise tax and reporting requirements resulting in additional administration expenses and restrictions.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|83|31:81"><para.text>The transfer to a private foundation contemplated by this form may also affect the amount of the charitable deduction available to the Settlor: (1) if appreciated property is transferred by any Settlor, whether individual or corporate; or (2) if by an individual, when the maximum amount of the charitable deduction will be lower than in the case of a contribution not made to a private foundation.</para.text></para>

<section.body>
<form uuid="Ic70efa50181b11e68c12afa7f3a24041">
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|84|31:82"><form.text>I, <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of donor&rsqb;</inline.instr>, residing at <inline.instr>&lsqb;address of donor&rsqb;</inline.instr>, <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of city&rsqb;</inline.instr>, <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of county&rsqb;</inline.instr>, State of New York, desire and intend to make a gift to <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of institution&rsqb;</inline.instr>, of <inline.instr>&lsqb;address of institution&rsqb;</inline.instr>, <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of city&rsqb;</inline.instr>, <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of county&rsqb;</inline.instr>, <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of state&rsqb;</inline.instr>. To that end, I hereby give to <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of institution&rsqb;</inline.instr>, <inline.instr>&lsqb;OPTIONAL: a New York corporation not-for-profit,&rsqb;</inline.instr> the sum of &dollar;<inline.instr>&lsqb;dollar amount of donation&rsqb;</inline.instr>, together with the property described as follows: <inline.instr>&lsqb;description of property&rsqb;</inline.instr>, to be invested, sold, or reinvested, alone or in combination with other funds of <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of institution&rsqb;</inline.instr> by the <inline.instr>&lsqb;title of proper officers&rsqb;</inline.instr> as they see fit. Income from this sum is to be used exclusively for <inline.instr>&lsqb;specification of purpose of usage&rsqb;</inline.instr>.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|84|31:82"><form.text>My personal check made out to the order of <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of institution&rsqb;</inline.instr> in the sum of &dollar;<inline.instr>&lsqb;dollar amount of check&rsqb;</inline.instr> is enclosed in payment of the cash portion of this gift. The balance of the gift, consisting of the above-mentioned property, will be delivered <inline.instr>&lsqb;specification of delivery manner&rsqb;</inline.instr> on <inline.instr>&lsqb;date of delivery&rsqb;</inline.instr>.</form.text></form.para>
<form.vertical.space amt="1"/>
<form.line align="l">Dated: <inline.instr>&lsqb;date of gift&rsqb;</inline.instr></form.line>
<signature.block ref="manual">
<signature.group position="r">
<form.vertical.space amt="1"/>
<form.line align="l" lineover="y"><inline.instr>&lsqb;Name of donor&rsqb;</inline.instr></form.line>
</signature.group>
</signature.block>
<note.block>
<note.group note.head="none">
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|84|31:82"><para.text>&ldquo;Endowment fund&rdquo; means an institutional fund or part thereof that, under the terms of a gift instrument, is not wholly expendable by the institution on a current basis. The term does not include assets that an institution may designate as an endowment fund for its own use, consistent with the terms of the applicable gift instrument. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="551" subref="(b)">N-PCL &sect;551(b)</cite>.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|84|31:82"><para.text>An institution, in managing and investing an institutional fund, must consider the purposes of the institution and the purposes of the institutional fund. In addition to complying with the duty of loyalty imposed by law other than this article, each person responsible for managing and investing an institutional fund must manage and invest the fund in good faith and with the care an ordinarily prudent person in a like position would exercise under similar circumstances. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" secref="552" subref="(a)">N-PCL &sect;552(a)</cite>. Therefore, while it may be unnecessary for the settlor to include additional language concerning duration of the fund in order to convey an intention that the gift be maintained as a permanent fund, the drafter may find it advisable to review the provisions of <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-notforprofitcorp" artref="5-A">Article 5-A of the Not-for-Profit Corporation Law</cite>, Prudent Management of Institutional Funds Act. Note that an endowment fund is, by definition, a permanent fund. <cite type="case">In re Huntingdon College, 22 Misc. 3d 1124(A), 880 N.Y.S.2d 224, 2009 N.Y. Slip Op. 50276(U), 2009 WL 416088 (Sur. Ct. 2009)</cite>.</para.text></para>
</note.group>
<research.reference.block>
<reference.entry><ref.text><cite type="topic.key" normalpub="key" sub="Charities" numref="6">West&apos;s Key Number Digest, Charities &key;6</cite></ref.text></reference.entry>

<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|93|31:89"><para.text>No person may act as a professional fundraiser or fundraising counsel before he or she has registered with the Attorney General or after the expiration or cancellation of such registration or any renewal of the registration. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-exec" secref="173" subref="(1)">Exec. Law &sect;173(1)</cite>.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|93|31:89"><para.text>Applications for registration and re-registration must be in writing, under oath, in the form prescribed by the Attorney General and must be accompanied by an annual fee in the sum of &dollar;800. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-exec" secref="173" subref="(1)">Exec. Law &sect;173(1)</cite>.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|93|31:89"><para.text>Registration or re-registration, when effected, shall be for a period of one year, expiring one year from the date of registration or re-registration, and may be renewed upon written application, under penalties for perjury, for additional one-year periods. Applications for registration and re-registration, when filed with the Attorney General, shall become public records of the Attorney General. If there is any material change in the information provided in any application for registration and re-registration, the applicant or registrant is required to notify the Attorney General in writing within 20 days of the change. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-exec" secref="173" subref="(1)">Exec. Law &sect;173(1)</cite>.</para.text></para>
<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|93|31:89"><para.text>For form of annual bond of professional fundraiser, see <cite type="secondaryxref" secref="31:90">&sect;31:90</cite>.</para.text></para>

<para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|94|31:90"><para.text>A professional fundraiser shall at the time of filing each application for registration or re-registration, file with, and have approved by, the Attorney General a bond. In said bond, the filer shall be the principal obligor, in the sum of &dollar;10,000, with one or more sureties whose liability in the aggregate as such sureties will at least equal the said sum. The bond which may be in the form of a rider to a larger blanket liability bond shall run to the Attorney General for the use of the state and to any person who may have a cause of action against the obligor of said bond for any malfeasance or misfeasance in the conduct of such solicitation. <cite type="lrre" normalpub="statute-us-ny-law-exec" secref="173" subref="(1)">Exec. <section.front>
<outline.name.block><label>&sect;</label><designator>31:96</designator><name>Contract to provide management services to charitable organization</name></outline.name.block>
<online.view>
<online.view.item>FMS</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>NFP</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>COL</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>FCV</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>FTR</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>CML</online.view.item>
<online.view.item>NUC</online.view.item>

<section.body>
<form uuid="Ic711b970181b11e68c12afa7f3a24041">
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|100|31:96"><form.text>Whereas <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of management firm&rsqb;</inline.instr> is a New York corporation that is experienced in and offers management services to charitable organizations;</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|100|31:96"><form.text>Whereas <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of nonprofit organization&rsqb;</inline.instr> is a nonprofit <inline.instr>&lsqb;association/corporation/&lsqb;type of entity&rsqb;&rsqb;</inline.instr> and is largely operated by volunteers;</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|100|31:96"><form.text>Therefore, in consideration of the mutual promises contained in this agreement and other good and valuable consideration, the adequacy and receipt of which are hereby acknowledged, <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of nonprofit organization&rsqb;</inline.instr> and <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of management firm&rsqb;</inline.instr> hereby agree as follows:</form.text></form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>1</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Term.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|100|31:96"><form.text>This agreement shall be for term of <inline.instr>&lsqb;&lsqb;number of years&rsqb; years/&lsqb;number of months&rsqb; months&rsqb;</inline.instr> from the date hereof and shall be automatically renewed for successive additional periods of <inline.instr>&lsqb;&lsqb;number of years&rsqb; years/&lsqb;number of months&rsqb; months&rsqb;</inline.instr> each unless earlier terminated as provided for in this agreement.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>2</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Services to Be Provided.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|100|31:96"><form.text>During the term of this agreement, <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of management firm&rsqb;</inline.instr> shall manage the affairs of <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of nonprofit organization&rsqb;</inline.instr>, furnishing to <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of nonprofit organization&rsqb;</inline.instr> the specific services, facilities, and personnel set forth in Exhibit <inline.instr>&lsqb;designation of exhibit&rsqb;</inline.instr> to this agreement, as it may be revised by mutual agreement from time to time.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>3</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Fees and Expenses.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|100|31:96"><form.text><inline.instr>&lsqb;Name of nonprofit organization&rsqb;</inline.instr> agrees to pay <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of management firm&rsqb;</inline.instr> in consideration of the services to be furnished by <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of management firm&rsqb;</inline.instr>, set forth in Exhibit <inline.instr>&lsqb;designation of exhibit&rsqb;</inline.instr> attached this agreement, the fees specified in Exhibit <inline.instr>&lsqb;designation of exhibit&rsqb;</inline.instr> attached to this agreement, as it may be revised by mutual agreement from time to time. <inline.instr>&lsqb;Name of nonprofit organization&rsqb;</inline.instr> agrees to pay monthly fees due to <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of management firm&rsqb;</inline.instr> on or before the first of every month. Costs and expenses incurred by <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of management firm&rsqb;</inline.instr> on behalf of <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of nonprofit organization&rsqb;</inline.instr> shall be promptly reimbursed to <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of management firm&rsqb;</inline.instr> by <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of nonprofit organization&rsqb;</inline.instr>. Fee or expense reimbursement amounts not paid by <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of nonprofit organization&rsqb;</inline.instr> to <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of management firm&rsqb;</inline.instr> when due pursuant to this agreement shall accrue interest at a per annum rate of over the prime rate of interest as provided in the <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of reporting source&rsqb;</inline.instr>, or the maximum amount of interest allowable by law, whichever is less, from the due date until the date of payment.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>4</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Charity&apos;s Responsibilities.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|100|31:96"><form.text><inline.instr>&lsqb;Name of nonprofit organization&rsqb;</inline.instr> will be responsible for directing the activities of its Board and its committees and insuring that they made agreed-upon deadlines, travel and meeting commitments, and specific duties. The signature of the President of <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of nonprofit organization&rsqb;</inline.instr> is required for all legal documents such as bank cards, tax forms, and hotel contracts. <inline.instr>&lsqb;Name of nonprofit organization&rsqb;</inline.instr> will be responsible for payment of the management fee and all reasonable, direct, out-of-pocket (line-item) expenses, such as telephone, postage, printing, typesetting, mailing labor, travel, or other outside services related to day-to-day operation of the enterprise.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|100|31:96"><form.text>Any problems that arise between a <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of nonprofit organization&rsqb;</inline.instr> member, exhibitor, speaker, or any other individual regarding an issue that is not easily resolved should be referred to the President of <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of nonprofit organization&rsqb;</inline.instr>, who will mediate or refer to the proper Board member of <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of nonprofit organization&rsqb;</inline.instr> for action.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>5</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Independent Contractor.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|100|31:96"><form.text>In carrying out its responsibilities under this agreement, <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of management firm&rsqb;</inline.instr> shall at all times be an independent contractor. Nothing contained in this agreement shall be construed to create an employer&ndash;-employee relationship, a partnership, or joint venture between <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of nonprofit organization&rsqb;</inline.instr> and <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of management firm&rsqb;</inline.instr>.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>6</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Indemnification.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|100|31:96"><form.text><inline.instr>&lsqb;Name of nonprofit organization&rsqb;</inline.instr> shall indemnify, defend, and hold <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of management firm&rsqb;</inline.instr> harmless against all claims, damages, suits, causes of action, judgments, and liabilities (and against all associated costs and expenses, including, without limitation, reasonable attorney&apos;s fees), arising from <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of management firm&rsqb;</inline.instr>&apos;s proper performance of its obligations under this agreement.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>7</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Termination.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|100|31:96"><form.text>This agreement may be terminated at any time by either party without cause, provided that written notice of termination given a specified in this agreement shall be delivered to the other party at least <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of days&rsqb;</inline.instr> days before the intended termination date.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>8</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Employment of &lsqb;name of management firm&rsqb; Personnel.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|100|31:96"><form.text><inline.instr>&lsqb;Name of nonprofit organization&rsqb;</inline.instr> agrees that it will not, during the term of this agreement, and for <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of months&rsqb;</inline.instr> months after termination of this agreement, for any reason hire any person who had at any time during the <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of months&rsqb;</inline.instr>-months preceding the date of intended employment by <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of nonprofit organization&rsqb;</inline.instr> been an employee of <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of management firm&rsqb;</inline.instr> without the prior written approval of <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of management firm&rsqb;</inline.instr>. <inline.instr>&lsqb;Name of nonprofit organization&rsqb;</inline.instr> acknowledges that it is impossible for <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of management firm&rsqb;</inline.instr> to calculate at this time the damages <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of management firm&rsqb;</inline.instr> will suffer in the event of a breach of this paragraph by <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of nonprofit organization&rsqb;</inline.instr>. Accordingly, <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of management firm&rsqb;</inline.instr> and <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of nonprofit organization&rsqb;</inline.instr> agree that if <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of nonprofit organization&rsqb;</inline.instr> breaches this paragraph of the agreement, <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of nonprofit organization&rsqb;</inline.instr> agrees to pay as liquidated damages to <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of management firm&rsqb;</inline.instr> an amount equal to <inline.instr>&lsqb;percentage of annual salary&rsqb;</inline.instr>&percnt; of the annual salary paid by <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of management firm&rsqb;</inline.instr> to the employee or employees of <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of management firm&rsqb;</inline.instr> hired by <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of nonprofit organization&rsqb;</inline.instr> in breach of this agreement during the <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of months&rsqb;</inline.instr> months immediately preceding the date the employee or employees are hired by <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of nonprofit organization&rsqb;</inline.instr>. <inline.instr>&lsqb;Name of nonprofit organization&rsqb;</inline.instr> agrees that such amount is reasonable compensation to <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of management firm&rsqb;</inline.instr> for <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of nonprofit organization&rsqb;</inline.instr>&apos;s breach of this paragraph of the agreement. Such liquidated damages are to be paid to <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of management firm&rsqb;</inline.instr> no later than the date on which the employment of <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of management firm&rsqb;</inline.instr>&apos;s former employee or employees commences with <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of nonprofit organization&rsqb;</inline.instr>.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>9</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Client Files.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|100|31:96"><form.text>All documents and files created by <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of management firm&rsqb;</inline.instr> for <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of nonprofit organization&rsqb;</inline.instr> shall be the property of <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of nonprofit organization&rsqb;</inline.instr>. Upon Termination of <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of management firm&rsqb;</inline.instr>&apos;s services under this agreement, <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of management firm&rsqb;</inline.instr> will return all of <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of nonprofit organization&rsqb;</inline.instr>&apos;s files and documents to <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of nonprofit organization&rsqb;</inline.instr> at a location specified by <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of nonprofit organization&rsqb;</inline.instr>. <inline.instr>&lsqb;Name of management firm&rsqb;</inline.instr> shall not be required to return <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of nonprofit organization&rsqb;</inline.instr>&apos;s files and documents after termination of this agreement until all of <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of nonprofit organization&rsqb;</inline.instr>&apos;s financial obligations to <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of management firm&rsqb;</inline.instr> under this agreement have been satisfied.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>10</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Notices.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|100|31:96"><form.text>Any notice required to be given under this agreement by either party to the other shall be sufficient if addressed and mailed, certified mail, postage prepaid, to the President of <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of nonprofit organization&rsqb;</inline.instr> at his or her business address with copies to the members of the executive committee of <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of nonprofit organization&rsqb;</inline.instr>. Any notice required to be given under this agreement to <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of management firm&rsqb;</inline.instr> shall be sufficient if mailed by certified mail, postage prepaid, to <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of authorized person&rsqb;</inline.instr> and <inline.instr>&lsqb;address of authorized person&rsqb;</inline.instr>, <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of city&rsqb;</inline.instr>, <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of county&rsqb;</inline.instr>, <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of state&rsqb;</inline.instr>.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>11</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Applicable Law.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|100|31:96"><form.text>This agreement shall be governed by and construed in accord with the laws of the State of New York as if entered into and to be put fully performed in the State of New York.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>12</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Entire Agreement.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|100|31:96"><form.text>This agreement sets forth the entire agreement and understanding between the parties on the subject matter of disagreement and supersedes all prior discussions and negotiations between the parties. Neither party shall be bound by any conditions, definitions, representations, or warranties with respect to subject matter of this agreement other than those as expressly provided herein.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>13</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Amendment and Waiver.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|100|31:96"><form.text>No modification of this agreement shall be binding unless made in writing and executed by both parties. No waiver by either party of any breach or obligation of the other party under this agreement shall constitute a waiver of any other prior or subsequent breach or obligation.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>14</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Severability.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|100|31:96"><form.text>If any provision of this agreement is held by a court of competent jurisdiction to be contrary to law, the remaining provisions in this agreement shall remain in full force and effect.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>15</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Arbitration.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|100|31:96"><form.text>Any differences, controversies, or claims arising out of, or relating to this agreement or the breach thereof, shall be settled by arbitration in accordance with the Commercial Arbitration Rules of the American Arbitration Association. The determination of the arbitrators will be accepted and binding upon both parties and a judgment upon the award of the arbitrators may be entered in any court having jurisdiction thereof. <inline.instr>&lsqb;Name of nonprofit organization&rsqb;</inline.instr> and <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of management firm&rsqb;</inline.instr> shall each select one arbitrator, which two arbitrators shall issue a final, binding decision. The parties shall share equally the costs of such arbitration.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|100|31:96"><form.text>In witness whereof, the parties have executed this agreement by their duly authorized representatives as of the date first written above.</form.text></form.para>

<form.line align="l" lineover="y"><inline.instr>&lsqb;Name of nonprofit organization&rsqb;</inline.instr></form.line>
<form.vertical.space amt="1"/>

<section.body>
<form uuid="Ic7122ea0181b11e68c12afa7f3a24041">
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|101|31:97"><form.text>This is an agreement between <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of management firm&rsqb;</inline.instr>, a corporation chartered in New York, to provide management and administrative services to <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of nonprofit organization&rsqb;</inline.instr>, a nonprofit <inline.instr>&lsqb;association/corporation/&lsqb;specification of entity&rsqb;&rsqb;</inline.instr>.</form.text></form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.item><head><name.block><designator>1</designator><name>SERVICES</name></name.block></head>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>A</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Routine Services.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|101|31:97"><form.text><inline.instr>&lsqb;Name of management firm&rsqb;</inline.instr> shall provide to <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of nonprofit organization&rsqb;</inline.instr> the management and administrative services outlined in Attachment A for the duration of this agreement and any extensions thereof.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>B</designator></name.block><form.para><form.text>Special Project Services.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|101|31:97"><form.text><inline.instr>&lsqb;Name of management firm&rsqb;</inline.instr> may provide management and administrative services to <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of nonprofit organization&rsqb;</inline.instr> for special projects that are not otherwise included within the scope of this agreement if <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of nonprofit organization&rsqb;</inline.instr> obtains preauthorization and approval for the provision of such special project services from <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of management firm&rsqb;</inline.instr>.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><designator>2</designator><name>SCOPE OF SERVICES</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|101|31:97"><form.text>The scope of the services to be provided by <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of management firm&rsqb;</inline.instr> is outlined in Attachment A which is incorporated herein by reference.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><designator>3</designator><name>REMUNERATION AND REIMBURSEMENT</name></name.block></head>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|101|31:97"><form.text><inline.instr>&lsqb;Name of nonprofit organization&rsqb;</inline.instr> shall pay to <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of management firm&rsqb;</inline.instr> the sum of &dollar;<inline.instr>&lsqb;dollar amount of monthly compensation&rsqb;</inline.instr> a month in compensation for routine services performed or to be performed by <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of management firm&rsqb;</inline.instr>. This compensation shall be payable <inline.instr>&lsqb;specification of terms of payment&rsqb;</inline.instr>.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|101|31:97"><form.text><inline.instr>&lsqb;Name of nonprofit organization&rsqb;</inline.instr> shall pay to <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of management firm&rsqb;</inline.instr> for special project services performed or to be performed in accordance with the agreement reached by the parties for the performance of such special project services.</form.text></form.para>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|101|31:97"><form.text><inline.instr>&lsqb;Name of management firm&rsqb;</inline.instr> shall be promptly reimbursed for all expenses incurred by it in behalf of <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of nonprofit organization&rsqb;</inline.instr>.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><designator>4</designator><name>PERSONNEL</name></name.block></head>
<form.unit>
<form.item><name.block><designator>A</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|101|31:97"><form.text><inline.instr>&lsqb;Name of management firm&rsqb;</inline.instr> will assign such support staff as it deems necessary to manage the day-to-day activities of <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of nonprofit organization&rsqb;</inline.instr>. All personnel assigned to provide services to <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of nonprofit organization&rsqb;</inline.instr> will be employed by <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of management firm&rsqb;</inline.instr> and <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of management firm&rsqb;</inline.instr> assumes responsibility for their compensation and terms of employment. Employees of <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of management firm&rsqb;</inline.instr> are not considered employees of <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of nonprofit organization&rsqb;</inline.instr> within purview of Social Security accounts, workers&apos; compensation laws, or in any other regard. All employees are bonded and will be bonded during the entire term of this contract and any extension thereof.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
<form.item><name.block><designator>B</designator></name.block><form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|101|31:97"><form.text><inline.instr>&lsqb;Name of nonprofit organization&rsqb;</inline.instr> agrees that it will not during the term of this agreement or for <inline.instr>&lsqb;number of months&rsqb;</inline.instr> months thereafter hire any executive or administrative personnel currently employed by <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of management firm&rsqb;</inline.instr> without the express written approval of <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of officer of management firm&rsqb;</inline.instr>.</form.text></form.para></form.item>
</form.unit></form.item>
<form.item><head><name.block><designator>5</designator><name>OFFICE LOCATION AND HOURS</name></name.block></head>

<section.body>
<form uuid="Ic71255b0181b11e68c12afa7f3a24041">
<form.name.block><name>Independent Contractor</name></form.name.block>
<form.para ct.id="f477b8b0b92511efa86bc22ba615bad8|102|31:98"><form.text>The relationship of <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of service provider&rsqb;</inline.instr> to <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of charitable organization&rsqb;</inline.instr> will be that of independent contractors and nothing set forth in the agreement will be deemed or construed to render the parties as joint venturers, partners or employer and employee. <inline.instr>&lsqb;Name of service provider&rsqb;</inline.instr> personnel are neither employees nor agents of <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of charitable organization&rsqb;</inline.instr> and are not eligible to participate in any employment benefit plans or other conditions of employment available to <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of charitable organization&rsqb;</inline.instr>&apos;s employees. <inline.instr>&lsqb;Name of service provider&rsqb;</inline.instr> will be solely responsible for making or causing to be made all deductions and withholdings from its personnel&apos;s salaries and other compensation if personnel provide services to <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of charitable organization&rsqb;</inline.instr>. <inline.instr>&lsqb;Name of service provider&rsqb;</inline.instr> will have exclusive control over its personnel and over the labor and employee relations, and the policies relating to wages, hours, working conditions or other conditions of its personnel. <inline.instr>&lsqb;Name of service provider&rsqb;</inline.instr> will have the exclusive right to hire, transfer, suspend, lay off, recall, promote, assign, discipline, discharge and adjust grievances with its personnel. At any time, however, <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of charitable organization&rsqb;</inline.instr> will have the right to require <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of service provider&rsqb;</inline.instr> to remove from any <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of charitable organization&rsqb;</inline.instr> project, initiative, fund raiser or event, any personnel objectionable to <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of charitable organization&rsqb;</inline.instr> for any lawful reason.</form.text></form.para>
